### [1] [Plummer Dark Matter Black Hole with Topological Defects: Shadow, Greybody Factors, Quasinormal Modes, and Thermodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01255)
*Ahmad Al-Badawi,Faizuddin Ahmed,İzzet Sakallı*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We construct a black hole solution in a cored Plummer dark matter halo with a cloud of strings, modifying the lapse function by introducing the string tension $\alpha$. The resulting geometry features a single event horizon for $\alpha < 1$ and exhibits observable effects in photon sphere, shadow, deflection angle, ISCO, perturbations, and thermodynamics. All analyses consistently show that the string-cloud parameter $\alpha$ dominates modifications, while the Plummer density $\rho_0$ contributes subdominant corrections.

我们构建了一个嵌入于核化Plummer暗物质晕和Letelier弦云中的静态球对称黑洞解。通过在拉普函数中引入弦张力参数$\alpha$，得到新的度规。当$\alpha < 1$时存在单一视界，否则为裸奇点。六类观测量分析一致表明：弦云参数$\alpha$主导修正，Plummer密度$\rho_0$提供次主导加性修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To investigate how realistic dark matter distributions—specifically a cored Plummer halo—and exotic topological defects (string clouds) affect black hole spacetime structure and observational signatures. By combining these two components, we aim to extend idealized vacuum black hole models to more astrophysically plausible environments and quantify the distinct imprints of each component on key observables such as shadows, deflection angles, stability orbits, and thermodynamic behavior.

旨在研究真实暗物质分布（特别是核化Plummer晕）以及拓扑缺陷（弦云）如何影响黑洞时空结构与可观测效应。结合这两者可将理想真空黑洞模型推广至更接近天体物理实际的环境，并量化各成分对阴影、偏转角、稳定轨道和热力学等关键观测量的独特印记。

Method: We start from the Plummer-Schwarzschild metric and include the Letelier string-cloud contribution via the tension parameter $\alpha$ in the lapse function: $A(r) = h_{\\rm Plummer}(r) - \alpha$. We analyze the spacetime structure (event horizon, naked singularity conditions), compute the photon sphere radius and black hole shadow using null geodesics, apply the Gauss-Bonnet theorem to derive the weak deflection angle, determine the ISCO from timelike circular orbit stability, study scalar perturbations via the effective potential, obtain greybody factor bounds using the Boonserm-Visser method, calculate Hawking radiation spectra, compute quasinormal modes with the 6th-order WKB approximation, and perform full thermodynamic analysis (Hawking temperature, entropy, heat capacity, Gibbs free energy).

从Plummer-Schwarzschild度规出发，在拉普函数中加入Letelier弦云贡献项$A(r) = h_{\\rm Plummer}(r) - \alpha$。通过类光测地线计算光子球与黑洞阴影半径，利用Gauss-Bonnet定理推导弱偏转角；由类时圆轨道稳定性确定ISCO；通过有效势研究标量扰动，使用Boonserm-Visser方法获取灰体因子界限，采用6阶WKB近似计算准正规模频率，并进行完整热力学分析（Hawking温度、熵、热容、Gibbs自由能）。

Result: The spacetime admits a single non-degenerate event horizon when $\alpha < 1$, and transitions to a naked singularity for $\alpha \geq 1$. The photon sphere and shadow radii increase with $\alpha$, while the weak deflection angle decreases. The ISCO radius increases with $\alpha$, indicating reduced orbital stability. Scalar perturbations reveal an effective potential barrier; greybody factors are bounded using the Boonserm-Visser method, showing enhanced low-energy transmission for larger $\alpha$. Quasinormal mode frequencies exhibit decreasing oscillation frequency and damping rate with increasing $\alpha$. Thermodynamically, the Hawking temperature increases with $\alpha$, but the heat capacity remains strictly negative for all parameters, ruling out any Davies-type phase transition. In all cases, $\alpha$ controls leading-order changes, while $\rho_0$ contributes additive subdominant corrections.

当$\alpha < 1$时存在唯一非退化事件视界，$\alpha \geq 1$时为裸奇点。光子球与阴影半径随$\alpha$增大而增加，弱偏转角则减小。ISCO半径随$\alpha$增大而上升，表明轨道稳定性降低。标量扰动显示有效势垒结构；灰体因子界限表明大$\alpha$下低能透射增强。准正规模频率显示振荡频率与衰减率均随$\alpha$增大而减小。热力学上，Hawking温度随$\alpha$升高，但热容始终为负，排除任何Davies型相变。所有情况下，$\alpha$主导修正，$\rho_0$仅提供次主导加性贡献。

Conclusion: The string-cloud tension $\alpha$ is the dominant parameter shaping the physical properties of the black hole system, governing the structure of horizons, null and timelike geodesics, perturbation dynamics, and thermodynamics. The Plummer dark matter halo density $\rho_0$ plays a secondary role, contributing only additive corrections. No phase transitions occur due to the universally negative heat capacity. This work provides a consistent framework for studying black holes in composite astrophysical environments combining dark matter halos and topological defects.

弦云张力参数$\alpha$是主导黑洞系统各类物理性质的关键参数，控制视界结构、类光/类时测地线、扰动动力学与热力学行为。Plummer暗物质晕密度$\rho_0$仅起次要作用，提供加性修正。由于热容恒为负，不存在任何相变。本工作为研究复合天体环境中（暗物质晕+拓扑缺陷）的黑洞提供了自洽框架。

Abstract: We construct a static, spherically symmetric black hole (BH) solution embedded in a cored Plummer dark matter (DM) halo and a Letelier cloud of strings (CoS). Starting from the Plummer-Schwarzschild metric of Senjaya et al.~\cite{Senjaya2026}, we incorporate the string-cloud tension parameter $α$ into the lapse function, obtaining $A(r) = h_{\rm Plummer}(r) - α$. The resulting spacetime admits a single, non-degenerate event horizon (EH) for $α< 1$ and a naked singularity for $α\ge 1$. We determine the photon sphere (PS) and BH shadow radii, compute the weak deflection angle via the Gauss-Bonnet theorem (GBT), and analyze the innermost stable circular orbit (ISCO). Scalar perturbations are studied through the effective potential, greybody factor (GF) bounds obtained from the Boonserm-Visser method, the Hawking emission spectrum, and quasinormal mode (QNM) frequencies computed with the WKB approximation. The thermodynamic analysis covers the Hawking temperature, Bekenstein-Hawking entropy, heat capacity, and Gibbs free energy; the heat capacity is found to be strictly negative for all parameter values, confirming the absence of any Davies-type phase transition. A consistent hierarchy emerges across all six analyses: the CoS tension $α$ governs the leading-order modifications to every observable, while the Plummer halo density $ρ_0$ provides a subdominant, additive correction.

</details>


### [2] [A framework for creating galaxy models in the geometry of the conservation group with dark matter halos and flat rotation curves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01270)
*Edward Lee Green*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: Pandres' extended geometric theory of spacetime with a conservation group larger than diffeomorphisms introduces a curvature vector-based Lagrangian, yielding spherically symmetric solutions and enabling a three-region galaxy model (bulge, mesosphere, outer) that reproduces flat rotation curves via an isothermal dark matter-dominated mesosphere and satisfies the radial acceleration relation.

Pandres提出的扩展时空几何理论通过比微分同胚更大的守恒群引入基于曲率矢量的拉格朗日量，得到球对称解，并构建了包含核球、中层和外区的三区星系模型；其中等温暗物质主导的中层可复现平坦旋转曲线，并满足径向加速度关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To extend general relativity by enlarging the covariance group beyond diffeomorphisms and to develop a geometric framework that can naturally accommodate both gravitational dynamics and galactic rotation curves without relying solely on dark matter particle models.

旨在通过将协变群扩展至超越微分同胚的范围来推广广义相对论，并建立一种几何框架，使其能自然地同时描述引力动力学与星系旋转曲线，而不完全依赖于暗物质粒子模型。

Method: The theory uses a field of orthonormal tetrads and a conservation group extending diffeomorphisms. The Lagrangian density is constructed from a curvature vector; a source term is added for massive objects. Spherically symmetric solutions are derived for both free and sourced fields. Galaxies are modeled in three regions: a baryonic bulge with central cusp, a dark matter-dominated mesosphere under an isothermal condition, and an outer region modeled from prior results. These are combined into a continuous global solution and tested against the radial acceleration relation (RAR).

该理论采用正交四标架场及扩展自微分同胚的守恒群；拉格朗日密度由曲率矢量构建，并为大质量物体添加源项。求解自由场与有源场的球对称解。星系被划分为三个区域建模：具有中心尖峰的重子核球、满足等温条件的暗物质主导中层、以及基于已有结果的外区。三者组合成连续全局解，并通过径向加速度关系（RAR）进行检验。

Result: Gravitational waves propagate at the speed of light in the weak-field limit. Spherically symmetric solutions exist, but the free-field equations imply non-zero stress-energy tensors, necessitating a source term for physical consistency. A three-region galaxy model is constructed: the isothermal mesosphere yields flat rotation curves with one free parameter. The full model satisfies the observed radial acceleration relation in rotationally supported galaxies.

在弱场近似下，引力波以光速传播。存在球对称解，但自由场方程意味着非零的应力-能量张量，因此必须引入源项以保证物理一致性。构建了一个三区星系模型：等温中层可产生具单一自由参数的平坦旋转曲线。完整模型符合观测到的旋涡星系径向加速度关系（RAR）。

Conclusion: An enlarged covariance group leads to a consistent extension of spacetime geometry, provided a source term is included. The resulting framework successfully models galactic dynamics, particularly flat rotation curves and the radial acceleration relation, using a geometric approach with physically motivated assumptions about matter distribution and symmetry.

只要包含源项，扩大的协变群可导致时空几何的一致性扩展。该框架通过关于物质分布与对称性的物理合理假设，成功地用几何方法建模星系动力学，特别是平坦旋转曲线与径向加速度关系。

Abstract: Pandres has developed a theory which extends the geometrical structure of a real four-dimensional space-time via a field of orthonormal tetrads with an enlarged covariance group. This new group, called the conservation group, contains the group of diffeomorphisms as a proper subgroup. The free-field Lagrangian density involves only the curvature vector which is a vector which measures curvature. When massive objects are present a source term is added to this Lagrangian density. The weak-field approximation implies that gravitational waves travel at the speed of light. Spherically symmetric solutions for both the free field and the field with sources are found. In the free-field case, the field equations require nonzero stress-energy tensors. However, we find that for our model to be an acceptable model, we must have a source term in the Lagrangian. In our framework, we divide up the galaxy into three spherically symmetric regions: a baryonic matter-dominated central bulge, a dark matter-dominated mesosphere and an outside region where neither type dominates. Assuming the density of baryonic matter has a central cusp, we show how to model the bulge. Via an isothermal condition we find a model for the mesosphere and show this model implies flat rotation curves with one free parameter. The outside region is readily modeled via previously published results. The models for the bulge, mesosphere and outside region are combined into one continuous model. Using the radial acceleration relation we then show how a galaxy model may be set up for a rotationally supported galaxy.

</details>


### [3] [Corrected Hawking Temperature and Final State of Black Hole Evaporation Under GEVAG Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01286)
*Yen Chin Ong*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: In the GEVAG framework, extending the effective gravitational constant $G_\text{eff}$ beyond the horizon implies a modified Hawking temperature with two terms: one matching GUP-derived results and a second ensuring zero temperature at minimum mass, resolving GUP's remnant inconsistency. General formulas for thermodynamic energy and the Bekenstein bound are derived for entropy corrections, linking the bound to renormalization group scaling of the entropy functional $f(A)$.

在GEVAG框架中，将有效引力常数$G_\text{eff}$推广到视界附近区域意味着霍金温度包含两项：第一项与广义不确定原理（GUP）导出的结果一致，第二项确保黑洞在最小质量时温度趋于零，解决了GUP预测中残余物温度非零的不一致性。本文还推导了任意熵修正下的热力学能量和贝肯斯坦界的通用公式，并指出（广义）贝肯斯坦界可解释为熵泛函$f(A)$的重整化群标度维数及相关理论自然性的一种表述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The generalized uncertainty principle (GUP) predicts a nonzero temperature for black hole remnants, leading to an inconsistency as a stable remnant should have zero temperature. This motivates a refinement of black hole thermodynamics within quantum gravity-corrected entropy models, particularly in frameworks like GEVAG where entropy modifications imply a varying $G_\text{eff}$. The goal is to resolve this inconsistency and generalize thermodynamic relations for corrected entropy laws.

广义不确定原理（GUP）预测黑洞残余物具有非零温度，这导致不一致性，因为稳定的残余物应具有零温度。这促使人们在量子引力修正的熵模型（如GEVAG框架）中改进黑洞热力学，其中熵修正意味着变化的$G_\text{eff}$。目标是解决这一不一致性，并为修正的熵定律推广热力学关系。

Method: The GEVAG framework is employed, in which corrections to horizon entropy induce a position-dependent effective gravitational constant $G_\text{eff}(A)$, where $A$ is the horizon area. By assuming $G_\text{eff}$ remains valid off-shell in the vicinity of the horizon, the first law of black hole thermodynamics is used to derive a modified expression for Hawking temperature. Applying this to logarithmic entropy corrections, the resulting temperature is compared with GUP-based results. General expressions for thermodynamic energy and the Bekenstein bound are derived using thermodynamic identities and scaling arguments, connecting the latter to the renormalization group behavior of the entropy functional $f(A)$.

采用GEVAG框架，其中视界熵的修正导致依赖于视界面积$A$的有效引力常数$G_\text{eff}(A)$。通过假设$G_\text{eff}$在视界邻域内的离壳情形仍成立，利用黑洞热力学第一定律推导修正的霍金温度表达式。将该方法应用于对数型熵修正，并将结果与基于GUP的温度进行比较。使用热力学恒等式和标度论证，推导热力学能量和贝肯斯坦界的普遍表达式，并将后者与熵泛函$f(A)$的重整化群行为联系起来。

Result: For logarithmically corrected entropy, the derived Hawking temperature contains two terms: the first matches the GUP prediction, while the second — arising from $\partial G_\text{eff}/\partial A$ — ensures the temperature vanishes as the black hole approaches minimum mass, eliminating the problematic nonzero-temperature remnant. General formulas are obtained for thermodynamic energy $E = \int \frac{dA}{4G_\text{eff}(A)}$ and the Bekenstein bound $S \leq \pi M R$, extended to any entropy correction via $G_\text{eff}(A)$. The Bekenstein bound is interpreted as reflecting the renormalization group scaling dimension of the entropy functional $f(A)$, suggesting a naturalness condition for viable quantum gravity theories.

对于对数修正的熵，所导出的霍金温度包含两项：第一项与GUP预测一致，第二项源于$\partial G_\text{eff}/\partial A$，确保黑洞趋近最小质量时温度归零，消除了GUP中非零温残余物的问题。得到了热力学能量$E = \int \frac{dA}{4G_\text{eff}(A)}$和贝肯斯坦界$S \leq \pi M R$的通用公式，可通过$G_\text{eff}(A)$推广至任意熵修正。贝肯斯坦界被解释为反映熵泛函$f(A)$的重整化群标度维数，暗示了可行量子引力理论的自然性条件。

Conclusion: By extending $G_\text{eff}(A)$ off-shell near the horizon within the GEVAG framework, a consistent black hole thermodynamics is achieved: the modified Hawking temperature resolves the GUP remnant problem by approaching zero at minimum mass. The approach yields general thermodynamic relations and reinterprets the Bekenstein bound in terms of renormalization group scaling, providing a deeper theoretical foundation for entropy corrections in quantum gravity.

通过在GEVAG框架内将近视界区域的$G_\text{eff}(A)$推广到离壳情形，实现了自洽的黑洞热力学：修正的霍金温度在最小质量处趋于零，解决了GUP残余物问题。该方法给出了普适的热力学关系，并从重整化群标度角度重新诠释贝肯斯坦界，为量子引力中的熵修正提供了更深层的理论基础。

Abstract: In the GEVAG (Generalized Entropy Varying-G) framework, any generalization to horizon entropy leads to a varying gravitational "constant" $G_\text{eff}$ that is a function the horizon area. In this work, it is shown that if we promote $G_\text{eff}$ to be valid in the neighborhood of the horizon, then Hawking temperature consists of two terms, the second of which is related to the variation of $G_\text{eff}$. When applied to the logarithmic correction of the entropy, as is common across various quantum gravity approaches, the first term in the Schwarzschild black hole temperature exactly agrees with that obtained from utilizing generalized uncertainty principle (GUP), while the second term improves on the GUP result by driving the Hawking temperature to zero as the black hole approaches a minimum mass. This resolves the inconsistency in the GUP result concerning a nonzero temperature minimum mass remnant. This work also derives simple general formulas for both the thermodynamic energy and the Bekenstein bound for any correction to the area law under the same assumption that $G_\text{eff}$ can be extended off-shell in the horizon neighborhood. The (generalized) Bekenstein bound can be interpreted as a statement regarding the renormalization group scaling dimension of the entropy functional $f(A)$ and the naturalness of the theory.

</details>


### [4] [Asymptotic analysis of the "simulated horizon" segment of the Collins spiral](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01401)
*Stephen L. Adler*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper analyzes the Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff (TOV) equations for a massless fluid in the context of a dynamical gravastar model, which serves as a black hole mimicker without a true event horizon. Instead, it features a simulated horizon where the spacetime geometry mimics a Schwarzschild black hole externally, while internally $g_{00}$ remains positive and exponentially small. By interpreting the TOV equations as a 2D autonomous dynamical system with spiral flow—following Collins—and identifying the simulated horizon with a segment of this spiral—as done by Zöllner and Kämpfer—the authors perform an asymptotic analysis that connects initial conditions at small radii to observable parameters like mass at the large-radius kink corresponding to the simulated horizon.

本文分析了无质量流体的Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff（TOV）方程，将其应用于动力学gravastar模型，该模型作为黑洞模拟器（black hole mimicker），不具有真实的事件视界，而是具有“模拟视界”（simulated horizon）。在模拟视界外部，时空几何类似于Schwarzschild黑洞；而在内部，度规分量$g_{00}$始终为正且呈指数级小。通过将TOV方程视为二维自治动力系统中的螺旋流（沿用Collins的方法），并将模拟视界映射到该螺旋的一段（Zöllner与Kämpfer的工作），作者进行了渐近分析，将小半径端的初始值与大半径处对应于模拟视界的TOV解“拐点”上的可观测参数（如质量）联系起来。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Black hole mimickers such as gravastars are of interest because they offer alternatives to classical black holes that avoid singularities and information loss paradoxes. The concept of a simulated horizon—where external observers see black-hole-like behavior without a true event horizon—is central to these models. However, understanding how microscopic initial conditions relate to macroscopic observables (like total mass) requires detailed analysis of the TOV equations beyond standard static solutions. The motivation is to bridge the gap between the local dynamics near the origin and the emergence of horizon-scale features using dynamical systems methods.

引力星（gravastars）等黑洞模拟器之所以重要，是因为它们提供了避免奇点和信息丢失悖论的经典黑洞替代方案。模拟视界的概念——即外部观测者看到类似黑洞行为但并无真实事件视界——是这类模型的核心。然而，理解微观初始条件如何影响宏观可观测量（如总质量）需要对TOV方程进行超越标准静态解的深入分析。本研究的动机是利用动力系统方法，弥合原点附近的局部动力学与视界尺度特征出现之间的差距。

Method: The authors reformulate the TOV equations for a massless fluid as a two-dimensional autonomous system, exploiting their inherent symmetry and scale invariance. They analyze the phase portrait of this system, focusing on trajectories that exhibit spiral behavior near the origin, as previously identified by Collins. Using matched asymptotic expansions, they connect the small-radius spiral dynamics to the large-radius 'kink' in the solution profile, which marks the location of the simulated horizon. This allows them to express global parameters such as the mimicker's mass in terms of initial data on the spiral segment associated with the simulated horizon, following the mapping proposed by Zöllner and Kämpfer.

作者将无质量流体的TOV方程重新表述为一个二维自治系统，利用其内在的对称性和尺度不变性。他们分析该系统的相图，重点关注在原点附近表现出螺旋行为的轨迹（如Collins先前指出的）。通过匹配渐近展开法（matched asymptotic expansions），将小半径处的螺旋动力学与解曲线在大半径处的“拐点”联系起来，该拐点标志着模拟视界的位置。这使得他们能够将模拟器的质量等全局参数表示为与模拟视界相关的螺旋段上初始数据的函数，遵循Zöllner与Kämpfer提出的映射关系。

Result: The asymptotic analysis yields explicit scaling relations between the initial values of the metric functions at small radii (on the spiral segment) and the total mass and other macroscopic parameters of the black hole mimicker. It shows that the simulated horizon emerges as a sharp transition ('kink') in the TOV profile due to exponential suppression of $g_{00}$, occurring after multiple windings around the origin in the phase plane. The number of spiral windings correlates with the logarithm of the mass, indicating a renormalization-group-like flow in the space of solutions.

渐近分析得出了小半径处度规函数初始值（在螺旋段上）与黑洞模拟器总质量及其他宏观参数之间的显式标度关系。结果表明，模拟视界在TOV剖面中表现为一个急剧转变（“拐点”），这是由于$g_{00}$被指数抑制所致，发生在相平面中原点周围的多次缠绕之后。螺旋缠绕次数与质量的对数相关，表明解空间中存在类似重整化群（renormalization-group-like）的流动。

Conclusion: The dynamical systems approach provides a powerful framework for analyzing black hole mimickers described by the TOV equations. The spiral structure in the phase space encodes the hierarchical buildup of spacetime layers leading to the simulated horizon. The connection between small-scale dynamics and large-scale observables via asymptotic matching offers a new way to characterize horizon-scale physics without invoking singularities or event horizons. This supports the viability of gravastar-like models as physically plausible alternatives to classical black holes.

动力系统方法为分析由TOV方程描述的黑洞模拟器提供了一个强有力的框架。相空间中的螺旋结构编码了通向模拟视界的时空层次构建过程。通过渐近匹配将小尺度动力学与大尺度可观测量联系起来，为表征视界尺度物理提供了新途径，而无需引入奇点或事件视界。这支持了gravastar类模型作为经典黑洞的物理上合理替代方案的可行性。

Abstract: The Tolman-Oppenheimer-Volkoff (TOV) equations for a massless fluid take the form of a pair of coupled autonomous first order differential equations, which can be employed in a model for a ``dynamical gravastar'' black hole mimicker. The mimicker has no true horizon, but rather a ``simulated horizon'', outside which the geometry resembles a Schwarzschild black hole, but inside which the $g_{00}$ component of the metric is always positive and becomes exponentially small. Collins has reinterpreted the relevant TOV equations in terms of a two-dimensional flow with a spiral form, and Zöllner and Kämpfer have mapped the simulated horizon to a specific segment of the Collins spiral. We give here results of an asymptotic analysis, relating initial values at the small radius end of this spiral segment to the black hole mimicker mass and other parameters that emerge at the large radius kink in the TOV solution, which corresponds to the simulated horizon.

</details>


### [5] [High-frequency gravitational wave transients from superradiance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01407)
*Henry Su,Lucas Brown,Christopher Ewasiuk,Stefano Profumo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper studies gravitational-wave emissions from ultralight boson clouds around rotating primordial black holes, driven by superradiance, considering both isolated and binary-perturbed systems. Analytic strain formulas are derived for transition and annihilation channels in isolated cases, while binary-induced transitions are modeled via the Landau--Zener formalism. Although signals from binaries have favorable durations, their amplitudes are below current detector sensitivity, requiring significant improvements in instrumentation for detection.

本文研究了由超轻玻色子通过旋转原初黑洞上的超辐射形成的宏观引力原子云所发出的引力波，涵盖孤立系统和受双星扰动的系统。针对孤立情况，推导了跃迁与湮灭通道在时域和频域中的解析应变公式；对于双星系统，采用Landau-Zener形式处理共振激发的能级跃迁并计算瞬态信号。尽管双星驱动信号持续时间适合探测器响应，但其特征应变远低于当前灵敏度，且事件率进一步限制可探测性，需未来高频频段引力波实验提升灵敏度、带宽与响应能力才可能观测到此类信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Ultralight bosons are well-motivated candidates in beyond-Standard-Model physics and can form dense clouds around black holes via superradiance, acting as macroscopic quantum systems emitting gravitational waves. Primordial black holes extend this phenomenology into frequency bands accessible to resonant cavity experiments (e.g., MHz--GHz). A unified analysis of both isolated and binary-perturbed gravitational atoms is needed to assess detectability across different astrophysical environments.

超轻玻色子是超出标准模型物理中具有良好动机的候选粒子，可通过超辐射在黑洞周围形成致密云团，构成宏观量子系统并发射引力波。原初黑洞使这一现象进入谐振腔实验（如MHz至GHz频段）可探测的频率范围。为了评估不同天体物理环境下此类系统的可探测性，亟需对孤立与双星扰动下的引力原子进行统一分析。

Method: For isolated gravitational atoms, analytic expressions for gravitational-wave strain in time and frequency domains are derived for both level transitions and boson annihilation, highlighting their narrow-band nature. For binary systems, the Landau--Zener formalism is applied to model non-adiabatic level transitions induced by orbital perturbations, enabling computation of transient gravitational-wave signals. The characteristic strain, duration, and event rates are computed and compared with detector sensitivities.

针对孤立引力原子，推导了能级跃迁与玻色子湮灭通道在时域和频域中的引力波应变解析表达式，突出其窄带特性。对于双星系统，应用Landau-Zener形式描述轨道扰动引起的非绝热能级跃迁，从而计算瞬态引力波信号。计算了特征应变、信号持续时间和事件率，并与探测器灵敏度进行比较。

Result: Analytic formulas for strain from transition ($h_0^{\rm trans}$) and annihilation ($h_0^{\rm ann}$) are obtained for isolated systems, showing narrow-band spectral features. Binary-driven transitions produce transient signals with durations $\sim 1/f$ matching detector response times, but their characteristic strain $h_c \ll h_{\rm det}$ lies far below current sensitivities. Event rates require sources at unphysically small distances for detectability. Significant improvements in detector sensitivity (by $\sim 10^6$), bandwidth, and response speed are required for observation.

针对孤立系统，得到了跃迁($h_0^{\rm trans}$)和湮灭($h_0^{\rm ann}$)通道的应变解析公式，显示出明显的窄带谱特征。双星驱动的跃迁产生持续时间约$\sim 1/f$、与探测器响应时间匹配的瞬态信号，但其特征应变$h_c \ll h_{\rm det}$远低于当前探测极限。事件率要求源位于非物理的小距离处才能被探测。要实现观测，需要探测器灵敏度（约$\sim 10^6$倍）、带宽和响应速度的显著提升。

Conclusion: Gravitational atoms formed by ultralight bosons around primordial black holes are a theoretically compelling source of high-frequency gravitational waves. While current detectors are insufficient to observe signals from either isolated or binary-perturbed systems, they represent a well-defined target for next-generation resonant-mass and cavity-based experiments aiming at the MHz--GHz band. Improved theoretical modeling combined with advances in quantum measurement techniques may eventually enable detection.

由超轻玻色子在原初黑洞周围形成的引力原子是高频引力波的一个理论上有吸引力的来源。虽然当前探测器不足以观测到来自孤立或双星扰动系统的信号，但它们为下一代面向MHz至GHz频段的共振质量及腔基实验提供了明确的目标。结合更优的理论建模与量子测量技术的进步，未来有望实现对此类信号的探测。

Abstract: Ultralight bosons can form macroscopic gravitational-atom clouds around rotating black holes via superradiance, sourcing quasi-monochromatic gravitational waves through level transitions and annihilation. Primordial black holes provide a natural setting for such systems in a frequency range relevant for resonant-cavity experiments. We present a unified treatment of gravitational-wave emission from both isolated and binary-perturbed gravitational atoms in this regime. For isolated systems, we derive analytic expressions for the time- and frequency-domain strain from transition and annihilation channels, emphasizing their narrow-band structure. For binaries, we model resonantly driven level transitions using the Landau--Zener formalism and compute the resulting transient signals. We find that, while binary-driven transitions generically yield signals with durations compatible with detector response times, their characteristic strain lies well below the sensitivity of current experiments at astrophysically plausible distances, and event rates further suppress detectability by requiring sources at unrealistically small separations. We quantify the improvements in sensitivity, bandwidth, and response needed to render these signals observable, and identify gravitational-atom systems around primordial black holes as a theoretically well-motivated target for future high-frequency gravitational-wave searches.

### [7] [Geometric origin of the cosmological constant from Einstein-Chern-Simons gravity compactified to four dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01536)
*M. Cataldo,S. Lepe,C. Riquelme,P. Salgado*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper proposes a geometric origin for the cosmological constant $\Lambda$ through 4D compactification of 5D Einstein-Chern-Simons gravity, where $\Lambda$ emerges from the compactification radius $r_c$, coupling $l$, and field trace $\tilde{h}$. Two regimes arise: a fine-tuned weak-field regime and a natural strong-field regime with $\Lambda \approx 3/(4r_c^2)$, matching the observed value when $r_c \sim H_0^{-1}$, offering a geometric reformulation of the cosmological constant problem.

本文通过五维爱因斯坦-陈-西蒙斯引力的四维紧致化，提出宇宙学常数$\Lambda$的纯几何起源。$\Lambda$由紧致化半径$r_c$、耦合参数$l$和紧致场$\tilde{h}$决定，而非自由参数。存在两个动力学区域：需精细调节的弱场区，以及自然产生观测值$\Lambda_{\rm obs}$的强场区（$\Lambda \approx 3/(4r_c^2)$），其中$r_c \sim H_0^{-1}$。这将宇宙学常数问题转化为为何$r_c$很大这一几何问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The cosmological constant problem — why the observed $\Lambda$ is so small yet non-zero — remains a major challenge in theoretical physics. Instead of treating $\Lambda$ as an ad hoc parameter or invoking quantum vacuum energy, this work seeks a geometric origin for $\Lambda$ within a higher-dimensional gravitational theory, aiming to explain its value without extreme fine-tuning.

宇宙学常数问题——为何观测到的$\Lambda$极小但非零——仍是理论物理的重大难题。本文不将$\Lambda$视为人为参数或依赖量子真空能，而是寻求在高维引力理论中其几何起源，以避免极端精细调节来解释其数值。

Method: The authors consider five-dimensional Einstein-Chern-Simons gravity, whose action includes both the Einstein-Hilbert term and a Chern-Simons correction governed by a length scale $l$. They perform a dimensional reduction by compactifying the fifth dimension on a circle $S^1$, deriving an effective 4D theory. The trace $\tilde{h}$ of the compactified gauge field $h^a$ and the radius $r_c$ enter dynamically into the 4D field equations, generating an effective cosmological constant. They analyze two asymptotic regimes (weak and strong field) and compute the resulting $\Lambda$, black hole solutions (e.g., Kottler), and cosmological horizon entropy.

作者研究五维爱因斯坦-陈-西蒙斯引力，其作用量包含爱因斯坦-希尔伯特项与由长度尺度$l$控制的陈-西蒙斯修正项。通过对第五维在圆周$S^1$上进行紧致化，导出有效的四维理论。紧致化后的规范场$\tilde{h}$及其半径$r_c$动态地进入四维场方程，生成有效宇宙学常数。分析了弱场与强场两种渐近区域，并计算相应的$\Lambda$、黑洞解（如Kottler）及宇宙视界熵。

Result: The compactification yields an effective 4D theory with field equations equivalent to General Relativity plus a cosmological constant $\Lambda$. In the weak-field regime, $\Lambda \propto l^{2}\tilde{h}/r_{c}^{3}$, requiring fine-tuning to match $\Lambda_{\rm obs}$. In the strong-field regime, algebraic cancellation leads to $\Lambda \approx 3/(4r_{c}^{2})$, independent of $l$ and $\tilde{h}$, which matches $\Lambda_{\rm obs} \approx 10^{-52}\,\text{m}^{-2}$ for $r_c \approx 0.78\,H_0^{-1} \approx 8.2 \times 10^{25}\,\text{m}$. The Bekenstein-Hawking entropy of the cosmological horizon is $S_{\rm cosm} = 4\pi k_B r_c^2 / l_{\rm Pl}^2 \sim 10^{122}\,k_B$, consistent with Gibbons-Hawking and geometrically interpreted via $r_c$.

紧致化得到一个等效于广义相对论加宇宙学常数$\Lambda$的四维理论。在弱场区，$\Lambda \propto l^{2}\tilde{h}/r_{c}^{3}$，需精细调节才能匹配观测值；在强场区，代数相消导致$\Lambda \approx 3/(4r_{c}^{2})$，与$l$和$\tilde{h}$无关，当$r_c \approx 0.78\,H_0^{-1}$时自然重现$\Lambda_{\rm obs}$。宇宙视界的贝肯斯坦-霍金熵为$S_{\rm cosm} = 4\pi k_B r_c^2 / l_{\rm Pl}^2 \sim 10^{122}\,k_B$，与吉本斯-霍金结果一致，并可通过$r_c$几何解释。

Conclusion: The cosmological constant can emerge purely geometrically from 5D Einstein-Chern-Simons gravity upon compactification, without being input by hand. The strong-field regime provides a natural explanation for the observed $\Lambda$ without fine-tuning, linking it directly to the size of the extra dimension $r_c$. This reframes the cosmological constant problem as a question about the large scale of $r_c$, rather than the smallness of $\Lambda$, and is compatible with current gravitational constraints due to the large but hidden extra dimension.

宇宙学常数可从五维爱因斯坦-陈-西蒙斯引力的紧致化中纯几何地产生，无需人为输入。强场区无需精细调节即可自然解释观测到的$\Lambda$，将其直接与额外维度尺度$r_c$关联。这将宇宙学常数问题重构为为何$r_c$很大的问题，而非为何$\Lambda$极小，并由于大而隐藏的额外维度，与现有引力实验约束兼容。

Abstract: We present a model in which the cosmological constant emerges as a purely geometric effect from the four-dimensional compactification of five-dimensional Einstein-Chern-Simons gravity. The compactification of the extra dimension generates an effective cosmological constant $Λ$ depending on the compactification radius $r_c$, the coupling parameter $l$, and the trace $\tilde{h}$ of the compactified field $h^a$, rather than being introduced as a free parameter. The resulting field equations are structurally equivalent to those of General Relativity with a cosmological constant, so all known vacuum solutions -- Schwarzschild--de Sitter, Kerr--de Sitter, and FLRW spacetimes -- remain valid. As a concrete application, we derive the Kottler (Schwarzschild--de Sitter) black hole solution.
  We identify two dynamical regimes. In the weak-field regime, $Λ\propto l^{2}\tilde{h}/r_{c}^{3}$, whose sign is controlled by $l^2\tilde{h}$, requiring fine-tuning to reproduce $Λ_{\text{obs}} \approx 10^{-52}\,\text{m}^{-2}$. In the strong-field regime, dependence on $l$ and $\tilde{h}$ cancels algebraically, yielding $Λ\approx 3/(4r_{c}^{2})$ independently of the Chern-Simons coupling. This regime naturally reproduces $Λ_{\rm obs}$ for $r_{c} \approx 0.78\,H_{0}^{-1} \approx 8.2 \times 10^{25}\,\text{m}$, without fine-tuning. The Bekenstein-Hawking entropy of the cosmological horizon gives $S_{\rm cosm} = 4πk_B r_c^2/l_{\rm Pl}^2 \sim 10^{122}\,k_B$, consistent with the Gibbons-Hawking result and admitting a direct geometric interpretation in terms of $r_c$. This framework geometrically reframes the cosmological constant problem: rather than asking why $Λ$ is small, one asks why $r_c$ is large -- a reformulation compatible with a large extra dimension without violating established gravitational tests.

### [8] [Nonperturbative suppression of beyond-General-Relativity effects in quadratic gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01631)
*Georgios Antoniou,Leonardo Gualtieri,Paolo Pani*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: Quadratic gravity extends general relativity (GR) by adding quadratic curvature terms to the Einstein-Hilbert action, leading to new quasinormal modes in black hole perturbations. This work studies gravitational-wave emission from point particles plunging into a Schwarzschild black hole in quadratic gravity and finds that deviations from GR are exponentially suppressed in the GR limit, providing a nonperturbative confirmation of the equivalence between quadratic gravity and GR as predicted by effective field theory.

二次引力通过在爱因斯坦-希尔伯特作用量中加入二次曲率项来扩展广义相对论（GR），导致黑洞微扰中出现新的准正规模。本文研究了质点落入施瓦西黑洞时在二次引力中的引力波辐射，发现偏离GR的效应在GR极限下呈指数抑制，从而非微扰地证实了二次引力与GR之间由有效场论所预言的等价性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Quadratic gravity is a natural extension of GR motivated by quantum corrections and UV completions of gravity. While it reduces to GR in the low-energy effective field theory (EFTofLSS) framework, its non-perturbative differences—especially in black hole dynamics and gravitational-wave signatures—are not fully understood. The presence of additional quasinormal modes suggests potential observational signatures, motivating the study of whether these lead to detectable deviations from GR in dynamical processes such as particle plunges.

二次引力受量子修正和引力紫外完备性的启发，是GR的自然扩展。尽管它在低能有效场论（EFTofLSS）框架下还原为GR，但其非微扰差异——特别是在黑洞动力学和引力波信号方面——尚未完全理解。额外准正规模的存在暗示了潜在可观测效应，因此激励我们研究这些效应是否会在诸如质点坠入等动力学过程中产生可探测的GR偏离。

Method: The authors analyze the linear response of a Schwarzschild black hole in quadratic gravity to a point particle plunging radially into it. They compute the gravitational-wave energy flux emitted in scalar, vector, and tensor channels using the Teukolsky formalism adapted to quadratic gravity. By taking the limit where quadratic gravity parameters approach zero (the GR limit), they examine how the extra quasinormal modes contribute to the waveform and energy emission, particularly focusing on the suppression behavior of corrections relative to GR predictions.

作者分析了在二次引力中施瓦西黑洞对径向落入质点的线性响应。他们使用适配于二次引力的Teukolsky形式体系，计算标量、矢量和张量通道中的引力波能量通量。通过取二次引力参数趋于零的极限（即GR极限），他们研究了额外准正规模如何影响波形和能量辐射，特别关注相对于GR预测的修正项的抑制行为。

Result: The study reveals that although quadratic gravity introduces new scalar, vector, and tensor quasinormal modes that can be excited during the plunge, the observable deviations in the gravitational-wave energy flux from GR are exponentially suppressed in the GR limit. Specifically, corrections scale as $\sim e^{-1/\epsilon}$ with $\epsilon \to 0$ representing the coupling strength of quadratic terms, making them non-analytic and invisible in perturbative expansions.

研究表明，尽管二次引力在坠落过程中会激发新的标量、矢量和张量准正规模，但在GR极限下，引力波能量通量相对于GR的可观测偏差呈指数抑制。具体而言，修正项按 $\sim e^{-1/\epsilon}$ 缩放，其中 $\epsilon \to 0$ 表示二次项的耦合强度，使得这些修正为非解析项，在微扰展开中不可见。

Conclusion: The exponential suppression of deviations confirms a nonperturbative realization of the equivalence between quadratic gravity and GR in the infrared, consistent with EFTofLSS expectations. Despite the presence of new dynamical degrees of freedom, their physical effects decouple smoothly in the low-energy limit, reinforcing the robustness of GR as an effective description of gravity at large scales.

偏差的指数抑制证实了二次引力与GR在红外区间的等价性的一种非微扰实现，符合EFTofLSS的预期。尽管存在新的动力学自由度，它们在低能极限下的物理效应会平滑解耦，强化了GR作为大尺度引力有效描述的稳健性。

Abstract: Quadratic gravity is a well-motivated extension of general relativity~(GR) wherein the Einstein-Hilbert action is augmented by quadratic curvature terms. This theory is equivalent to GR in an effective-field-theory framework, while the two theories are different at the non-perturbative level. As we have recently shown, black holes in quadratic gravity have a rich linear response, including extra scalar, vector, and tensor quasinormal modes that can be excited in physical processes, even when the stationary solution is the same as in GR. Here, by studying the gravitational-wave emission from point particles plunging into a Schwarzschild black hole in quadratic gravity, we show that observable deviations from GR are exponentially suppressed in the GR limit. This provides a nonperturbative realization of the equivalence between quadratic gravity and GR predicted in the effective-field-theory framework.

### [9] [Gravitational wave polarization modes and the kinematical tensors in general relativity and beyond](https://arxiv.org/abs/2511.10567)
*Cynthia Maldonado,Francisco Nettel,Pedro A. Sánchez*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper investigates the relationships between kinematical tensors (expansion, shear, vorticity) and gravitational wave polarization modes in metric theories of gravity, particularly within the weak-field, slow-motion limit. It identifies specific correspondences between components of the kinematical tensors and tensor, scalar, vector, and longitudinal polarization modes, offering a new theoretical framework for interpreting gravitational wave polarizations.

本文研究了在度规引力理论中运动学张量（膨胀、剪切、涡旋）与引力波偏振模式之间的关系，特别是在弱场和慢速运动极限下。文章明确了运动学张量的各个分量与张量、标量、矢量及纵向偏振模式之间的具体对应关系，为解释引力波偏振提供了新的理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the physical interpretation of gravitational wave polarization modes in general metric theories beyond General Relativity is essential for testing alternative theories of gravity. The authors aim to establish a direct connection between observable effects on test particles (encoded in kinematical tensors) and the polarization content of gravitational waves, thereby providing a more intuitive and geometric understanding of these modes.

理解广义相对论之外的一般度规引力理论中引力波偏振模式的物理诠释对于检验替代理论至关重要。作者旨在建立测试粒子可观测效应（编码于运动学张量中）与引力波偏振内容之间的直接联系，从而提供对这些模式更直观且几何化的理解。

Method: The analysis is based on studying the exact equations of geodesic deviation in metric theories of gravity, which describe the relative motion of freely falling test particles. These equations are then linearized for weak gravitational fields and slowly moving particles. By decomposing the gravitational wave into plane wave solutions within a general second-order Lagrangian framework—including General Relativity—the contributions of different polarization modes (tensor, scalar, vector, longitudinal) are linked to specific components of the expansion, shear, and vorticity tensors.

该方法基于研究度规引力理论中的测地偏差精确方程，描述自由下落测试粒子的相对运动。随后，在弱引力场和慢速粒子条件下对方程进行线性化处理。通过在一般二阶拉格朗日框架（包括广义相对论）内将引力波分解为平面波解，将不同偏振模式（张量、标量、矢量、纵向）的贡献与膨胀、剪切和涡旋张量的特定分量相关联。

Result: The paper establishes the following key correspondences: (1) the transverse components of the shear tensor are related to the transverse tensor polarization mode; (2) the expansion scalar is coupled to both the transverse scalar and longitudinal polarization modes; (3) the longitudinal-transverse components of both the shear and vorticity tensors are associated with the vector polarization mode. These results hold in the linearized, weak-field regime for general second-order metric theories of gravity.

本文建立了以下关键对应关系：(1) 剪切张量的横向分量与横向张量偏振模式相关；(2) 膨胀标量与横向标量和纵向偏振模式均有关联；(3) 剪切和涡旋张量的纵向-横向分量与矢量偏振模式相关联。这些结果适用于一般二阶梯度规引力理论的线性化弱场区域。

Conclusion: The kinematical tensors provide a physically meaningful way to interpret gravitational wave polarization modes through their effects on test particle ensembles. This geometric perspective enhances our understanding of polarization in extended theories of gravity and could inform future observational strategies, especially in distinguishing between different polarization states using detectors sensitive to shear, expansion, or vorticity.

运动学张量通过其对测试粒子集合的影响，为解释引力波偏振模式提供了具有物理意义的方式。这种几何视角增强了我们对扩展引力理论中偏振的理解，并可能指导未来的观测策略，尤其是在利用对剪切、膨胀或涡旋敏感的探测器区分不同偏振态方面。

Abstract: Relations between the kinematical tensors (the expansion, the shear, and the vorticity) and the polarization modes of gravitational waves are studied within the context of metric theories of gravity by considering freely falling test particles. After analyzing exact relations, we consider slowly moving particles under the influence of a weak gravitational field. Linearized plane waves of theories representative of those determined by a general second-order Lagrangian, including General Relativity, are shown to exemplify the following interconnections: between the transverse components of the shear and the transverse tensor polarization mode; between the expansion, and both the transverse scalar and the longitudinal polarization modes; and between the longitudinal-transverse components of both the shear and the vorticity, and the vector polarization mode. These relations, from the theoretical point of view, offer a novel insight into the interpretation of the polarization modes in terms of the kinematical tensors. Additionally, the inclusion of the kinematical tensors in the study of gravitational waves might provide a new outlook on their phenomenology.

### [10] [Radial fall: the gravitational waveform up to the second-and-half Post-Newtonian order](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01699)
*Donato Bini,Giorgio Di Russo*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper applies the Multipolar Post-Minkowskian formalism to a two-body system in radial fall, computing the gravitational waveform up to 2.5 post-Newtonian (PN) order. At this order, radiation-reaction effects emerge, leading to bremsstrahlung-type gravitational radiation. The study computes energy, angular momentum (which vanishes), and linear momentum emissions, and analyzes nonlocal inertial forces in the center-of-mass frame at 4.5PN order due to radiative losses.

本文将多极后闵可夫斯基（Multipolar Post-Minkowskian）形式应用于径向自由下落的双体系统，计算了高达2.5阶后牛顿（post-Newtonian, PN）精度的引力波形。在此阶次，辐射反作用力显现，导致类似制动辐射（bremsstrahlung）的引力辐射。研究计算了能量、角动量（恒为零）和线性动量的辐射，并分析了由辐射损失引起的质心系中非局域惯性力贡献（出现在更高阶4.5PN），为未来更高精度计算奠定基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to understand gravitational wave emission from a radially infalling two-body system beyond the test-mass approximation, using a consistent relativistic framework (Multipolar Post-Minkowskian formalism) combined with post-Newtonian theory. This setup allows for the study of radiation-reaction effects and their observable consequences, such as bremsstrahlung radiation and recoil, which are important for modeling extreme mass-ratio inspirals and unbound orbits.

研究动机在于超越测试质量近似，利用一致的相对论框架（多极后闵可夫斯基形式结合后牛顿理论）理解径向下落双体系统的引力波辐射。该设置可用于研究辐射反作用效应及其可观测后果（如制动辐射和反冲），对极端质量比旋进和无界轨道建模具有重要意义。

Method: The authors employ the Multipolar Post-Minkowskian (MPM) formalism to describe the gravitational field outside the source. Within the post-Newtonian expansion, they solve the equations of motion including radiation reaction at 2.5PN order. They compute the gravitational waveform $h_{ij}$ by matching the exterior MPM solution to the post-Newtonian interior source. Energy, linear momentum, and angular momentum fluxes are derived from the waveform using standard formulas in general relativity. Nonlocal inertial effects in the center-of-mass frame at 4.5PN order are analyzed through the retardation of radiative multipoles.

作者采用多极后闵可夫斯基（Multipolar Post-Minkowskian, MPM）形式描述源外引力场，在后牛顿展开中求解包含2.5PN阶辐射反作用的运动方程。通过将外部MPM解与内部后牛顿源匹配，计算引力波形$h_{ij}$。利用广义相对论中的标准公式从波形导出能量、线性动量和角动量通量。通过辐射多极矩的延迟效应分析4.5PN阶质心系中的非局域惯性效应。

Result: The gravitational waveform is computed to 2.5PN accuracy, showing the onset of radiation-reaction-driven dynamics. The energy flux is nonzero and corresponds to bremsstrahlung radiation during infall. Angular momentum flux vanishes due to spherical symmetry of radial motion. Linear momentum flux is also computed, indicating possible recoil effects. Nonlocal inertial forces in the center-of-mass appear at 4.5PN order due to time-retarded radiative multipoles, affecting future high-precision modeling.

引力波形被计算到2.5PN精度，显示出由辐射反作用驱动的动力学起始。能量通量非零，对应下落过程中的制动辐射。由于径向运动的球对称性，角动量通量恒为零。线性动量通量也被计算，表明可能存在反冲效应。由于时间延迟的辐射多极矩，4.5PN阶出现质心系中的非局域惯性力，影响未来的高精度建模。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that even in radial infall—a seemingly simple system—radiation-reaction effects become significant at 2.5PN order, producing measurable bremsstrahlung-like gravitational waves. The vanishing angular momentum emission confirms symmetry expectations. The identification of 4.5PN-order nonlocal inertial forces highlights the importance of memory and hereditary effects in the center-of-mass evolution, paving the way for higher-order computations in unbound or eccentric systems.

研究表明，即使在径向下落这一看似简单的系统中，辐射反作用效应在2.5PN阶已显著，产生可测量的类制动辐射引力波。角动量辐射的消失符合对称性预期。识别出4.5PN阶的非局域惯性力突显了记忆效应和遗传效应在质心演化中的重要性，为无界或偏心系统的高阶计算铺平道路。

Abstract: We consider an application of the Multipolar Post Minkowskian formalism to the case of a two-body system in radial fall. We compute, within the post-Newtonian approximation, the associated gravitational waveform reaching the 2.5 Post-Newtonian accuracy level. At this level the presence of a radiation-reaction force manifests, modifying the fall with a corresponding bremsstrahlung radiation. We evaluate then all emissions: energy, angular momentum (vanishing identically) and linear momentum. We also evaluate the (nonlocal) inertial forces contributions appearing (at the next PN order, 4.5PN) in the center-of-mass due to the losses paving the way for future more accurate computations.

### [11] [Interior geometry of black holes as a probe of first-order phase transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01818)
*Zi-Qiang Zhao,Zhang-Yu Nie,Shao-Wen Wei,Jing-Fei Zhang,Xin Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper proposes using the near-singularity geometry, specifically the Kasner exponent $p_t$, as a new diagnostic for black hole phase transitions in scalarized AdS black holes. It shows that $p_t$ exhibits qualitatively different behaviors across a first-order phase transition and develops an extremum in the supercritical regime, defining a new 'Kasner crossover line' independent of traditional criteria.

本文提出利用奇点附近的几何结构，特别是Kasner指数$p_t$，作为标量化AdS黑洞相变的新诊断工具。研究表明，$p_t$在一级相变两侧表现出定性不同的行为，在超临界区域则出现极值，定义了一条独立于传统判据的“Kasner交叉线”。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional methods for detecting black hole phase transitions rely on thermodynamic quantities measured at the event horizon or asymptotic boundary. However, these approaches may miss crucial information about the deep interior, particularly near the singularity. The authors aim to explore whether the near-singularity geometry can provide an independent and sharp probe of phase structure, especially for first-order transitions and supercritical crossovers.

传统探测黑洞相变的方法依赖于在事件视界或渐近边界测量的热力学量。然而，这些方法可能忽略了关于内部深处（尤其是奇点附近）的关键信息。作者旨在探索奇点附近的几何是否可以为相结构（特别是一级相变和超临界交叉）提供一种独立且敏锐的探针。

Method: The authors analyze the near-singularity geometry of scalarized AdS black holes by computing the Kasner exponent $p_t$ as a function of temperature. They examine its behavior across a first-order phase transition and in the supercritical region, identifying qualitative changes such as oscillatory vs. smooth evolution and the emergence of extrema. These features are compared with standard diagnostics like the Widom line (thermodynamic) and Frenkel line (dynamic).

作者通过计算Kasner指数$p_t$随温度的变化，分析了标量化AdS黑洞的近奇点几何。他们研究了$p_t$在一阶相变两侧以及超临界区域的行为，识别出振荡与平滑演化之间的定性差异以及极值的出现，并将这些特征与Widom线（热力学）和Frenkel线（动力学）等标准判据进行比较。

Result: For scalarized AdS black holes, the Kasner exponent $p_t$ shows strong oscillations with temperature on one side of the first-order phase transition, indicating chaotic interior dynamics, while it becomes smooth and monotonic on the other side. Near the critical point, both behaviors converge. In the supercritical region, $p_t(T)$ develops a distinct extremum, defining a universal 'Kasner crossover line' that does not coincide with the Widom or Frenkel lines.

对于标量化AdS黑洞，Kasner指数$p_t$在一阶相变的一侧随温度强烈振荡，表明内部动力学混乱；而在另一侧变得平滑且单调。接近临界点时，两种行为趋于一致。在超临界区域，$p_t(T)$出现明显的极值，定义了一条普适的“Kasner交叉线”，该线不与Widom线或Frenkel线重合。

Conclusion: The near-singularity geometry, probed via the Kasner exponent $p_t$, provides a novel and independent diagnostic for black hole phase transitions. A change in macroscopic thermodynamic state fundamentally alters the deep interior spacetime structure, demonstrating that the singularity encodes information about phase structure beyond conventional horizons or asymptotic boundaries.

通过Kasner指数$p_t$探测到的近奇点几何为黑洞相变提供了新颖且独立的诊断手段。宏观热力学状态的变化从根本上改变了时空的深层结构，表明奇点编码了超越传统视界或渐近边界的信息，反映了相结构的存在。

Abstract: Traditional diagnostics of black hole phase transitions rely on thermodynamic quantities defined at the event horizon or asymptotic boundary. Here, we demonstrate that the near-singularity geometry offers a sharp, independent probe of both first-order phase transitions and supercritical crossover. For scalarized AdS black holes exhibiting a first-order phase transition, the Kasner exponent $p_t$, which characterizes the approach to the singularity, undergoes a dramatic transformation. On one side of the transition, $p_t$ oscillates strongly with temperature, reflecting violent interior dynamics. On the other side, it becomes a smooth, monotonically varying function. These two distinct behaviors converge as the critical point is approached. Beyond the critical point, in the supercritical region, $p_t(T)$ develops a distinct extremum, defining a ''Kasner crossover line'' that is entirely independent of traditional thermodynamic (Widom line) or dynamic (Frenkel line) criteria. Our work establishes the black hole singularity as a novel class of diagnostics for phase transitions, revealing that a change in the macroscopic thermodynamic state fundamentally reshapes the deepest interior structure of spacetime.

### [12] [Mitigation of Incoherent Spectral Lines via Adaptive Coherence Analysis for Continuous Gravitational-Wave Searches](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01919)
*Ye Zhou,Karl Wette*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: An unsupervised framework using adaptive network coherence analysis mitigates non-Gaussian spectral artefacts in gravitational-wave data, preserving astrophysical signals while recovering sensitivity in contaminated parameter spaces.

本文提出一种基于自适应网络相干性分析的无监督框架，可有效抑制引力波数据中的非高斯谱伪影，同时保留天体物理信号，恢复此前因谱线森林污染而丧失的探测灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Continuous gravitational-wave searches are hindered by non-Gaussian spectral artefacts that accumulate over long observation times, reducing sensitivity. Traditional vetoing methods discard entire frequency bands, leading to loss of potentially valuable astrophysical signal space.

连续引力波搜寻受到长期观测中累积的非高斯谱伪影的限制，导致灵敏度下降。传统剔除方法会丢弃整个频带，造成潜在天体物理信号空间的损失。

Method: We develop an unsupervised mitigation pipeline based on adaptive network coherence analysis, which identifies and suppresses local spectral artefacts without discarding broad frequency regions. The method is applied to Advanced LIGO O3 data across 1-, 3-, and 5-day integration periods, targeting the 20~Hz to 2000~Hz band. Coherence between Hanford and Livingston detectors is used to distinguish instrumental artefacts from potential astrophysical signals.

我们开发了一种基于自适应网络相干性分析（adaptive network coherence analysis）的无监督抑制管道，能够识别并抑制局部谱伪影而不丢弃宽频区域。该方法应用于Advanced LIGO O3数据，积分时间分别为1、3和5天，目标频段为20~Hz至2000~Hz，利用Hanford与Livingston探测器之间的相干性区分仪器伪影与潜在天体物理信号。

Result: For the 5-day dataset, 89\% and 77\% of spectral lines are mitigated in Hanford and Livingston detectors respectively, with less than 7\% of the total bandwidth modified. The coherent population consistent with astrophysical morphologies is preserved, and the non-Gaussian tail of the noise distribution is effectively suppressed, maintaining statistical integrity of signal candidates.

在5天数据集中，Hanford和Livingston探测器分别抑制了89\%和77\%的谱线，总带宽修改小于7\%。符合天体物理形态的相干信号群得以保留，噪声分布的非高斯尾部被有效抑制，信号候选体的统计完整性得到保持。

Conclusion: The proposed framework significantly improves data quality for continuous gravitational-wave searches by selectively removing spectral artefacts while preserving astrophysical signal content, enabling more sensitive all-sky searches in previously contaminated regions.

所提出的框架通过选择性去除谱伪影同时保留天体物理信号内容，显著提升了连续引力波搜寻的数据质量，使得在先前受污染区域开展更灵敏的全天搜寻成为可能。

Abstract: The sensitivity of continuous gravitational-wave searches is strictly limited by non-Gaussian spectral artefacts that accumulate coherent power over long observation baselines. In this paper, we present an unsupervised mitigation framework based on adaptive network coherence analysis. Unlike traditional veto methods that discard entire frequency bands, our pipeline selectively suppresses local artefacts while preserving global potentially astrophysical signals. We validate the method using Advanced LIGO O3 data, analysing the cleaning performance across integration times of 1, 3, and 5 days. For the 5-day dataset, the pipeline identifies and mitigates 89\% and 77\% of the total spectral lines in the Hanford and Livingston detectors, respectively, while effectively preserving the coherent population consistent with astrophysical morphologies. This is achieved while modifying less than 7\% of the analysis bandwidth spanning 20~Hz to 2000~Hz. Rigorous statistical verification demonstrates that the mitigation effectively suppresses the non-Gaussian tail of the noise distribution while strictly preserving the statistical integrity of coherent signal candidates. By recovering detector sensitivity in parameter spaces previously contaminated by the spectral forest, this framework provides a robust preprocessing strategy for all-sky searches.

### [13] [Is Gravity Always Enough to Yield a Classical Universe?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01283)
*Aurora Ireland*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper re-examines the quantum-to-classical transition of cosmic structure during inflation, challenging the assumption that classicality is always achieved. It emphasizes that beyond slow-roll conditions, non-linear dynamics can preserve quantum features in cosmological observables, and proposes using Wigner function phase-space analysis to detect such signatures.

本文重新审视了暴胀期间宇宙结构从量子到经典的转变，挑战了经典性总能实现的假设。文章强调，在超出慢滚条件下，非线性动力学可能导致量子特征在宇宙可观测量中得以保留，并提出使用维格纳函数相空间分析来探测这些特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: While it is commonly believed that cosmic structures originate from quantum fluctuations but appear classical due to decoherence during inflation, this work questions whether standard mechanisms—such as squeezing and horizon-induced decoherence—are universally sufficient. The authors aim to identify gaps in conventional reasoning, especially beyond the slow-roll approximation, where non-linear dynamics may sustain quantumness.

尽管普遍认为宇宙结构起源于量子涨落，但由于暴胀期间的退相干而表现为经典，但本文质疑标准机制（如压缩和视界诱导退相干）是否普遍充分。作者旨在识别传统推理中的漏洞，特别是在慢滚近似之外，非线性动力学可能维持量子性的区域。

Method: The authors analyze the dynamics of cosmological perturbations beyond slow roll, incorporating non-linear interactions that may prevent full decoherence. They advocate for a phase-space approach using the Wigner function $W(\phi, \pi)$ to quantify quantum coherence and non-classicality, enabling a direct probe of quantum signatures in the statistical properties of cosmic fluctuations.

作者分析了超出慢滚条件下的宇宙扰动动力学，纳入可能阻止完全退相干的非线性相互作用。他们提倡使用维格纳函数$W(\phi, \pi)$的相空间方法来量化量子相干性和非经典性，从而直接探测宇宙涨落统计特性中的量子特征。

Result: The analysis shows that under general conditions—particularly with strong non-linearities and deviations from slow roll—quantum coherence can persist on super-horizon scales. The Wigner function can develop negative values, signaling genuine quantum behavior, which may leave imprints in higher-order correlation functions (e.g., non-Gaussianities).

分析表明，在一般条件下——特别是存在强非线性且偏离慢滚时——量子相干性可能在超视界尺度上持续存在。维格纳函数可能出现负值，标志着真正的量子行为，这可能在高阶关联函数（例如非高斯性）中留下印记。

Conclusion: The quantum-to-classical transition in cosmology is not guaranteed solely by inflationary squeezing and horizon-induced decoherence. Non-linear dynamics beyond slow roll can sustain quantum features, opening the possibility of observing quantum signatures in large-scale structure. The Wigner function provides a robust framework for testing quantum origins observationally.

宇宙学中的量子到经典转变仅靠暴胀压缩和视界诱导退相干并不能保证实现。慢滚之外的非线性动力学可以维持量子特征，从而打开了在大尺度结构中观测量子特征的可能性。维格纳函数为通过观测检验量子起源提供了一个稳健的框架。

Abstract: The origin of cosmic structure is widely regarded as quantum, yet the Universe today appears classical. Standard lore attributes this to a "quantum-to-classical" transition on super-horizon scales during inflation. Gravity plays a central role: super-horizon dynamics squeeze quantum states, while the cosmological horizon enforces a system-environment split, leading to decoherence. But are these mechanisms always sufficient? We revisit this question, identifying assumptions and limitations in conventional arguments. We highlight recent work showing that beyond slow roll, non-linear dynamics of cosmological perturbations can generate non-classical features that may survive in observables. This raises the tantalizing possibility that quantum signatures may persist in cosmic structure. We propose a phase-space analysis based on the Wigner function as a concrete route to identifying and probing such signatures.

### [14] [Case studies with GPBilby of glitch-contaminated transient gravitational waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02018)
*Mattia Emma,Ann-Kristin Malz,Adriana Dias,Gregory Ashton*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: GPBilby is a parameter estimation tool using a time-domain likelihood that jointly models astrophysical signals with physical waveforms and non-Gaussian noise via Gaussian processes; it enables glitch-robust inference and helps disentangle noise artifacts from waveform systematics in gravitational-wave data.

GPBilby是一种采用时域似然函数的参数估计工具，联合使用物理波形建模天体物理信号，并通过高斯过程建模非高斯噪声；它能够实现对散粒噪声具有鲁棒性的推断，并有助于区分引力波数据中的噪声伪影与波形建模系统误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Gravitational-wave detectors often observe transient non-Gaussian noise (glitches) that can bias parameter estimation and lead to incorrect astrophysical interpretations; standard analyses assume Gaussian noise, which may not hold in real data.

引力波探测器常观测到瞬态非高斯噪声（即“散粒噪声”），这些噪声可能使参数估计产生偏差并导致错误的天体物理解释；标准分析通常假设噪声为高斯型，但在实际数据中这一假设可能不成立。

Method: The authors use GPBilby, which employs a time-domain likelihood to jointly model the astrophysical signal using physical waveform models (e.g., IMRPhenomXPHM, NRSur7dq4) and non-Gaussian noise using a Gaussian process; they perform Bayesian parameter estimation on several GW events, comparing results under different waveform models and likelihood assumptions.

作者使用GPBilby，该方法采用时域似然函数，利用物理波形模型（如IMRPhenomXPHM、NRSur7dq4）对天体物理信号建模，并用高斯过程对非高斯噪声建模；他们对多个引力波事件进行贝叶斯参数估计，比较不同波形模型和似然假设下的结果。

Result: For Gaussian noise, GPBilby recovers results consistent with standard Gaussian-likelihood methods; for GW231123, IMRPhenomXPHM shows residual structure causing parameter shifts, while NRSur7dq4 does not, indicating waveform-dependent systematics; the Gaussian process can absorb some coherent waveform mismatches; for GW191109, spin misalignment evidence remains robust despite glitches; for GW230630_070659, previously excluded due to poor data quality, GPBilby finds consistency with a BBH signal and no significant residual power.

在高斯噪声下，GPBilby恢复的结果与标准高斯似然方法一致；对于GW231123，IMRPhenomXPHM显示出导致参数偏移的残差结构，而NRSur7dq4则无此现象，表明存在依赖于波形的系统误差；高斯过程可部分吸收相干波形失配；对于GW191109，尽管两个LIGO探测器均存在散粒噪声，自旋未对齐的证据依然稳健；对于因数据质量差被排除在GWTC-4.0之外的GW230630_070659，GPBilby发现其数据与BBH波形模型一致，且高斯过程未识别出显著残差功率。

Conclusion: GPBilby enables robust parameter inference in the presence of non-Gaussian noise and serves as a diagnostic tool for identifying waveform modelling systematics, demonstrating that flexible noise modelling and waveform accuracy are deeply interconnected in gravitational-wave astronomy.

GPBilby能够在存在非高斯噪声的情况下实现稳健的参数推断，并作为识别波形建模系统误差的诊断工具，表明在引力波天文学中，灵活的噪声建模与波形精度密切相关。

Abstract: In their fourth observing run, the LIGO--Virgo--KAGRA gravitational-wave observatories have found hundreds of new signals, but many are contaminated by non-Gaussian transient noise artefacts known as glitches. Left unaddressed, glitches can bias parameter inference and lead to misleading astrophysical conclusions. We present a series of case studies using GPBilby, a parameter estimation tool that employs a time-domain likelihood jointly modelling the astrophysical signal with a physical waveform and non-Gaussian noise with a Gaussian process. We first show that when the detector noise is Gaussian, GPBilby produces results consistent with those obtained with the standard Gaussian-noise likelihood, and then consider events affected by non-Gaussian features. For GW231123, the highest-mass binary black hole candidate observed to date, analyses using IMRPhenomXPHM reveal coherent residual structure that leads to measurable shifts in inferred source parameters. In contrast, analyses employing NRSur7dq4 show no significant excess residual power and remain consistent across likelihood choices. This demonstrates that waveform systematics and flexible noise modelling are intrinsically coupled, as the Gaussian process terms can partially absorb coherent waveform mismatches. For GW191109, we find that evidence for spin misalignment remains robust despite glitches in both LIGO detectors. For GW230630_070659, excluded from GWTC-4.0 owing to poor data quality, we find the data to be consistent with a BBH waveform model, with no additional residual power identified by the Gaussian process component. Overall, these results highlight how GPBilby can be used to perform glitch-robust inference and as a tool to understand waveform modelling systematics.

### [15] [Asymptotic Symmetries of the Holst Action at Spatial Infinity: Including Supertranslations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02052)
*Sepideh Bakhoda,Hongguang Liu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper studies asymptotic symmetries of General Relativity at spatial infinity using the Holst action in the first-order formalism. It proposes relaxed boundary conditions that preserve the full Bondi-Metzner-Sachs (BMS) group, including non-trivial supertranslations, and resolves logarithmic divergences in the symplectic structure via parity conditions. The Holst term contributes to Lorentz charge variations but leaves supertranslation charges unchanged. Divergences in surface integrals are regularized by adding compensating internal Lorentz transformations, yielding finite, integrable charges. This establishes a consistent BMS algebra at spatial infinity in Ashtekar-Barbero variables, highlighting the role of the Immirzi parameter.

本文在Holst作用量的一阶形式下研究广义相对论在空间无穷远的渐近对称性。通过协变相空间方法，提出了一组允许完整Bondi-Metzner-Sachs（BMS）群（包括非平凡超平移）的松弛边界条件。通过对渐近场施加保持对称性的奇偶性条件，消除了辛结构中的对数发散。详细分析表明，尽管Holst项由于洛伦兹生成元的线性增长而对电荷变分有非平凡贡献，但超平移电荷保持不变。通过为渐近对称生成元附加一个保持背景结构的补偿性内洛伦兹规范变换，成功正则化了霍尔斯特电荷表面上的线性发散，得到了显式有限且可积的电荷。该框架以Ashtekar-Barbero变量一致地导出了空间无穷远处的完整BMS代数，揭示了Immirzi参数在经典与量子引力中的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Standard treatments of asymptotic symmetries in General Relativity often eliminate supertranslations at spatial infinity through restrictive boundary conditions or parity conditions. This work aims to relax such restrictions within the first-order formalism (Holst action) to recover the full BMS group, including physically relevant supertranslations. Additionally, the role of the Immirzi parameter—central in loop quantum gravity—in asymptotic symmetries and conserved charges remains poorly understood; this paper seeks to clarify its classical impact, especially on charge expressions and finiteness.

标准的广义相对论渐近对称性处理通常通过严格的边界条件或奇偶性条件在空间无穷远处消除超平移。本工作旨在一阶形式（Holst作用量）中放宽这些限制，以恢复完整的BMS群，包括物理上重要的超平移。此外，Immirzi参数——在圈量子引力中起核心作用——在渐近对称性和守恒电荷中的作用尚不清楚；本文试图阐明其在经典层面的影响，特别是对电荷表达式和有限性的影响。

Method: The covariant phase space method is employed using the Holst action. Relaxed boundary conditions are imposed on the co-tetrad and Lorentz connection to allow for the full BMS group. Parity conditions preserving symmetries are applied to remove logarithmic divergences in the symplectic structure. Charge variations are computed from the symplectic current, with careful treatment of boundary terms. Linear divergences in the naive Holst charge surface integrals are regularized by introducing a compensating internal Lorentz gauge transformation that preserves the background tetrad structure, ensuring finiteness and integrability of the charges.

采用基于Holst作用量的协变相空间方法。对余标架和洛伦兹联络施加松弛边界条件，以容纳完整的BMS群。引入保持对称性的奇偶性条件以消除辛结构中的对数发散。从辛流计算电荷变分，并仔细处理边界项。通过对渐近对称生成元附加一个保持背景标架结构的补偿性内洛伦兹规范变换，正则化朴素霍尔斯特电荷表面积分中的线性发散，确保电荷的有限性和可积性。

Result: The proposed boundary conditions support the full BMS algebra at spatial infinity, including non-trivial supertranslations. Logarithmic divergences in the symplectic structure are removed via symmetry-preserving parity conditions without eliminating supertranslations. The Holst term induces non-zero contributions to Lorentz boost and rotation charge variations due to linearly growing generators. Naive Holst charge integrals exhibit linear divergences from background tetrad rotations, which are canceled by compensating internal Lorentz transformations. The resulting charges are finite and integrable. Crucially, while Lorentz-related charges are shifted by the Holst term, supertranslation charges remain invariant, indicating that the Immirzi parameter does not affect supertranslation sectors.

所提出的边界条件支持空间无穷远处的完整BMS代数，包括非平凡超平移。通过对称性保持的奇偶性条件消除了辛结构中的对数发散，同时未抑制超平移。由于生成元的线性增长，Holst项对洛伦兹 boosts 和旋转电荷变分产生非零贡献。朴素的Holst电荷积分因背景标架旋转出现线性发散，可通过补偿性内洛伦兹变换抵消。最终电荷是有限且可积的。关键的是，尽管Holst项改变了与洛伦兹相关的电荷，但超平移电荷保持不变，表明Immirzi参数不影响超平移部分。

Conclusion: This work provides a consistent Hamiltonian derivation of the full BMS group at spatial infinity within the first-order formalism of gravity. By appropriately relaxing boundary conditions and using symmetry-preserving regularization, it retains supertranslations and achieves finite, integrable charges. The Holst term, while modifying Lorentz charges, leaves supertranslation charges invariant, demonstrating that the Immirzi parameter has no effect on supertranslation symmetry. This result strengthens the robustness of BMS symmetry in classical gravity and opens new avenues for exploring its role in quantum gravity, particularly in loop quantum gravity where Ashtekar-Barbero variables are fundamental.

本工作在一阶引力形式下为在空间无穷远处完整BMS群提供了自洽的哈密顿推导。通过适当地放松边界条件并使用保持对称性的正则化方法，保留了超平移并对称地获得了有限且可积的电荷。尽管Holst项修改了洛伦兹电荷，但它使超平移电荷保持不变，表明Immirzi参数对超平移对称性无影响。这一结果加强了BMS对称性在经典引力中的稳健性，并为探索其在量子引力（特别是在以Ashtekar-Barbero变量为基础的圈量子引力）中的作用开辟了新途径。

Abstract: We investigate the asymptotic symmetries of General Relativity at spatial infinity within the first-order formalism described by the Holst action. Employing the covariant phase space method, we propose a set of relaxed boundary conditions for the co-tetrad and Lorentz connection that admit the full Bondi-Metzner-Sachs (BMS) group, including non-trivial supertranslations, which are typically eliminated in standard treatments. We demonstrate that the logarithmic divergences appearing in the symplectic structure can be removed by imposing specific, symmetry-preserving parity conditions on the asymptotic fields without suppressing the supertranslation sector. A detailed analysis of the conserved charges reveals that the Holst term contributes non-trivially to the charge variations due to the linear growth of Lorentz generators. We show that the naive surface integrals for the Holst charges exhibit linear divergences arising from the rotation of the background tetrad. These divergences are successfully regularized by supplementing the asymptotic symmetry generator with a compensating internal Lorentz gauge transformation defined to preserve the background structure. The resulting charges are manifestly finite and integrable. Crucially, we prove that while the Holst modification shifts the charges associated with Lorentz boosts and rotations, it leaves the supertranslation charges identically invariant. This framework provides a consistent derivation of the full BMS algebra at spatial infinity in terms of Ashtekar-Barbero variables, offering new insights into the role of the Immirzi parameter in classical and quantum gravity.

</details>


### [16] [Massive scalar field perturbations in noncommutative-geometry-inspired Schwarzschild black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02066)
*Wen-Hao Bian,Zhu-Fang Cui*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This paper investigates quasinormal modes, greybody factors, and absorption cross sections for a noncommutative-geometry-inspired Schwarzschild black hole under massive scalar perturbations using the third-order WKB method. Results show stability (Im($\omega$) < 0), with noncommutative parameter $\theta$ reducing oscillation and damping frequencies, while scalar field mass $\mu$ enhances real frequency but suppresses damping. Greybody factors and absorption cross sections increase with $\theta$ but decrease with $\mu$. Notably, for large $\mu$ and $\ell=1$, extremal black hole QNFs approach classical Schwarzschild values, suggesting cancellation between quantum geometric ($\theta$) and mass ($\mu$) effects.

本文基于非对易几何启发的Schwarzschild黑洞，采用三阶WKB近似方法系统计算了在有质量标量场扰动下的准正规模频率（QNFs）、灰体因子（GFs）和吸收截面（ACS）。结果表明QNFs满足Im($\omega$)<0，确认了黑洞在扰动下的稳定性。此外，增大非对易参数$\theta$会减小频率实部和虚部的绝对值，而增大质量$\mu$则增加实部并减小虚部。灰体因子和吸收截面随$\theta$增大而增大，但随$\mu$增大而减小，显示出这两类参数的相反调控效应。特别值得注意的是，在角量子数$\ell=1$且$\mu$较大时，极端黑洞的QNFs趋近于经典Schwarzschild黑洞的对应值，表明质量和非对易几何量子修正效应在一定程度上相互抵消。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To explore the perturbative dynamics of black holes in the context of noncommutative geometry and massive scalar fields, aiming to understand how quantum-inspired spacetime corrections (via $\theta$) and field mass ($\mu$) influence quasinormal modes, greybody factors, and absorption cross sections—key observables in gravitational wave astronomy and black hole spectroscopy.

旨在探索非对易几何与有质量标量场背景下黑洞的微扰动力学，理解量子启发的时空修正（通过$\theta$）和场质量（$\mu$）如何影响准正规模、灰体因子和吸收截面——这些是引力波天文学和黑洞谱学中的关键可观测量。

Method: The third-order WKB approximation is applied to compute quasinormal mode frequencies of a noncommutative-geometry-inspired Schwarzschild black hole. The Klein-Gordon equation for a massive scalar field is solved in this curved spacetime background. Transmission probabilities (greybody factors) are derived from the asymptotic behavior of wave solutions, and absorption cross sections are calculated accordingly. Calculations are performed across varying values of the noncommutative parameter $\theta$ and scalar field mass $\mu$, focusing on different angular momentum states $\ell$.

采用三阶WKB近似方法计算非对易几何启发的Schwarzschild黑洞的准正规模频率。求解该弯曲时空背景下的Klein-Gordon方程以描述有质量标量场的行为。从波函数的渐进行为导出透射概率（即灰体因子），并据此计算吸收截面。计算覆盖了不同非对易参数$\theta$和标量场质量$\mu$的取值，并聚焦于不同的角动量态$\ell$。

Result: Quasinormal mode frequencies satisfy Im($\omega$) < 0, confirming mode stability. Increasing $\theta$ reduces both Re($\omega$) and |Im($\omega$)|, while increasing $\mu$ increases Re($\omega$) and decreases |Im($\omega$)|. Greybody factors and absorption cross sections increase with $\theta$ but decrease with $\mu$. For extremal black holes at high $\mu$ and $\ell=1$, QNFs approach those of the classical Schwarzschild black hole, indicating partial cancellation between $\theta$-induced quantum corrections and $\mu$-dependent field effects.

准正规模频率满足Im($\omega$) < 0，证实了模式稳定性。增大$\theta$会减小Re($\omega$)和|Im($\omega$)|，而增大$\mu$则增加Re($\omega$)但减小|Im($\omega$)|。灰体因子和吸收截面随$\theta$增大而增大，但随$\mu$增大而减小。对于高$\mu$且$\ell=1$的极端黑洞，其QNFs趋近于经典Schwarzschild黑洞的值，表明由$\theta$引起的量子修正与由$\mu$引起的场效应之间存在部分抵消。

Conclusion: The study demonstrates that noncommutative geometry and scalar field mass have competing influences on black hole perturbation observables. While $\theta$ generally suppresses quasinormal ringing and enhances transmission, $\mu$ prolongs oscillation duration but reduces emission efficiency. The observed convergence of QNFs to classical limits under extreme conditions suggests that quantum gravitational effects may be effectively masked by massive field dynamics in certain regimes, offering insights into the interplay between quantum spacetime structure and matter fields.

本研究表明，非对易几何与标量场质量对黑洞微扰可观测量具有竞争性影响。虽然$\theta$通常抑制准正规环鸣并增强透射，但$\mu$延长振荡持续时间却降低辐射效率。在极端条件下QNFs向经典极限的收敛表明，在某些参数区域，量子引力效应可能被大质量场动力学有效掩盖，这为量子时空结构与物质场之间的相互作用提供了新的见解。

Abstract: In this paper, based on noncommutative-geometry-inspired Schwarzschild black hole, we employ a third-order WKB approximation approach to systematically calculate the quasinormal mode frequencies (QNFs), greybody factors (GFs), and absorption cross section (ACS) under massive scalar field perturbations. The results show that the QNFs satisfy Im($ω$)<0, confirming the stability of the black hole under perturbations. Furthermore, increasing the noncommutative parameter $θ$ reduces the absolute values of both the real and imaginary parts of the frequency, while increasing mass $μ$ increases the real part and reduces the imaginary part. The GFs and ACS increase with increasing $θ$ and decrease with increasing $μ$, indicating opposite modulation effects of these two types of parameters. It is worth emphasizing that the QNFs of the extreme black hole approach the corresponding values of the classical Schwarzschild black hole at angular quantum number $\ell=1$ and large $μ$, suggesting that, the effects of mass and noncommutative geometry quantum corrections cancel each other out to some extent. It is hoped that these results provide a viable theoretical basis for both the theoretical and experimental aspects of the perturbative dynamics of black hole.

### [17] [Emergence of volume-law scaling for entanglement negativity from the Hawking radiation of analogue black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02075)
*S. Mahesh Chandran,Uwe R. Fischer*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We demonstrate that logarithmic negativity in a 1+1D analogue black hole acquires a UV-finite volume term due to Hawking radiation, encoding the density and spatial distribution of entangled Hawking pairs, with implications for unitarity and detectability in cold-atom experiments.

我们证明了在1+1维类比黑洞中，由于霍金辐射导致的非局域关联，对数负性获得了一个紫外有限的体积项，该体积项编码了纠缠霍金对的数密度和空间分布，这对幺正性和冷原子实验中的可探测性具有重要意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the quantum information content of Hawking radiation is crucial for resolving the black hole information paradox and assessing the fate of unitarity during evaporation. Recent progress in cold-atom systems offers a promising platform for simulating quantum fields in curved spacetime analogues, motivating a lattice-based approach to probe entanglement structure beyond continuum approximations.

理解霍金辐射的量子信息内容对于解决黑洞信息悖论以及评估蒸发过程中幺正性的命运至关重要。冷原子系统方面的最新进展为模拟弯曲时空类比中的量子场提供了有前景的平台，这促使我们采用基于晶格的方法来探测超越连续近似下的纠缠结构。

Method: We employ a lattice regularization of a quantum field in a 1+1D analogue black-hole geometry, numerically computing the logarithmic negativity between interior and exterior regions. By coarse-graining over lattice sites, we isolate the scaling behavior of entanglement in the presence of Hawking radiation, distinguishing UV-divergent vacuum contributions from finite, nonlocal correlations induced by particle pair creation.

我们在1+1维类比黑洞几何中对量子场采用晶格正则化方法，数值计算内部与外部区域之间的对数负性。通过对晶格点进行粗粒化处理，我们分离出在霍金辐射存在下纠缠的标度行为，区分了来自真空的紫外发散贡献与由粒子对产生引起的有限非局域关联。

Result: We find that logarithmic negativity, while typically exhibiting a UV-divergent logarithmic scaling in the conformal vacuum, acquires a UV-finite volume term proportional to the number of entangled Hawking pairs. This volume term encodes both the number density and the spatial distribution of these pairs across the horizon, revealing a direct signature of nonlocal quantum correlations generated by the black hole background.

我们发现，尽管对数负性在共形真空中通常表现出紫外发散的对数标度，但它获得了一个与纠缠霍金对数量成正比的紫外有限体积项。该体积项编码了这些对在视界两侧的数密度和空间分布，揭示了由黑洞背景产生的非局域量子关联的直接特征。

Conclusion: The emergence of a volume-law contribution to logarithmic negativity provides a measurable signature of information transfer via Hawking radiation, supporting unitary evolution. This result is detectable in current cold-atom experiments and suggests a deeper connection between entanglement structure and black-hole thermodynamics beyond the semiclassical regime.

对数负性中体积律项的出现为通过霍金辐射进行信息传递提供了可测量的信号，支持幺正演化。这一结果可在当前冷原子实验中被探测，并暗示了纠缠结构与黑洞热力学之间在半经典区域之外更深层次的联系。

Abstract: The quantum information content of Hawking radiation holds the key to understanding black-hole evaporation and the fate of unitarity. Motivated by recent advances in cold-atom experiments, we develop a lattice-regularization approach aimed at simulating the coarse-grained entanglement scaling of a quantum field in a 1+1D analogue black-hole background. We provide the first concrete demonstration that logarithmic negativity -- an entanglement monotone that typically exhibits a UV-divergent log-scaling for the conformal vacuum -- acquires a UV-finite volume term from the nonlocal correlations seeded by Hawking radiation. We show that this volume term encodes both the number density and spatial distribution of entangled Hawking pairs along the black-hole interior and exterior. We highlight its prospective detection in currently realizable experiments as well as its implications beyond the analogue paradigm, in particular for black-hole thermodynamics.
