### [18] [Boundedness and decay for the conformal wave equation in Schwarzschild-AdS under dissipative boundary conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02084)
*Alex Tullini*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We prove boundedness and polynomial decay of the non-degenerate energy for solutions to the conformal wave equation on 4-dimensional Schwarzschild--Anti de Sitter spacetimes under dissipative boundary conditions, at rate $(1+v)^{-n}$, assuming control over up to $n$-times $T$-commuted energies. This improves upon inverse logarithmic decay under Dirichlet conditions and shows that photon sphere trapping does not obstruct decay under dissipation.

我们证明了在四维Schwarzschild--反德西特时空中，满足耗散边界条件的共形波动方程解的非退化能量具有有界性，并以$(1+v)^{-n}$的任意多项式速率衰减，前提是控制最多$n$次$T$-交换子能量。这一结果优于狄利克雷边界条件下的逆对数衰减，且表明光子球处的陷获不影响在耗散条件下的能量衰减。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the stability and decay properties of linear waves on black hole backgrounds in Anti-de Sitter (AdS)-like geometries is central to the AdS/CFT correspondence and the problem of nonlinear stability. In pure AdS, dissipative boundary conditions can lead to faster energy decay compared to Dirichlet conditions. However, in Schwarzschild--AdS, the presence of a photon sphere introduces additional trapping, which could potentially slow down decay. The motivation is to determine whether dissipative boundary conditions can overcome both the slow Dirichlet-type decay and the obstruction from trapping, thus revealing the interplay between boundary dissipation and local geometry.

理解反德西特（AdS）类几何中黑洞背景下线性波的稳定性与衰减特性，对于AdS/CFT对偶及非线性稳定性问题至关重要。在纯AdS中，耗散边界条件可导致比狄利克雷条件更快的能量衰减。然而，在Schwarzschild--AdS中，光子球的存在引入了额外的陷获效应，可能减缓衰减。本研究旨在探究耗散边界条件是否能同时克服狄利克雷型慢衰减和几何陷获的阻碍，揭示边界耗散与局部几何之间的相互作用。

Method: The analysis is based on constructing suitable energy identities using the vector field method. A red-shifted multiplier near the event horizon captures the local redshift effect, while a globally defined $T$-vector field ($\partial_t$) generates conserved and monotonic energies. Dissipative boundary conditions allow flux control at the timelike boundary at infinity, enabling integrated decay estimates. By commuting the equation with the $T$-vector field up to $n$ times and controlling the corresponding higher-order energies, polynomial decay at rate $(1+v)^{-n}$ is established via a hierarchical bootstrap argument. Crucially, the proof shows that the trapping at the photon sphere does not prevent such decay under these boundary conditions.

该分析基于向量场方法构建适当的能量恒等式。事件视界附近的红移乘子捕捉局部红移效应，而全局定义的$T$-向量场（$\partial_t$）生成守恒且单调的能量。耗散边界条件允许在无限远类时边界上控制通量，从而获得积分衰减估计。通过将方程与$T$-向量场最多交换$n$次并控制相应的高阶能量，利用分层自举论证建立了$(1+v)^{-n}$的多项式衰减。关键的是，证明表明在这些边界条件下，光子球处的陷获并不阻碍此类衰减。

Result: We establish that solutions to the conformal wave equation $\square_g ψ + \frac{2}{l^2} ψ = 0$ on 4-dimensional Schwarzschild--AdS spacetimes exhibit non-degenerate energy boundedness and decay at an arbitrary polynomial rate $(1+v)^{-n}$, provided the initial data has finite $T$-commuted energies up to order $n$. This decay rate holds despite the presence of trapping at the photon sphere. The result contrasts sharply with the inverse logarithmic decay known under Dirichlet boundary conditions and matches the behavior observed in pure AdS under dissipative conditions.

我们证明了在四维Schwarzschild--AdS时空中，共形波动方程$\square_g ψ + \frac{2}{l^2} ψ = 0$的解具有非退化能量的有界性，并以任意多项式速率$(1+v)^{-n}$衰减，前提是初始数据的$T$-交换子能量至多为$n$阶有限。尽管存在光子球处的陷获，该衰减速率依然成立。此结果与狄利克雷边界条件下已知的逆对数衰减形成鲜明对比，并与纯AdS在耗散条件下的行为一致。

Conclusion: Dissipative boundary conditions are sufficient to ensure polynomial decay of energy for the conformal wave equation on Schwarzschild--AdS spacetimes, even in the presence of photon sphere trapping. This demonstrates that boundary dissipation can dominate over geometric obstructions to decay, highlighting a key difference between Dirichlet and dissipative settings in asymptotically AdS geometries. The result supports the expectation that dissipation enhances stability in AdS-like spacetimes.

耗散边界条件足以确保Schwarzschild--AdS时空中共形波动方程的能量以多项式速率衰减，即使存在光子球陷获。这表明边界耗散可以压倒几何对衰减的阻碍，凸显了渐近AdS几何中狄利克雷与耗散设置之间的关键差异。该结果支持了耗散增强AdS类时空稳定性的预期。

Abstract: We study the conformal wave equation $\square_g ψ+ \frac{2}{l^2} ψ= 0$ on 4-dimensional Schwarzschild--Anti de Sitter spacetimes under dissipative boundary conditions. We prove boundedness and decay of the non-degenerate energy of $ψ$ at an arbitrary polynomial rate of $(1+v)^{-n}$ provided that we control the (up to) $n$-times $T$-commuted energy. This contrasts with the inverse logarithmic decay obtained under Dirichlet boundary conditions and is in line with the result obtained in the pure Anti-de Sitter case under dissipative boundary conditions. In particular, the decay is not affected by the additional trapping at the photon sphere.

### [19] [Localized formation of quiescent big bang singularities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02104)
*Andrés Franco-Grisales*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We prove a localized big bang formation result without requiring initial data to be near any background solution. By introducing a new foliation via a time function solving a second-order equation, we synchronize the singularity and obtain a symmetric hyperbolic formulation of Einstein's equations, allowing for curvature blow-up in a neighborhood of a point. The method is matter-model-independent and provides geometric initial data on the singularity.

我们证明了一个局部大爆炸形成结果，且不要求初始数据接近任何背景解。通过引入一种新的时间函数（满足二阶微分方程）定义的叶状结构，我们实现了奇点的同步，并得到了爱因斯坦方程的对称双曲形式，从而在某点邻域内实现曲率发散。该方法不依赖物质模型，并提供了奇点上的几何初始数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Previous big bang formation results often rely on global assumptions or proximity to known solutions (e.g., FLRW). A major goal is to establish singularity formation from generic, localized initial conditions without symmetry or closeness to background spacetimes. This work aims to remove these restrictions and provide a fully localized criterion for big bang formation.

以往的大爆炸形成结果通常依赖于全局假设或接近已知解（如FLRW）。主要目标是从更一般的局部初始条件出发，在无对称性或远离背景时空的情况下建立奇点形成机制。本工作旨在消除这些限制，提供一个完全局部化的大爆炸形成判据。

Method: We introduce a novel foliation of spacetime by spacelike hypersurfaces defined as level sets of a time function $\tau$ satisfying a second-order differential equation. This yields a symmetric hyperbolic system for the Einstein--nonlinear scalar field equations. Using this formulation, we derive sufficient conditions on initial data in a neighborhood of a point $x \in U$ such that the maximal globally hyperbolic development exhibits a local quiescent big bang singularity with curvature blow-up to the past of $x$. The time function allows synchronization of the singularity and is compatible with various matter models.

我们引入了一种新的时空叶状结构，由满足二阶微分方程的时间函数$\tau$的等值面定义。这使得爱因斯坦-非线性标量场方程可写为对称双曲系统。利用此形式，我们在点$x \in U$的邻域内推导出初始数据的充分条件，使得最大全局双曲发展在$x$的过去方向呈现局部寂静型大爆炸奇点并伴随曲率发散。该时间函数实现了奇点同步，并与多种物质模型兼容。

Result: We prove that if the initial data satisfy a specific condition in a sufficiently large neighborhood of a point $x$, then the corresponding solution develops a local quiescent big bang singularity with curvature blow-up to the past of $x$. The new formulation is matter-model-independent and allows us to define geometric initial data on the singularity itself, providing a complete description of asymptotic behavior toward the big bang.

我们证明：若初始数据在某点$x$足够大的邻域内满足特定条件，则对应解将在$x$的过去方向发展出局部寂静型大爆炸奇点，并伴有曲率发散。新形式不依赖物质模型，且允许我们在奇点本身定义几何初始数据，从而完整描述趋向大爆炸的渐近行为。

Conclusion: We have established a localized criterion for big bang formation that does not require proximity to a background solution. The use of a specially constructed time function enables both singularity synchronization and a symmetric hyperbolic formulation, which are crucial for proving local singularity formation. The framework's independence from the matter model and its ability to induce geometric data on the singularity make it a significant advance in the mathematical understanding of cosmological singularities.

我们建立了无需接近背景解的大爆炸形成的局部判据。通过构造特殊的时间函数，实现了奇点同步和对称双曲形式，这对证明局部奇点形成至关重要。该框架不依赖物质模型，并能在奇点上诱导几何数据，标志着对宇宙学奇点数学理解的重要进展。

Abstract: We prove a localized big bang formation result, which does not require proximity of the initial data to any background solution. Suppose that we are given initial data for the Einstein--nonlinear scalar field equations on an open set $U \subset \mathbb{R}^3$. We identify a general condition on the initial data such that if the condition is satisfied in a large enough neighborhood of $x \in U$, then the corresponding maximal globally hyperbolic development has a local quiescent big bang singularity with curvature blow up to the past of $x$. We achieve the localization by introducing a new kind of foliation by spacelike hypersurfaces, given by the level sets of a time function satisfying a certain second order differential equation. This time function allows us to synchronize the singularity while at the same time yielding a symmetric hyperbolic formulation of Einstein's equations. Our new formulation also has two key advantages over previous localized big bang stability results. First, it is independent of the matter model, so it is possible that it could be used to prove big bang formation with matter models different from a scalar field. And second, it allows us to conclude that our solutions induce geometric initial data on the singularity, thus giving a complete description of the asymptotics towards the big bang.

</details>


### [20] [Axial gravitational perturbations and echo-like signals of a hairy black hole from gravitational decoupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02164)
*Yi Yang,Ali Ovgun,Gaetano Lambiase,Dong Liu,Zheng-Wen Long*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: The paper studies axial gravitational perturbations in a hairy black hole within the gravitational decoupling framework, deriving the odd-parity master equation and showing that echo-like signals arise from a dynamically generated double-peak potential, offering a geometric origin for late-time echoes without ad hoc reflectivity.

本文在引力解耦框架下研究了带毛黑洞的轴向引力扰动，推导了奇宇称主方程，并表明回声类信号源于动态形成的双峰势，从而为晚期回声提供了几何起源，而无需人为引入近 horizon 反射性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand the geometric origin of echo-like signals in gravitational waveforms from black hole mergers, particularly whether such signals can emerge naturally from spacetime geometry rather than being imposed by exotic boundary conditions or new physics near the horizon.

旨在理解黑洞并合中引力波形回声信号的几何起源，特别是此类信号是否能自然地从时空几何中产生，而非依赖于视界附近的人为边界条件或新物理。

Method: Derived the odd-parity (axial) master equation for gravitational perturbations in a hairy black hole spacetime constructed via gravitational decoupling. Computed the effective potential and analyzed its structure. Used both frequency-domain (continued fraction, matrix method) and time-domain integration techniques to compute quasinormal modes and late-time waveforms.

推导了通过引力解耦构造的带毛黑洞时空中引力扰动的奇宇称（轴向）主方程，计算了有效势并分析其结构，采用频域方法（连分数法、矩阵法）和时域积分技术计算准正规模和晚期波形。

Result: The effective potential for axial perturbations develops a double-peak structure in certain parameter regimes, forming a trapping cavity that supports long-lived quasinormal modes and generates echo-like late-time signals. These echoes arise purely from the geometry, without requiring artificial near-horizon reflectivity. However, the parameter region allowing echoes does not necessarily satisfy the weak energy condition everywhere outside the horizon.

在特定参数区域内，轴向扰动的有效势呈现双峰结构，形成捕获腔，支持长寿命的准正规模并产生回声类晚期信号。这些回声纯属几何效应，无需人为引入近 horizon 反射性。然而，允许回声出现的参数区域未必在整个视界外区域满足弱能量条件。

Conclusion: Echo-like signals in black hole ringdown can emerge dynamically from the geometry of hairy black holes in gravitational decoupling, providing a novel mechanism for observable deviations from general relativity. This offers a new avenue for probing black hole hair via gravitational-wave observations, although physical viability depends on energy condition considerations.

回声类信号可在引力解耦的带毛黑洞几何中动态产生，为可观测偏离广义相对论提供了新机制。这为通过引力波观测探测黑洞毛提供了新途径，但其物理可行性依赖于对能量条件的考量。

Abstract: We study axial gravitational perturbations of a hairy black hole constructed in the framework of gravitational decoupling and investigate the geometric origin of echo-like late-time signals in this spacetime. We derive the odd-parity master equation and the corresponding effective potential, and we compute the quasinormal-mode spectrum by using frequency-domain and time-domain methods. We show that, in a suitable region of parameter space, the axial potential develops a double-peak structure that supports a trapping cavity and gives rise to echo-like late-time waveforms. Rather than imposing near-horizon reflectivity by hand, the delayed pulses therefore arise dynamically from the geometry of the effective potential. We also clarify that the parameter region exhibiting echoes need not coincide with the region in which the weak energy condition is satisfied everywhere outside the event horizon, and this distinction must be taken into account when interpreting the physical status of the solution. Our results provide a useful framework for probing black-hole hair through gravitational-wave ringdown and for exploring possible observational departures from the standard no-hair paradigm.

</details>


### [21] [Quadratic gravity corrections to scalar QNMs of rapidly rotating black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02214)
*Stef J. B. Husken,Tom van der Steen,Simon Maenaut,Kelvin Ka-Ho Lam,Maxim D. Jockwer,Adrian Ka-Wai Chung,Thomas Hertog,Tjonnie G. F. Li,Nicolás Yunes*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: This study computes leading-order deviations from general relativity in the scalar quasinormal mode spectra of rotating black holes within scalar Gauss-Bonnet and dynamical Chern-Simons gravity, using numerical black-hole solutions valid for large spins. The calculations extend to dimensionless spins up to $a/M = 0.99$ with high precision, revealing that corrections to certain modes increase dramatically for spins above $a/M > 0.9$.

本文在标量高斯-邦特和动力学陈-西蒙斯引力框架下，利用适用于大自旋的数值黑洞解，计算了旋转黑洞标量准正规模谱偏离广义相对论的主导修正。计算覆盖无量纲自旋高达 $a/M = 0.99$ 的情形，精度极高；结果显示当自旋超过 $a/M > 0.9$ 时，某些模式的修正幅度可增加数个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Previous calculations of quasinormal mode corrections in quadratic-curvature, scalar-tensor theories were limited to small or moderate black-hole spins due to reliance on spin expansions. This restricts their applicability to astrophysically relevant, rapidly rotating black holes. The motivation is to extend these predictions to the high-spin regime using numerically constructed, non-perturbative-in-spin black-hole solutions.

以往在二次曲率、标量-张量理论中对准正规模修正的计算受限于自旋展开，仅适用于小或中等自旋黑洞，限制了其在天体物理中常见高速旋转黑洞的应用。本研究旨在利用非微扰自旋的数值黑洞解，将这些预测扩展至高自旋区域。

Method: Using recently developed numerical black-hole solutions that remain valid for large spins (up to $a/M = 0.99$), the authors solve the perturbation equations for scalar quasinormal modes in scalar Gauss-Bonnet and dynamical Chern-Simons gravity. The equations are solved via pseudo-spectral collocation methods, enabling high-precision computation of mode frequencies and their deviations from general relativity.

利用最新构建的适用于大自旋（高达 $a/M = 0.99$）的数值黑洞解，作者求解了标量高斯-邦特和动力学陈-西蒙斯引力中标量准正则模的扰动方程。通过伪谱配置方法求解这些方程，实现了对模式频率及其偏离广义相对论行为的高精度计算。

Result: The leading-order corrections to scalar quasinormal modes are computed with accuracy better than $\lesssim 10^{-3}$ for the $l=m=0$ mode and $\lesssim 10^{-6}$ for higher multipoles. For black-hole spins $a/M > 0.9$, the deviations from general relativity increase by orders of magnitude, particularly for certain modes, highlighting the importance of non-perturbative-in-spin treatments in testing modified gravity.

主导阶的标量准正则模修正被计算得出：对于 $l=m=0$ 模式精度优于 $\lesssim 10^{-3}$，更高多极模式精度达 $\lesssim 10^{-6}$。当黑洞自旋 $a/M > 0.9$ 时，偏离广义相对论的程度可增加数个数量级，尤其针对某些特定模式，突显了在检验修改引力理论时采用非微扰自旋处理的重要性。

Conclusion: By employing numerical black-hole backgrounds valid at large spins, this work enables precise computation of quasinormal mode corrections in effective-field-theory extensions of gravity. The significant enhancement of deviations at high spins suggests that observations of rapidly spinning black holes can provide powerful constraints on scalar-tensor modifications such as scalar Gauss-Bonnet and dynamical Chern-Simons gravity.

通过采用适用于大自旋的数值黑洞背景，本工作实现了在引力有效场论扩展中对准正则模修正的精确计算。高自旋下偏差的显著增强表明，对快速旋转黑洞的观测可为标量-张量类修改引力（如标量高斯-邦特和动力学陈-西蒙斯引力）提供强有力的约束。

Abstract: In an effective-field-theory framework for gravity, black-hole quasinormal mode spectra acquire corrections in quadratic-curvature, scalar-tensor extensions of general relativity. Previous calculations of such corrections were limited to moderate spins, since the corresponding background solutions relied on expansions in the spin parameter. Using recently constructed numerical black-hole solutions valid for large spin, we compute the leading-order deviations from general relativity in the scalar quasinormal mode spectrum of rotating black holes in scalar Gauss-Bonnet and dynamical Chern-Simons gravity. We solve the resulting perturbation equations with pseudo-spectral collocation methods, allowing us to determine the quasinormal-mode corrections for dimensionless spins up to $a/M=0.99$, with accuracy better than $\lesssim 10^{-3}$ for the $l=m=0$ mode and $\lesssim 10^{-6}$ for higher multipoles. For spins $a/M>0.9$, the corrections to certain modes can increase by orders of magnitude.

</details>


### [22] [Fluid perturbations from expanding bubbles in first-order phase transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02240)
*Chiara Caprini,Antonino S. Midiri,Simona Procacci,Alberto Roper Pol*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: We derive a refined template for the velocity power spectrum generated during a first-order phase transition in the radiation-dominated era, showing that spectral breaks are determined by the position of discontinuities in the velocity profile rather than bubble size or sound shell thickness. This has significant implications for supersonic deflagrations near the Chapman-Jouguet speed, affecting gravitational wave predictions. The asymptotic behavior of the spectrum is governed by single-bubble profiles at large scales and velocity discontinuities at small scales. Results are implemented in the public Python package CosmoGW.

我们推导了辐射主导时期一阶相变期间产生的速度场功率谱的改进模板，表明谱上的拐点由速度分布不连续处的位置决定，而非气泡大小或声学壳层厚度。这对接近Chapman-Jouguet速度的超声速去燃现象具有重要意义，并影响引力波预测。谱的渐近行为在大尺度上由单个气泡轮廓积分决定，在小尺度上由速度轮廓的不连续性决定。所有结果已集成到公开Python包CosmoGW中。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The production of gravitational waves from first-order phase transitions depends crucially on the velocity field's power spectrum, particularly during the sound-wave regime. Previous templates assumed that spectral breaks were set by bubble size and sound shell thickness, but a more accurate understanding of the underlying hydrodynamics—especially for non-trivial wall velocities—is needed to improve predictions of gravitational wave signals.

引力波的产生强烈依赖于速度场的功率谱，特别是在声波阶段。以往的模板假设谱拐点由气泡尺寸和声壳厚度决定，但为了更精确预测引力波信号，需要对底层流体动力学（尤其是非平凡壁速度情形）有更准确的理解。

Method: We analyze the Fourier-space velocity power spectrum by decomposing the multi-bubble velocity field into contributions from individual bubbles, using realistic velocity profiles obtained from hydrodynamic simulations. We identify the role of discontinuities in the velocity profile (e.g., shock fronts) in setting the scale-dependent features of the spectrum. We compute the power spectrum analytically in limiting cases and validate with numerical integration, considering both exponential and simultaneous nucleation scenarios.

通过将多气泡速度场分解为单个气泡贡献，结合来自流体动力学模拟的真实速度轮廓，在傅里叶空间分析速度功率谱。我们识别出速度轮廓中不连续性（如激波前缘）在设定谱的尺度依赖特征中的作用。在极限情况下解析计算功率谱，并通过数值积分验证，同时考虑指数型和同时型成核情景。

Result: We find that the two breaks in the velocity power spectrum correspond to the positions of discontinuities in the fluid velocity profile, not the average bubble size or sound shell width. For supersonic deflagrations, as the wall velocity approaches the Chapman-Jouguet speed, the separation between the two breaks increases and the intermediate slope becomes steeper. At large scales, the spectrum follows $ k^3 $ scaling from the integral of single-bubble profiles; at small scales, it exhibits a $ k^{-1} $ tail due to velocity discontinuities. These results are robust across different nucleation distributions (exponential vs. simultaneous).

我们发现速度功率谱中的两个拐点对应于流体速度轮廓中不连续性的位置，而非平均气泡尺寸或声壳宽度。对于超声速去燃，当壁速度接近Chapman-Jouguet速度时，两个拐点之间的分离增大，中间斜率变得更陡。在大尺度上，谱遵循来自单气泡轮廓积分的$ k^3 $标度；在小尺度上，由于速度不连续性呈现出$ k^{-1} $尾部。这些结果在不同成核分布（指数型与同时型）下均稳健。

Conclusion: The standard interpretation of spectral breaks in the velocity power spectrum must be revised: they are set by hydrodynamic discontinuities rather than geometric scales like bubble size. This correction significantly impacts the modeling of anisotropic stresses and thus the predicted gravitational wave spectrum from cosmological phase transitions, especially for fast-moving bubble walls. Our findings are implemented in the publicly available CosmoGW package for use in precision cosmology.

必须修正对速度功率谱中谱拐点的标准解释：它们由流体动力学不连续性决定，而非气泡大小等几何尺度。这一修正显著影响各向异性应力的建模，从而影响宇宙相变（尤其快速移动气泡壁情形）引力波谱的预测。我们的结果已实现在公开可用的CosmoGW包中，可用于精确宇宙学研究。

Abstract: We study the power spectrum of the velocity field induced during a first-order phase transition occurring in the radiation-dominated era. We focus on the phase of bubble expansion, assuming that it ends with the onset of the sound-wave regime. The main result we present is a refined template for the velocity spectrum at the beginning of the sound-wave phase, which can be used for studying the resulting anisotropic stresses and gravitational wave production. In particular, we find that the breaks in the velocity spectrum are not associated to the bubble size and the sound shell thickness, as previously proposed, but to the position of the discontinuities. This distinction is particularly relevant for supersonic deflagrations, as it implies that the intermediate slope is more pronounced and the two breaks are more separated when the wall velocity approaches the Chapman-Jouget speed, instead of the sound speed. We also show that the asymptotic branches of the velocity power spectrum are determined by the integral over the single-bubble profiles at large scales, and by the discontinuities of the velocity profiles at small scales. Furthermore, we study the dependence of the two breaks and the intermediate slope on the distribution function of the times of bubble nucleation (exponential and simultaneous). All the results presented in this work have been included in the public Python package CosmoGW.

</details>

### [23] [Three-form lifting of dilaton flat direction without and with gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01272)
*Georgios K. Karananas*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper demonstrates that spontaneous scale symmetry breaking can occur without a flat direction in the action by coupling the dilaton to a three-form field, preserving gauge and dilatation invariance; the resulting potential forms an exponential plateau when gravity is included.

论文表明，通过将稀释子（dilaton）与三形式场（three-form field）耦合，可以在没有作用量中平坦方向的情况下实现自发尺度对称性破缺，同时保持规范和膨胀不变性；当包含引力时，相应的势能呈现指数平台形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Spontaneous scale symmetry breaking is traditionally linked to the existence of a flat direction (modulus) in the action, which poses challenges for stabilizing the dilaton and generating a non-trivial potential. The authors aim to show that such a flat direction is not necessary if the dilaton couples to a three-form field in a way that respects both gauge invariance and dilatations.

自发尺度对称性破缺传统上与作用量中的平坦方向（模空间）相关联，这对稳定稀释子并生成非平凡势能构成了挑战。作者旨在表明，如果稀释子以符合规范不变性和膨胀不变性的方式与三形式场耦合，则这种平坦方向并非必需。

Method: The authors construct a theoretical framework where the dilaton couples to a three-form gauge field through a gauge- and dilatation-invariant interaction. They analyze the effective dynamics of this system, particularly focusing on how the three-form modifies the dilaton potential. Gravity is then incorporated via the Jordan or Einstein frame to study the full gravitational implications.

作者构建了一个理论框架，其中稀释子通过满足规范不变性和膨胀不变性的相互作用与三形式规范场耦合。他们分析了该系统的有效动力学，特别关注三形式如何修改稀释子势。随后通过Jordan或Einstein框架引入引力，以研究其完整的引力效应。

Result: The coupling to the three-form lifts the flat direction of the dilaton potential without introducing explicit scale-symmetry-breaking terms. In the presence of gravity, the effective potential for the dilaton takes the form of an exponential plateau, $ V(\phi) \sim e^{-\lambda \phi} $, which resembles potentials used in inflation or dark energy models.

与三形式的耦合在不引入显式尺度对称性破缺项的情况下消除了稀释子势的平坦方向。在引力存在下，稀释子的有效势呈现指数平台形式 $ V(\phi) \sim e^{-\lambda \phi} $，类似于暴胀或暗能量模型中使用的势。

Conclusion: Spontaneous breaking of scale symmetry can occur without a flat direction in the action, provided the dilaton interacts with a three-form field in a symmetric manner. This mechanism offers a novel way to generate exponentially flat potentials relevant for cosmological model building, such as inflation or dark energy, while maintaining exact scale invariance at the fundamental level.

只要稀释子以对称方式与三形式场相互作用，即使作用量中没有平坦方向，也可以发生尺度对称性的自发破缺。这一机制为生成与宇宙学建模（如暴胀或暗能量）相关的指数平坦势提供了新途径，同时在基本层面上保持了精确的尺度不变性。

Abstract: Spontaneous scale symmetry breaking is commonly associated with a flat direction in the action. We show that this need not be so if the dilaton is coupled to a three-form field in a manner compatible with gauge invariance and dilatations. The resulting effective dynamics lifts the flat direction without introducing explicit scale-violating operators. When gravity is included, the corresponding potential takes the form of an exponential plateau.

### [24] [Symplectic structure in open string field theory III: Electric field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01273)
*Vinícius Bernardes,Theodore Erler,Atakan Hilmi Fırat*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: A new formula for the symplectic structure in open string field theory is used to compute the energy of a D-brane with constant electric flux, showing consistency with the Dirac-Born-Infeld (DBI) action via a generalized Ellwood invariant.

使用开放弦场论中辛结构的新公式计算带有恒定电通量D膜的能量，并通过推广至非多项式开放弦场论的Ellwood不变量，证明其与Dirac-Born-Infeld（DBI）作用的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the energy of D-branes with gauge field excitations, such as constant electric flux, is crucial for verifying the consistency of open string field theory (OSFT) with effective field theory descriptions like the DBI action. The motivation is to test whether recently developed tools—such as a new symplectic structure and generalized Ellwood invariant—can correctly reproduce physical observables in non-trivial backgrounds.

理解带有规范场激发（如恒定电通量）的D膜能量对于验证开放弦场论（OSFT）与有效场论（如DBI作用）描述之间的一致性至关重要。研究动机在于检验新发展的工具——如新的辛结构和推广的Ellwoood不变量——能否在非平凡背景下正确重现物理可观测量。

Method: The authors employ a newly derived formula for the symplectic structure on the phase space of open string field theory. They construct a solution corresponding to a D-brane with constant electric flux and compute its energy using this symplectic form. The result is then compared with the energy from the Dirac-Born-Infeld action. Consistency is established by generalizing the Ellwood invariant—previously defined for polynomial theories—to nonpolynomial open string field theories.

作者采用了一个新推导出的开放弦场论相空间上辛结构的公式。他们构造了一个对应于带有恒定电通量D膜的解，并利用该辛形式计算其能量。然后将结果与Dirac-Born-Infeld作用中的能量进行比较。通过将此前定义于多项式理论中的Ellwood不变量推广到非多项式开放弦场论来建立一致性。

Result: The computed energy of the D-brane with constant electric flux matches exactly the prediction from the Dirac-Born-Infeld action. The successful generalization of the Ellwood invariant to nonpolynomial OSFT provides a robust tool for evaluating physical quantities in non-trivial gauge backgrounds.

计算得到的带恒定电通量D膜的能量与Dirac-Born-Infeld作用的预测完全一致。将Ellwood不变量成功推广至非多项式OSFT为在非平凡规范背景下评估物理量提供了可靠工具。

Conclusion: The new symplectic structure in open string field theory correctly captures the physical energy of D-branes with constant electric fields. The generalized Ellwood invariant serves as a valid on-shell observable in nonpolynomial OSFT, reinforcing the consistency between OSFT and low-energy effective actions like DBI.

开放弦场论中的新辛结构能正确捕捉带有恒定电场的D膜的物理能量。推广后的Ellwood不变量可作为非多项式OSFT中有效的壳上可观测量，加强了OSFT与低能有效作用（如DBI）之间的一致性。

Abstract: We use a new formula for the symplectic structure on the phase space of open string field theory to evaluate the energy of a D-brane carrying a constant electric flux. This is shown to be consistent with the energy computed using the Dirac-Born-Infeld action through a generalization of the Ellwood invariant to nonpolynomial open string field theories.

### [25] [Descending into the Modular Bootstrap](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01275)
*Nathan Benjamin,A. Liam Fitzpatrick,Wei Li,Jesse Thaler*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We apply machine-learning-inspired optimization to solve the modular bootstrap in 2d CFTs with $c > 1$, using the Virasoro algebra. By formulating modular invariance as a loss function and employing a novel singular-value-based optimizer (Sven), we identify candidate CFTs in the central charge range $1 < c \leq \frac{8}{7}$, where no known theories exist. We also propose improved constraints on the spectral gap near $c=1$ and introduce methods to estimate truncation uncertainty.

我们采用受机器学习启发的优化方法求解 $c > 1$ 的二维共形场论（2d CFT）中的模不变自举方程。通过将模不变性转化为损失函数，并使用一种新的基于奇异值的优化器（Sven），我们在尚无已知理论的中心电荷范围 $1 < c \leq \frac{8}{7}$ 内数值构造了候选CFT。我们还提出了对 $c=1$ 附近谱隙更严格的约束，并引入了估计截断不确定性的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Two-dimensional conformal field theories (2d CFTs) are central to string theory and statistical mechanics, yet their landscape—especially for irrational central charges or non-rational theories—is poorly understood. The modular bootstrap provides a powerful non-perturbative approach by enforcing modular invariance of the torus partition function, but solving it analytically is generally intractable. Existing numerical methods struggle with the complex, hierarchical structure of the modular bootstrap landscape. This paper aims to develop more efficient and reliable numerical techniques to explore uncharted regions of 2d CFT space, particularly near $c = 1$, where analytic control is limited and new physics may emerge.

二维共形场论（2d CFT）在弦论和统计力学中至关重要，但其理论图景——尤其是对于无理中心电荷或非有理理论——仍不清楚。模自举通过强制环面配分函数的模不变性提供了一种强大的非微扰方法，但解析求解通常不可行。现有的数值方法难以处理模自举景观的复杂层级结构。本文旨在发展更高效可靠的数值技术，以探索2d CFT空间中尚未被研究的区域，特别是在 $c = 1$ 附近，该区域解析控制有限且可能存在新物理。

Method: We formulate the modular bootstrap equation as a minimization problem by defining a loss function that quantifies the failure of modular invariance of a given trial partition function. The partition function is built from a spectrum of primary operators under the Virasoro algebra with central charge $c > 1$. We truncate the spectrum to low-dimension operators and use numerical optimization to find spectra that minimize the loss. Two key innovations enhance reliability: (1) a method to estimate the error due to spectral truncation by analyzing the contribution of neglected high-dimension states, and (2) the use of a new optimizer called Sven, which leverages singular value decomposition to better navigate the multi-scale, hierarchical loss landscape compared to standard gradient descent.

我们将模自举方程转化为一个最小化问题，定义了一个损失函数来量化给定试验配分函数违反模不变性的程度。配分函数由中心电荷 $c > 1$ 下 Virasoro 代数的初级算符谱构建。我们对谱进行低维截断，并使用数值优化寻找使损失最小的谱。两个关键技术改进提高了可靠性：(1) 通过分析被忽略的高维态贡献来估计谱截断误差的方法；(2) 使用一种名为 Sven 的新型优化器，该优化器利用奇异值分解，在多尺度、层级化的损失景观中比标准梯度下降更有效。

Result: We successfully construct candidate partition functions for 2d CFTs in the previously unexplored range $1 < c \leq \frac{8}{7}$. These solutions appear to form a continuous family, suggesting the existence of a continuum of modular-invariant theories in this regime—potentially indicating new irrational CFTs. Our method reveals a tighter bound on the spectral gap near $c = 1$, improving upon the known bound $\Delta_{\rm gap} \leq \frac{c}{6} + \frac{1}{3}$, with numerical evidence suggesting $\Delta_{\rm gap} < \frac{c}{6} + \frac{1}{3} - \epsilon$ for small $\epsilon > 0$. The Sven optimizer demonstrates superior performance in avoiding local minima and converging to physically meaningful solutions compared to gradient-based methods.

我们成功构造了在先前未探索范围 $1 < c \leq \frac{8}{7}$ 内二维CFT的候选配分函数。这些解似乎形成一个连续族，表明在此区域内可能存在一系列模不变理论——可能暗示新的无理CFT的存在。我们的方法揭示了在 $c = 1$ 附近更紧的谱隙界限，优于已知的 $\Delta_{\rm gap} \leq \frac{c}{6} + \frac{1}{3}$ 界限，数值证据表明存在小量 $\epsilon > 0$ 使得 $\Delta_{\rm gap} < \frac{c}{6} + \frac{1}{3} - \epsilon$。与基于梯度的方法相比，Sven优化器在避免局部极小值并收敛到物理上有意义的解方面表现出更优性能。

Conclusion: This work demonstrates that machine-learning-style optimization, combined with domain-specific insights like singular value analysis, can significantly advance the numerical exploration of 2d CFTs via the modular bootstrap. The discovery of candidate theories in the $c \in (1, \frac{8}{7}]$ range suggests a richer structure in the CFT landscape than previously appreciated. Moreover, the improved bound on the spectral gap near $c=1$ hints at deeper constraints imposed by modular invariance. The framework introduced here—especially the Sven optimizer and truncation error estimation—can be generalized to other bootstrap problems, including higher dimensions and supersymmetric theories.

本研究表明，结合领域特定洞察（如奇异值分析）的类机器学习优化方法，能显著推进通过模自举对二维CFT的数值探索。在 $c \in (1, \frac{8}{7}]$ 范围内发现候选理论，表明CFT图景比此前认识的更为丰富。此外，$c=1$ 附近谱隙的改进界限暗示模不变性施加了更深层的约束。本文引入的框架——特别是Sven优化器和截断误差估计——可推广至其他自举问题，包括高维和超对称理论。

Abstract: In this paper, we attempt to explore the landscape of two-dimensional conformal field theories (2d CFTs) by efficiently searching for numerical solutions to the modular bootstrap equation using machine-learning-style optimization. The torus partition function of a 2d CFT is fixed by the spectrum of its primary operators and its chiral algebra, which we take to be the Virasoro algebra with $c>1$. We translate the requirement that this partition function is modular invariant into a loss function, which we then minimize to identify possible primary spectra. Our approach involves two technical innovations that facilitate finding reliable candidate CFTs. The first is a strategy to estimate the uncertainty associated with truncating the spectrum to the lowest dimension operators. The second is the use of a new singular-value-based optimizer (Sven) that is more effective than gradient descent at navigating the hierarchical structure of the loss landscape. We numerically construct candidate truncated CFT partition functions with central charges between 1 and $\frac{8}{7}$, a range devoid of known examples, and argue that these candidates likely come from a continuous space of modular bootstrap solutions. We also provide evidence for a more stringent constraint on the spectral gap near $c = 1$ than the existing bound of $Δ_{\rm gap} \le \frac{c}{6} + \frac{1}{3}$.

</details>


### [26] [Solving Lévy Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01320)
*Budhaditya Bhattacharjee,William. E. Salazar,Alexei Andreanov,Dario Rosa*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We solve the large-$N$ limit of the Lévy Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (LSYK) model with couplings drawn from a Lévy Stable distribution characterized by tail exponent $\mu \in [0,2]$, generalizing the Gaussian SYK model. Using a bosonic oscillator representation, we derive and solve Schwinger-Dyson equations in the large-$q$ and infrared limits, compute thermodynamic quantities, and analyze chaotic behavior via Krylov and Lyapunov exponents. The model interpolates continuously between a free theory ($\mu=0$) and maximal chaos ($\mu=2$), exhibiting non-maximal chaos for $0 < \mu < 2$. Connections to holography and non-Fermi liquids are discussed.

我们求解了Lévy Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev（LSYK）模型在大$N$极限下的精确解，其中耦合常数服从以尾部指数$\mu \in [0,2]$为参数的Lévy稳定分布，推广了标准高斯SYK模型。通过玻色振子表示法推导并求解了大$q$和红外极限下的Schwinger-Dyson方程，计算了热力学量，并通过Krylov指数和Lyapunov指数分析混沌行为。该模型在自由理论（$\mu=0$）与最大混沌的高斯SYK模型（$\mu=2$）之间连续插值，在中间区域$0 < \mu < 2$保持非最大混沌。讨论了其在全息对偶和非费米液体理论中的含义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The standard SYK model assumes Gaussian-distributed random couplings, which leads to maximal chaos and solvability in the large-$N$ limit. However, real-world complex systems often exhibit heavy-tailed coupling distributions. The LSYK model replaces Gaussian couplings with Lévy Stable distributions to study the effects of such heavy tails on quantum chaos, thermodynamics, and emergent conformal symmetry. This allows exploration of a broader universality class beyond Gaussian randomness.

标准SYK模型假设耦合为高斯分布，导致最大混沌和大$N$极限下的可解性。然而，真实复杂系统常表现出重尾耦合分布。LSYK模型采用Lévy稳定分布替代高斯耦合，以研究重尾对量子混沌、热力学及涌现共形对称性的影响，从而探索超越高斯随机性的更广泛普适类。

Method: Starting from the LSYK Hamiltonian and partition function, we employ a bosonic oscillator representation to handle the non-Gaussian nature of Lévy-distributed couplings. We derive the large-$N$ Schwinger-Dyson equations for the Green's function and self-energy. These are solved analytically in the large-$q$ and low-temperature limits, and numerically otherwise. Chaos is studied via the Krylov complexity (from the large-$q$ Green's function) and the out-of-time-order correlator (OTOC), from which the Lyapunov exponent is extracted. Thermodynamic quantities are computed from the free energy. An alternative decomposition of the Lévy distribution is also explored, linking LSYK to Gaussian SYK through effective couplings.

从LSYK哈密顿量和配分函数出发，采用玻色振子表示处理Lévy分布耦合的非高斯特性。推导出Green函数和自能的大$N$ Schwinger-Dyson方程，在大$q$和低温极限下解析求解，其余情况数值求解。通过Krylov复杂度（来自大$q$ Green函数）和非时序关联函数（OTOC）研究混沌，提取Lyapunov指数。热力学量由自由能计算得出。还探讨了Lévy分布的另一种分解方式，通过有效耦合将LSYK与Gaussian SYK联系起来。

Result: The parameter $\mu$ controls the degree of chaos and interaction strength: at $\mu = 0$, the system reduces to a free theory; at $\mu = 2$, it recovers the maximally chaotic Gaussian SYK model. For $0 < \mu < 2$, the model exhibits non-maximal chaos, with both Krylov and Lyapunov exponents depending continuously on $\mu$. Thermodynamic functions (entropy, free energy, specific heat) deviate from Gaussian SYK predictions, showing power-law behaviors influenced by $\mu$. The large-$q$ solution reveals an emergent conformal symmetry in the IR, modified by $\mu$-dependent corrections. The alternative representation confirms equivalence under renormalization of effective interactions.

参数$\mu$控制混沌程度和相互作用强度：当$\mu = 0$时系统退化为自由理论；$\mu = 2$时恢复最大混沌的高斯SYK模型。在$0 < \mu < 2$区间，模型表现出非最大混沌，Krylov指数和Lyapunov指数均连续依赖于$\mu$。热力学函数（熵、自由能、比热）偏离高斯SYK预测，呈现受$\mu$影响的幂律行为。大$q$解揭示了红外区涌现的共形对称性，其修正项依赖于$\mu$。另一种表示法证实了在有效相互作用重整化下的等价性。

Conclusion: The LSYK model provides a solvable extension of the SYK framework to heavy-tailed disorder, enriching the landscape of non-Fermi liquid and holographic quantum matter. The continuous interpolation controlled by $\mu$ offers a tunable model of quantum chaos, bridging integrable and maximally chaotic regimes. The results suggest that Lévy-stable distributed couplings lead to novel critical behavior and modified holographic duals, potentially relevant for strongly disordered condensed matter and black hole physics.

LSYK模型将SYK框架扩展到重尾无序情形，丰富了非费米液体和全息量子物质的研究图景。由$\mu$控制的连续插值提供了一个可调的量子混沌模型，连接了可积与最大混沌区域。结果表明，Lévy稳定分布的耦合会导致新的临界行为和修改的全息对偶，可能与强无序凝聚态系统和黑洞物理相关。

Abstract: We present an exact solution in the large-$N$ limit of the Lévy Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev (LSYK) model introduced in Ref. [1], wherein the couplings are drawn from a Lévy Stable distribution parameterized by a tail exponent $μ\in [0, 2]$. Starting from the Hamiltonian and its associated partition function, we highlight the key differences from the standard Gaussian SYK model and derive the large-$N$ Schwinger-Dyson equations via a bosonic oscillator representation of the action. These equations are solved both numerically and analytically in the large-$q$ and infrared limits. We subsequently analyze the chaotic properties of the model by computing the Krylov exponent from the large-$q$ Green's function and extracting the Lyapunov exponent from the $4$-point function. The parameter $μ$ continuously interpolates between a free theory at $μ= 0$ and the conventional, maximally chaotic Gaussian SYK model at $μ= 2$, with non-maximal chaos persisting throughout the intermediate regime $0 < μ< 2$. Thermodynamic quantities, including the entropy, free energy, average energy, and specific heat capacity, are computed and compared with their Gaussian SYK counterparts. The interpretations of the thermodynamics are discussed with respect to the holographic dual and non-Fermi liquid theory. Finally, we discuss an alternative representation of the LSYK model based on a distinct decomposition of the Lévy Stable distribution, which establishes a non-trivial connection to Gaussian SYK, and provide supporting analytical and numerical results in the appendices.

</details>


### [27] [AI usage in string theory, a case study: String Vacua in the Interior of Moduli Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01384)
*Timm Wrase*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper discusses recent progress in constructing stable $\mathcal{N}=1$ Minkowski vacua in type IIB string theory using Landau--Ginzburg models, particularly the $1^9$ and $2^6$ models, which are mirror to rigid Calabi--Yau threefolds. These models lack Kähler moduli, enabling precise studies of flux stabilization and swampland conjectures. The results provide concrete tests for the tadpole and massless Minkowski conjectures, with reference to recent work (arXiv:2407.16758) identifying fully massive vacua.

本文讨论了在IIB型弦理论中使用Landau-Ginzburg模型（特别是$1^9$和$2^6$模型）构建稳定的$\mathcal{N}=1$闵可夫斯基真空的最新进展，这些模型是刚性Calabi-Yau三重态的镜像。由于缺乏Kähler模，这些模型使得对通量稳定化和沼泽地猜想的研究更加精确。高阶通量超势项被证明可以稳定先前无质量的场，在$2^6$模型中产生孤立的闵可夫斯基真空。结果为泡利和无质量闵可夫斯基猜想提供了具体的测试，并参考了最近的工作（arXiv:2407.16758），该工作识别出首个所有场均为有质量的此类真空。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To explore whether all moduli can be stabilized in four-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=1$ Minkowski string vacua deep in moduli space, especially in settings free of Kähler moduli, thereby providing clean environments to test swampland conjectures such as the absence of massless scalars in consistent quantum gravity theories and the tadpole conjecture. The use of exactly solvable worldsheet theories like Landau--Ginzburg models allows for rigorous control over quantum corrections.

旨在探索在模空间深处的四维$\mathcal{N}=1$闵可夫斯基弦真空中是否所有模都可以被稳定，特别是在没有Kähler模的情况下，从而提供一个清晰的环境来检验诸如一致量子引力理论中不存在无质量标量场和泡利猜想等沼泽地猜想。使用如Landau-Ginzburg模型这样精确可解的世界面理论，可以严格控制量子修正。

Method: The analysis is based on type IIB string compactifications on orientifolds of Gepner models, realized via exactly solvable $\mathcal{N}=2$ Landau--Ginzburg theories. Flux superpotentials are computed including higher-order terms beyond quadratic approximation. Moduli stabilization is studied by analyzing critical points of the superpotential, with emphasis on the $1^9$ and $2^6$ models. Techniques include exact conformal field theory methods, algebraic geometry for determining D-term constraints, and numerical searches for vacua. Reference is made to independent work (arXiv:2407.16758) that identifies fully stabilized vacua.

分析基于在Gepner模型的取向面上进行IIB型弦紧化，通过精确可解的$\mathcal{N}=2$ Landau-Ginzburg理论实现。计算了通量超势，包括超出二次近似的高阶项。通过分析超势的临界点来研究模的稳定化，重点是$1^9$和$2^6$模型。技术包括精确共形场论方法、用于确定D项约束的代数几何以及对真空的数值搜索。参考了独立工作（arXiv:2407.16758），该工作识别出完全稳定的真空。

Result: Higher-order terms in the flux superpotential are essential for stabilizing certain flat directions that remain massless at quadratic order. In the $2^6$ model, this leads to the existence of isolated $\mathcal{N}=1$ Minkowski vacua. The absence of Kähler moduli in these mirror-rigid constructions allows for sharp tests of the massless Minkowski conjecture and the tadpole conjecture. The work referenced in arXiv:2407.16758 demonstrates the first explicit realization of such vacua with all fields massive, confirming the viability of full moduli stabilization in this framework.

通量超势中的高阶项对于稳定某些在二次阶仍保持无质量的平坦方向至关重要。在$2^6$模型中，这导致了孤立的$\mathcal{N}=1$闵可夫斯基真空的存在。这些镜像刚性构造中缺乏Kähler模，使得对无质量闵可夫斯基猜想和泡利猜想的精确检验成为可能。arXiv:2407.16758中引用的工作展示了首个所有场均为有质量的此类真空的具体实现，证实了在此框架内完全模稳定化的可行性。

Conclusion: Exact worldsheet constructions like the $1^9$ and $2^6$ Landau--Ginzburg models provide powerful laboratories for studying moduli stabilization and swampland conjectures in string theory. The inclusion of higher-order flux superpotential terms is crucial for achieving full stability, and recent results confirm the existence of isolated Minkowski vacua with all moduli fixed. These setups offer rigorous data for testing fundamental conjectures about quantum gravity, particularly the massless Minkowski and tadpole conjectures.

像$1^9$和$2^6$ Landau-Ginzburg模型这样的精确世界面构造为研究弦理论中的模稳定化和沼泽地猜想提供了强大的实验室。包含高阶通量超势项对于实现完全稳定性至关重要，最近的结果证实了存在所有模都被固定的孤立闵可夫斯基真空。这些设置为测试关于量子引力的基本猜想，特别是无质量闵可夫斯基和泡利猜想，提供了严格的数据。

Abstract: These proceedings start with a discussion of my recent experiences with large language models and potential implications for their usage in our field. This is followed by an AI generated summary of my talk at the workshop ``Recent Progress in Computational String Geometry,'' held at the Chennai Mathematical Institute in January 2026. The focus is on four-dimensional $\mathcal{N}=1$ Minkowski vacua in type IIB compactifications that live deep in the interior of moduli space and admit an exact worldsheet description in terms of Landau--Ginzburg models. The main examples are the $1^9$ and $2^6$ models, mirror to rigid Calabi--Yau threefolds and therefore free of Kähler moduli. This makes them ideal laboratories for testing whether fluxes can stabilize all fields and for probing conjectures about the string landscape and the swampland. Based mostly on arXiv:2406.03435, arXiv:2407.16756, we review how higher-order terms in the flux superpotential can stabilize fields that remain massless at quadratic order, how isolated Minkowski vacua arise in the $2^6$ model, and why these constructions provide sharp data for the tadpole and massless Minkowski conjectures. We also emphasize the role of arXiv:2407.16758 by other authors, where the first Minkowski vacua of this type with all fields massive were identified.

### [28] [Entanglement entropy and conformal bounds for $d=5$ CFTs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01436)
*Pablo Bueno,Adam Fernández García,Francesco Gentile,Oscar Lasso Andino,Javier Moreno*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper investigates the universal constant term $F(A)$ in the entanglement entropy of odd-dimensional CFTs, showing that while $F(A)$ has a local minimum at the spherical geometry in CFT$_5$, it is neither upper- nor lower-bounded for general regions, invalidating a previously conjectured extremization principle. Instead, a weaker bound involving $C_T/F_0$ is proposed and verified across known CFT$_5$'s.

本文研究了奇数维共形场论（CFT）中纠缠熵的普适常数项 $F(A)$，表明尽管在CFT$_5$中$F(A)$在球形几何附近具有局部极小值，但对于一般区域其值无上下界，从而否定了此前提出的极值猜想。取而代之，本文提出并验证了一个涉及应力张量两点函数与球面上欧几里得配分函数比值的弱约束条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: In odd-dimensional CFTs, the universal part of entanglement entropy, encoded in $F(A)$, provides a meaningful measure of quantum degrees of freedom. In 3D, $F(A)$ is positive and minimized by the disk, with strong evidence suggesting it is maximized within the space of theories by the free scalar. The authors aim to test whether analogous properties hold in higher dimensions, particularly $d=5$, where new geometric and conformal anomalies arise.

在奇数维CFT中，纠缠熵的普适部分$F(A)$是量子自由度的有效度量。在三维情况下，$F(A)$为正且由圆盘最小化，并有强证据表明其在理论空间中由自由标量场最大化。作者旨在检验类似性质是否在更高维度（特别是$d=5$）成立，其中会出现新的几何与共形反常。

Method: The authors use mutual information to define $F(A)$ robustly under small deformations of entangling surfaces. They analyze perturbative expansions around the spherical entangling surface $\mathbb{S}^3$ in CFT$_5$, leveraging conformal symmetry and known results for stress-tensor correlators. They compute corrections to $F_\varepsilon$ for deformed spheres and compare $C_T/F_0$ ratios across various CFT$_5$ models, including free fields and holographic theories.

作者利用互信息在纠缠面的小变形下稳健定义$F(A)$。他们基于CFT$_5$中的球面$\mathbb{S}^3$展开微扰分析，利用共形对称性及已知的应力张量关联函数结果，计算了变形球面下$F_\varepsilon$的修正，并比较了包括自由场和全息理论在内的各种CFT$_5$模型的$C_T/F_0$比值。

Result: While $F(A)$ has a local minimum at the round sphere in CFT$_5$, it can attain arbitrarily large positive or negative values for sufficiently deformed regions, so it is unbounded from above and below. Thus, the conjecture that $F(A)/F_0$ is universally maximized by the free scalar fails in $d=5$. However, the ratio $C_T/F_0$ satisfies $C_T/F_0 \leq [C_T/F_0]_{\text{free scalar}} \approx 0.314$ for all known CFT$_5$'s, suggesting a weaker but robust bound.

尽管在CFT$_5$中$F(A)$在球形区域附近具有局部极小值，但对于足够变形的区域可取得任意大正值或负值，因此既无上界也无下界。因此，在$d=5$时，$F(A)/F_0$由自由标量场普遍最大化的猜想不成立。然而，所有已知CFT$_5$均满足比值$C_T/F_0 \leq [C_T/F_0]_{\text{free scalar}} \approx 0.314$，提示存在一个较弱但稳健的界限。

Conclusion: The extremality conjecture for $F(A)/F_0$ does not generalize to CFT$_5$. Instead, a weaker bound involving the stress-tensor central charge $C_T$ and the sphere free energy $F_0$ holds empirically across known theories. This suggests that constraints on entanglement geometry in higher dimensions may be captured through combinations of $C_T$ and $F_0$, opening new avenues for bootstrap and holographic studies in higher-dimensional CFTs.

$F(A)/F_0$的极值猜想无法推广到CFT$_5$。相反，一个涉及应力张量中心荷$C_T$与球面自由能$F_0$的弱约束在已知理论中普遍成立。这表明高维CFT中纠缠几何的限制可能通过$C_T$与$F_0$的组合来刻画，为高维共形场论的bootstrap与全息研究开辟了新路径。

Abstract: The entanglement entropy of spacetime regions $A$ in odd-dimensional conformal field theories (CFTs) contains a universal constant term, $(-1)^{\frac{d-1}{2}}F(A)$. This quantity can be robustly defined by considering the mutual information of pairs of slightly deformed versions of $A$. In the case of general three-dimensional CFTs, $F(A)$ is positive definite and bounded below by the round disk result, $F(A)\geq F_0\equiv F(\partial A=\mathbb{S}^1)$. Additionally, strong evidence has been provided that for every region $A$, $F(A)/F_0$ is maximized, within the space of CFT$_3$'s, by the free scalar field result. In this paper we show that while $F(A)$ remains a local minimum around $F_0\equiv F(\partial A=\mathbb{S}^3)$ for small deformations of the spherical entangling surface, it can take values of arbitrarily large magnitude with either sign for more general regions, and hence it is neither upper- nor lower-bounded in general CFT$_5$'s. We argue that an analogous conjecture regarding the extremization of $F(A)/F_0$ for general regions within the space of theories fails in $d=5$. We instead analyze the viability of the weaker bound, $F_ε/F_0\leq \left[F_ε/F_0\right]_{\text{free scalar}}$, $\forall$CFT$_5$ for general small geometric deformations of the spherical entangling surface. This is equivalent to a general constraint involving the stress-tensor two-point function $C_T$ and the Euclidean partition function on the sphere, namely, $C_T/F_0\leq \left[C_T/F_0\right]_{\text{ free scalar}}\approx 0.314$, which we show to hold for all known CFT$_5$'s. We also comment on possible extensions of this result to higher dimensions.

</details>


### [29] [The $W_n$ Light One-Point Torus Conformal Block](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01804)
*Armen Poghosyan,Hasmik Poghosyan*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We analyze the light asymptotic limit of the one-point torus conformal block in $A_{n-1}$ Toda field theory via the AGT correspondence, mapping it to the instanton partition function of 4d ${\cal N}=2^*$ $U(n)$ SYM. In the $b \to 0$ limit at fixed conformal dimensions, we find a drastic simplification: only Young diagram boxes with specific arm lengths contribute to bifundamental factors. This enables an explicit formula for the light one-point torus $W_n$ block for any $n \geq 2$. The result is verified for $n=2$ (Liouville) against the known hypergeometric form and for $n=3$ ($W_3$) against shadow formalism results.

我们通过AGT对应研究了$A_{n-1}$ Toda场论中单点环面共形块的轻渐近极限，将其映射为四维${\cal N}=2^*$ $U(n)$超对称杨-米尔斯理论的瞬子配分函数。在固定共形维度下取$b \to 0$极限时，我们发现瞬子和大幅简化：仅具有特定臂长的杨图方框对双基表示因子有贡献。这使我们得以推导出适用于任意$n \geq 2$的轻单点环面$W_n$共形块的显式表达式。结果在$n=2$（Liouville）情形下与已知的超几何表示一致，在$n=3$（$W_3$）情形下与影子形式的结果相符。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The study of conformal blocks in Toda field theories is central to understanding higher-rank CFTs and their dualities, especially through the AGT correspondence which links 2d CFTs to 4d ${\cal N}=2$ gauge theories. The light asymptotic limit (where conformal dimensions remain finite while $b \to 0$, equivalent to $c \to \infty$) is particularly important for semiclassical analysis and holographic interpretations. However, explicit expressions for $W_n$ conformal blocks beyond $n=2$ are scarce. Thus, deriving a general formula for the one-point torus block in this limit provides crucial insight into the structure of higher-rank blocks and their gauge theory counterparts.

研究Toda场论中的共形块对于理解高秩共形场论（CFT）及其对偶性至关重要，特别是通过AGT对应将二维CFT与四维${\cal N}=2$规范理论联系起来。轻渐近极限（共形维度保持有限而$b \to 0$，等价于$c \to \infty$）在半经典分析和全息诠释中尤为重要。然而，关于$n>2$时$W_n$共形块的显式表达式非常稀少。因此，推导该极限下单点环面块的一般公式，对于理解高秩共形块及其规范理论对应物的结构具有重要意义。

Method: We use the AGT correspondence to map the one-point torus $W_n$ conformal block in $A_{n-1}$ Toda theory to the instanton partition function of four-dimensional ${\cal N}=2^{*}$ $U(n)$ supersymmetric Yang--Mills theory. We then analyze the limit $b \to 0$ with fixed external and internal conformal dimensions (light limit). In this regime, we identify that only specific boxes in each Young diagram—those whose arm lengths satisfy certain conditions—contribute to the bifundamental matter contribution. By isolating these dominant contributions, we derive a closed-form expression for the conformal block as a sum over restricted Young diagrams or equivalently over integer partitions. The derivation relies on the structure of the Nekrasov partition function and the representation theory of $W_n$ algebras.

我们利用AGT对应将$A_{n-1}$ Toda理论中的单点环面$W_n$共形块映射到四维${\cal N}=2^{*}$ $U(n)$超对称杨-米尔斯理论的瞬子配分函数。随后分析$b \to 0$但外部和内部共形维度固定的极限（轻极限）。在此区域中，我们发现只有杨图中满足特定臂长条件的方框才对双基物质项有贡献。通过提取这些主导项，我们推导出共形块的闭式表达式，表现为受限杨图或整数划分上的求和。该推导依赖于Nekrasov配分函数的结构以及$W_n$代数的表示论。

Result: We obtain an explicit formula for the light one-point torus $W_n$ conformal block for arbitrary $n \geq 2$, expressed as a sum over integer partitions $\lambda = (\lambda_1, \lambda_2, \dots)$ with weights determined by the arm-length condition in the Young diagram. Specifically, only boxes with arm length divisible by $n$ contribute in the bifundamental factor, leading to a significant simplification. For $n=2$, the result reduces to the known hypergeometric function $_2F_1$, providing a strong consistency check. For $n=3$, it matches an independent construction from the shadow formalism, confirming its validity in higher-rank cases.

我们得到了适用于任意$n \geq 2$的轻单点环面$W_n$共形块的显式公式，表达为整数划分$\lambda = (\lambda_1, \lambda_2, \dots)$上的求和，权重由杨图中的臂长条件决定。具体而言，仅当方框的臂长可被$n$整除时才对双基因子有贡献，从而导致显著简化。当$n=2$时，结果退化为已知的超几何函数$_2F_1$，构成强有力的自洽性检验；当$n=3$时，结果与影子形式的独立构造一致，验证了其在高秩情形下的有效性。

Conclusion: In the light asymptotic limit, the one-point torus $W_n$ conformal block in $A_{n-1}$ Toda theory simplifies dramatically due to a selection rule on Young diagram box contributions in the corresponding gauge theory instanton sum. This allows us to derive a general closed-form expression valid for all $n \geq 2$. The agreement with known results in the Liouville ($n=2$) and $W_3$ ($n=3$) cases confirms the robustness of our approach. This work provides new tools for studying higher-rank CFTs in the semiclassical regime and opens avenues for exploring integrability and holography in $W_n$ theories.

在轻渐近极限下，由于对应规范理论瞬子和中杨图方框贡献的选择定则，$A_{n-1}$ Toda理论中的单点环面$W_n$共形块显著简化。这使我们能够推导出适用于所有$n \geq 2$的通用闭式表达式。该结果在Liouville（$n=2$）和$W_3$（$n=3$）情形下与已知结果一致，验证了方法的可靠性。本工作为研究高秩共形场论的半经典行为提供了新工具，并为探索$W_n$理论中的可积性与全息对偶开辟了新路径。

Abstract: We study the light asymptotic limit of the one-point torus conformal block in $A_{n-1}$ Toda field theory. Through the AGT correspondence, this problem can be translated into the computation of the instanton partition function of four-dimensional ${\cal N}=2^{\ast}$ $U(n)$ supersymmetric Yang--Mills theory, which we then examine in the limit $b\to 0$ at fixed conformal dimensions. We show that, in this regime, the instanton sum simplifies drastically: for each Young diagram, only boxes with specific arm lengths contribute to the bifundamental factors. Exploiting this property, we derive an explicit representation for the light one-point torus $W_n$ conformal block valid for arbitrary $n\ge 2$.
  As a consistency check, we specialize our construction to the Liouville case $n=2$ and compare it with the previously known hypergeometric representation of the torus block in the light limit. We also discuss the $W_3$ case and its relation to a known alternative representation obtained by the shadow formalism.

</details>


### [30] [Symmetries and Critical Dimensions of Tensionless Branes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01883)
*Bin Chen,Zezhou Hu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: The paper studies the worldsheet symmetry of bosonic brane theories in the tensionless limit, identifying a new algebra $g^{(p)}_\lambda$ governing residual symmetries. By introducing a $bc$ ghost system and computing the BRST charge, the authors perform canonical quantization and compute the quantum anomaly of $g^{(p)}_\lambda$. Requiring anomaly cancellation leads to constraints that determine the critical spacetime dimensions, yielding nontrivial solutions such as $p=3$ in $D=4$ ($\lambda=-3$) and $p=6$ in $D=7$ ($\lambda=3$).

本文研究了无张力极限下玻色膜理论的世界面对称性，发现其剩余对称性由一种新代数$g^{(p)}_\lambda$生成。通过引入$bc$幽灵系统并计算BRST荷，作者在正则量子化框架下计算了该代数的量子反常。要求反常消失后，成功导出了膜理论的临界时空维度，得到了如$\lambda=-3$时$p=3$在$D=4$以及$\lambda=3$时$p=6$在$D=7$等非平庸解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding the quantum consistency of brane theories in the tensionless limit is crucial for exploring fundamental aspects of string/M-theory and higher-dimensional objects. The tensionless limit often reveals enhanced symmetries and may connect to higher-spin theories or holographic dualities. However, gauge fixing typically breaks manifest symmetry, so identifying the residual quantum worldsheet symmetry and ensuring its consistency via anomaly cancellation is essential for a well-defined quantization.

理解无张力极限下膜理论的量子一致性对于探索弦/M理论及高维物体的基本性质至关重要。该极限常展现出增强的对称性，并可能联系到高自旋理论或全息对偶。然而，规范固定通常会破坏显式对称性，因此识别剩余的量子世界面对称性并通过反常抵消确保其一致性，是实现良好量子化的关键步骤。

Method: The authors perform gauge fixing on the worldsheet action of bosonic branes to isolate residual symmetries, which are found to form a new algebra $g^{(p)}_\lambda$. They then introduce a $bc$ ghost system corresponding to this symmetry and construct the total BRST charge. Using canonical quantization, they compute the quantum anomaly (central extension) of the $g^{(p)}_\lambda$ algebra. By setting the anomaly to zero, they derive conditions that fix the spacetime dimension $D$ in terms of the parameters $p$ (brane dimension) and $\lambda$ (a deformation parameter).

作者通过对玻色膜的世界面作用量进行规范固定，分离出剩余对称性，发现其构成新的代数$g^{(p)}_\lambda$。随后引入对应此对称性的$bc$幽灵系统，并构造总的BRST荷。利用正则量子化方法，计算了$g^{(p)}_\lambda$代数的量子反常（中心扩张）。通过令反常为零，推导出以参数$p$（膜维度）和$\lambda$（形变参数）表示的时空维度$D$所必须满足的条件。

Result: The key result is the derivation of the quantum anomaly for the $g^{(p)}_\lambda$ algebra in arbitrary $p$, $\lambda$, and spacetime dimension $D$. Imposing anomaly cancellation yields specific critical dimensions. Notably, nontrivial solutions include: a 3-brane ($p=3$) in $D=4$ when $\lambda = -3$, and a 6-brane ($p=6$) in $D=7$ when $\lambda = 3$. These results suggest novel critical behaviors distinct from standard string theory ($p=1$).

主要结果是在任意$p$、$\lambda$和时空维度$D$下导出了$g^{(p)}_\lambda$代数的量子反常表达式。要求反常抵消后得到具体的临界维度。特别是，发现了非平庸解：当$\lambda = -3$时，在$D=4$中的3膜（$p=3$）；当$\lambda = 3$时，在$D=7$中的6膜（$p=6$）。这些结果表明，与标准弦理论（$p=1$）不同，高维膜可能存在新颖的临界行为。

Conclusion: The paper concludes that consistent quantization of tensionless bosonic branes requires the cancellation of anomalies in the residual $g^{(p)}_\lambda$ symmetry algebra. This condition determines the critical spacetime dimension, leading to new solutions beyond conventional string theory. The existence of such solutions at finite $p > 1$ suggests that higher-dimensional branes can have consistent quantum descriptions under specific symmetry constraints, opening potential avenues for exploring exotic conformal field theories and their role in quantum gravity.

论文结论是：无张力玻色膜的一致量子化要求剩余对称性代数$g^{(p)}_\lambda$的反常必须抵消。这一条件决定了临界时空维度，并导致超出传统弦理论的新解。这类在有限$p > 1$下存在的解表明，在特定对称性约束下，高维膜可以具有自洽的量子描述，为探索奇异共形场论及其在量子引力中的作用提供了潜在方向。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the worldsheet symmetry of bosonic brane theories and its quantum consistency in the tensionless limit. We find that the residual worldsheet symmetry after specific gauge fixing is generated by a novel algebra, denoted as $g^{(p)}_λ$. To achieve full quantization of the tensionless brane, we introduce a $bc$ ghost system and derive the overall BRST charge. Moreover, we calculate the quantum anomaly of the $g^{(p)}_λ$ algebra for general parameters $p$ and $λ$ in the framework of canonical quantization. After demanding that this quantum anomaly vanishes, we successfully derive the critical dimensions of the bosonic brane theories. Especially, we obtain nontrivial solutions: $p=3$ in $D=4$ spacetime dimensions when $λ=-3$ and $p=6$ in $D=7$ spacetime dimensions when $λ=3$.
