### [31] [Effective Field Theory for Superconducting Phase Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02133)
*Yanyan Bu,Zexin Yang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We develop an effective field theory (EFT) for s-wave superconducting phase transitions using the Schwinger-Keldysh formalism, incorporating dissipation and fluctuations systematically. The EFT includes higher-order operators and reproduces Ginzburg-Landau dynamics upon truncation. Near the critical point, the Higgs mode is overdamped and diffusive, while phase fluctuations are absorbed via the Higgs mechanism. Holographic validation confirms the EFT structure and reveals complex relaxation indicative of oscillatory, strongly coupled dynamics.

我们利用Schwinger-Keldysh形式论构建了s波超导相变的有效场论（EFT），系统地纳入了耗散与涨落。该EFT包含高阶算符，截断后可还原Ginzburg-Landau动力学。在临界点附近，Higgs模表现为过阻尼扩散模式，而相位涨落通过Higgs机制被规范场吸收。全息验证确认了EFT结构，并揭示出表明强耦合系统振荡动力学的复数弛豫参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Understanding real-time non-equilibrium dynamics near the superconducting critical point requires a systematic framework that consistently incorporates fluctuations, dissipation, and gauge symmetry. Traditional Ginzburg-Landau theory lacks a microscopic foundation for dynamical processes; thus, a quantum effective field theory approach is needed to go beyond phenomenology and include higher-order corrections and real-time evolution.

理解超导临界点附近的实时非平衡动力学需要一个系统框架，以一致地纳入涨落、耗散和规范对称性。传统的Ginzburg-Landau理论缺乏动力学过程的微观基础，因此需要量子有效场论方法超越唯象描述，包含高阶修正和实时演化。

Method: We employ the Schwinger-Keldysh closed-time-path formalism to construct a gauge-invariant effective action for a complex scalar order parameter and electromagnetic gauge field. The action is organized via derivative and power counting, respecting the underlying symmetries, including $U(1)$ gauge invariance and time-reversal symmetry. Higher-order terms involving additional dynamical fields and higher time derivatives are included. The framework is validated using holographic duality via the holographic Schwinger-Keldysh technique in a gravity dual model of a superconductor.

我们采用Schwinger-Keldysh闭时路径形式论，为复标量序参量和电磁规范场构建规范不变的有效作用量。该作用量通过导数和幂次计数组织，保持底层对称性（包括$U(1)$规范不变性和时间反演对称性）。我们包含了涉及额外动力学场和高阶时间导数的高阶项。通过全息对偶，在超导体引力对偶模型中使用全息Schwinger-Keldysh技术对该框架进行验证。

Result: The effective field theory successfully reproduces the time-dependent Ginzburg-Landau equations when truncated at leading order. Spontaneous breaking of $U(1)$ gauge symmetry occurs below the critical temperature due to order parameter condensation. The Higgs mode is found to be an overdamped diffusive excitation near the critical point, while the Goldstone mode is eaten by the gauge field via the Higgs mechanism. Holographic computation confirms the structure of the EFT and yields complex-valued Wilsonian coefficients, indicating oscillatory relaxation dynamics characteristic of strong coupling.

该有效场论在领头阶截断时成功还原了含时Ginzburg-Landau方程。低于临界温度时，由于序参量凝聚，$U(1)$规范对称性发生自发破缺。在临界点附近，Higgs模表现为过阻尼扩散激发，而Goldstone模通过Higgs机制被规范场吸收。全息计算确认了EFT的结构，并得到复数值的Wilson系数，表明具有强耦合特征的振荡弛豫动力学。

Conclusion: The Schwinger-Keldysh EFT provides a robust and systematic framework for studying real-time dynamics of superconducting phase transitions, naturally incorporating dissipation, fluctuations, and gauge symmetry. The inclusion of higher-order terms enables a deeper understanding of critical dynamics, while holographic duality offers non-perturbative validation and reveals novel features such as complex relaxation parameters, suggesting rich real-time behavior in strongly coupled superconductors.

Schwinger-Keldysh EFT为研究超导相变的实时动力学提供了稳健且系统的框架，自然地纳入了耗散、涨落和规范对称性。高阶项的引入深化了对临界动力学的理解，而全息对偶提供了非微扰验证，并揭示了复数弛豫参数等新特征，表明强耦合超导体中存在丰富的实时行为。

Abstract: Employing the Schwinger-Keldysh formalism, we formulate an effective field theory for s-wave superconducting phase transition, where the dynamical variables consist of electromagnetic gauge field and a complex scalar order parameter. Symmetry-constrained effective action allows systematic handling of dissipations and fluctuations. In particular, we explore the physical implications of higher-order terms, including those involving additional dynamical fields as well as higher time derivatives, for the real-time dynamics near the superconducting critical point. When appropriately truncated, the effective field theory reproduces the phenomenological Ginzburg-Landau equations. Upon crossing the critical temperature into the low-temperature phase, the electromagnetic gauge symmetry undergoes spontaneous breaking induced by the condensate of the order parameter. Collective excitation analysis reveals that the Higgs mode behaves as an overdamped diffusive mode near the critical point, while the phase fluctuation is absorbed into the gauge field via the Higgs mechanism. Via the holographic Schwinger-Keldysh technique, rigorous validation in a holographic superconductor confirms the structure of the effective action and quantifies the Wilsonian coefficients. The holographic results uncover a complex relaxation parameter that is indicative of oscillatory dynamics, a hallmark of strongly coupled systems.

</details>


### [32] [Gravitational null rays: Covariant Quantization and the Dressing Time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02228)
*Laurent Freidel,Josh Kirklin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We present a fully gauge-invariant quantization of gravitational null ray segments using a quantum reference frame (QRF) constructed from the gravitational field itself, introducing covariant normal ordering to restore diffeomorphism covariance. The algebra of gauge-invariant observables forms a Virasoro crossed product, and the quantum dressing map induces a deformed product akin to a quantized Dirac bracket. Anomalies are canceled via classical deformation, and the physical Hilbert space allows a Page-Wootters reduction, with non-ideal temporal coherence governed by the Teo-Takhtajan energy.

本文提出了一种基于引力场自身构建的量子参考系（QRF）对引力零射线段进行完全规范不变量子化的方法，引入协变正规序以恢复微分同胚协变性。规范不变观测量的代数具有Virasoro交叉积结构，量子dressing映射在规范固定算符上诱导出一种类似于量子化Dirac括号的变形乘积。通过对经典层面进行形变消除反常，从而在量子层面剔除所有虚假自由度。物理希尔伯特空间允许Page-Wootters约化到dressing时间视角，且该时间是非理想的，其不同相干态之间的非零重叠由Teo-Takhtajan能量（即Virasoro余伴随轨道的Kähler势）决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traditional approaches to quantum gravity often rely on fixed background structures or partial gauge fixings that break full diffeomorphism invariance. This work aims to overcome such limitations by constructing a quantum reference frame (QRF) directly from the dynamical gravitational field on a null ray, preserving the complete group of diffeomorphisms along the ray. The motivation is to achieve a background-independent, fully gauge-invariant quantization that does not truncate the symmetry group to a subgroup, thus capturing the full structure of gravitational constraints at the quantum level.

传统量子引力方法通常依赖固定背景结构或部分规范固定，破坏了完整的微分同胚不变性。本研究旨在通过直接从零射线上动力学引力场构造量子参考系（QRF），克服这些限制，保持沿射线的完整微分同胚群不变性。目标是实现背景无关且完全规范不变的量子化，不将对称群截断为子群，从而在量子层面完整捕捉引力约束的结构。

Method: We employ a gravitational degree of freedom as a quantum reference frame (QRF), specifically using the 'dressing time'—a relational observable defined through gauge-invariant correlations—to parametrize evolution. We introduce covariant normal ordering, a QRF-dependent but background-independent renormalization scheme that ensures diffeomorphism covariance at the quantum level. Using this, we construct a quantum dressing map that maps gauge-fixed operators to gauge-invariant observables, forming a Virasoro crossed product algebra. Anomalies in unitary representations are canceled by introducing a classical deformation prior to quantization. A Page-Wootters reduction is applied to recover dynamics relative to the dressing time, whose coherence properties are analyzed via overlaps of coherent states governed by the Teo-Takhtajan energy.

我们采用引力自由度作为量子参考系（QRF），具体使用'dressing时间'——通过规范不变关联定义的关系型可观测量——来参数化演化过程。我们引入协变正规序，这是一种依赖QRF但背景无关的重整化方案，确保量子层面的微分同胚协变性。基于此，我们构建了一个量子dressing映射，将规范固定算符映射到形成Virasoro交叉积代数的规范不变观测量。通过在量子化前引入经典形变来消除幺正表示中的反常。应用Page-Wootters约化以恢复相对于dressing时间的动力学，并通过由Teo-Takhtajan能量支配的相干态重叠分析该时间的相干性质。

Result: The algebra of gauge-invariant observables is shown to carry the structure of a Virasoro crossed product, indicating a deep connection between gravitational edge modes and two-dimensional conformal symmetry. The quantum dressing map induces a deformed product on operators, which corresponds to the quantization of the Dirac bracket and modifies quantum fluctuations. Covariant normal ordering restores diffeomorphism covariance despite regularization. By incorporating a classical deformation, anomalies in the physical Hilbert space representation are canceled, yielding a consistent quantum theory free of spurious degrees of freedom. The Page-Wootters reduction reveals that the dressing time is non-ideal: distinct coherent states have non-vanishing overlaps determined by the Teo-Takhtajan energy, reflecting intrinsic quantum uncertainty in time.

规范不变观测量的代数被证明具有Virasoro交叉积结构，揭示了引力边缘模与二维共形对称性之间的深刻联系。量子dressing映射在算符上诱导出变形乘积，对应于Dirac括号的量子化并改变量子涨落。尽管存在正则化，协变正规序仍恢复了微分同胚协变性。通过引入经典形变，物理希尔伯特空间表示中的反常被消除，得到一个无虚假自由度的一致量子理论。Page-Wootters约化显示dressing时间是非理想的：不同的相干态具有由Teo-Takhtajan能量决定的非零重叠，反映了时间上的内在量子不确定性。

Conclusion: By using a gravitational-field-based quantum reference frame and covariant normal ordering, we achieve a fully gauge-invariant and background-independent quantization of null ray segments. The resulting gauge-invariant algebra exhibits Virasoro symmetry, and the quantum dressing procedure provides a precise realization of relational quantum dynamics. The necessity of classical deformation to cancel anomalies suggests a feedback mechanism from quantum consistency conditions to classical structure. The non-ideality of the dressing time, quantified by the Teo-Takhtajan energy, implies fundamental limitations on time measurement in quantum gravity.

通过使用基于引力场的量子参考系和协变正规序，我们实现了对零射线段的完全规范不变且背景无关的量子化。所得到的规范不变代数展现出Virasoro对称性，量子dressing程序为关系型量子动力学提供了精确实现。为消除反常而必需的经典形变表明，量子一致性条件对经典结构存在反馈机制。由Teo-Takhtajan能量量化的dressing时间的非理想性，暗示了量子引力中时间测量的基本限制。

Abstract: We quantize the degrees of freedom on a gravitational null ray segment in a fully gauge-invariant manner by using the dressing time as a quantum reference frame (QRF). Our work goes beyond previous models in that the QRF we employ is made out of the gravitational field itself, and accounts for the full group of diffeomorphisms along the ray, not just a locally compact subgroup. The key tool we introduce is covariant normal ordering, a QRF-dependent but background-independent renormalization prescription that restores diffeomorphism covariance at the quantum level. This enables the definition of a quantum dressing map whose image is the algebra of gauge-invariant observables. We find that this algebra carries the structure of a Virasoro crossed product, and that the dressing map induces a deformed product on gauge-fixed operators which can be understood as a quantization of the Dirac bracket, with consequences for the fluctuations of observables. We explain how to cancel anomalies in the physical Hilbert space representation of the gauge-invariant algebra by including a deformation at the classical level, thereby eliminating all spurious degrees of freedom at the quantum level. The physical Hilbert space admits a Page-Wootters reduction map to the perspective of the dressing time, and we show that the dressing time is non-ideal in the sense that its distinct coherent states have non-vanishing overlaps governed by the Teo-Takhtajan energy, i.e. the Kähler potential for Virasoro coadjoint orbits.

</details>


### [33] [Recursive relations from diffeomorphism in the Randall-Sundrum model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02294)
*Haiying Cai,Giacomo Cacciapaglia*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We derive nonlinear diffeomorphism transformation rules for metric perturbations in the unitary gauge within warped extra-dimensional models, and show that diffeomorphism acts as an off-shell symmetry generating recursive relations in the effective Lagrangian expansion.

我们推导了在具有弯曲额外维模型的幺正规范下度规扰动的非线性微分同胚变换规则，并表明微分同胚作为离壳对称性，会在有效拉格朗日量展开中产生递归关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Diffeomorphism invariance is a fundamental symmetry in gravitational theories, including those with extra dimensions. Understanding its nonlinear realization in the unitary gauge is crucial for consistently constructing the effective field theory (EFT) of gravity in warped spacetimes such as Randall-Sundrum (RS) models.

微分同胚不变性是引力理论（包括含额外维的理论）中的基本对称性。理解其在幺正规范下的非线性实现对于在如Randall-Sundrum（RS）模型等弯曲时空背景下一致构建引力的有效场论（EFT）至关重要。

Method: We analyze the transformation properties of metric perturbations under diffeomorphisms in a warped extra-dimensional setup, focusing on the unitary gauge where the Goldstone modes are set to zero. By requiring off-shell diffeomorphism invariance, we derive recursive relations between coefficients at different orders in the expansion of the effective Lagrangian $\mathcal{L}_\text{eff}$.

我们在具有弯曲额外维的设定中分析度规扰动在微分同胚下的变换性质，重点关注幺正规范（Goldstone模式被设为零）。通过要求离壳微分同胚不变性，我们推导出有效拉格朗日量$\mathcal{L}_\text{eff}$展开中不同阶次系数之间的递归关系。

Result: We obtain explicit nonlinear transformation rules for the metric perturbations and establish a hierarchy of recursive Ward identities in the effective Lagrangian. These relations ensure consistency across orders in perturbation theory and constrain the allowed operators in the EFT. When applied to the Randall-Sundrum model with hard branes, these symmetries restrict the form of boundary-localized terms.

我们得到了度规扰动的显式非线性变换规则，并在有效拉格朗日量中建立了递归Ward恒等式的层级结构。这些关系确保了微扰论各阶之间的一致性，并限制了EFT中允许的算符形式。当应用于具有硬膜的Randall-Sundrum模型时，这些对称性限制了边界局域项的形式。

Conclusion: Diffeomorphism invariance in warped extra dimensions, even when realized nonlinearly in the unitary gauge, imposes powerful constraints on the structure of the effective theory through recursive relations. This provides a systematic way to construct consistent EFTs beyond linear order.

在弯曲额外维中，即使在幺正规范下以非线性方式实现，微分同胚不变性仍通过递归关系对有效理论的结构施加强有力的约束。这为在线性阶以上系统构建一致的EFT提供了途径。

Abstract: Models of gravity in warped extra dimensions enjoy invariance under diffeomorphism. We derive the nonlinear transformation rules for the metric perturbations in the unitary gauge. As an off-shell symmetry, the main consequence of diffeomorphism is a set of recursive relations linking consecutive orders in the field expansion of the effective Lagrangian. The physical consequences are briefly explored for the Randall-Sundrum model with hard branes.

</details>


### [34] [Topological Effects in Neural Network Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02313)
*Christian Ferko,James Halverson,Vishnu Jejjala,Brandon Robinson*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: We extend neural network field theory to include topological parameters, enabling the description of topological quantum numbers and recovering key phenomena such as the Berezinskii--Kosterlitz--Thouless (BKT) transition and T-duality in bosonic string theory, including vortex proliferation, Buscher rules, current algebra enhancement, and T-fold transitions.

我们将神经网络场论扩展以包含拓扑参数，从而能够描述拓扑量子数，并重现了Berezinskii--Kosterlitz--Thouless (BKT) 相变以及玻色弦理论中的T对偶性，包括涡旋增殖、Buscher规则、流代数在自对偶半径处的增强以及T-折叠（T-fold）转移函数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Neural network field theory provides a novel framework for defining quantum field theories through statistical ensembles of neural networks. However, it originally lacked the ability to describe topological effects, which are crucial in many physical systems such as low-dimensional condensed matter and string theory. Our goal is to incorporate topological structure—specifically discrete topological quantum numbers—into this framework to enable the study of non-perturbative and dual phenomena like the BKT transition and T-duality.

神经网络场论通过神经网络的统计系综为定义量子场论提供了新框架。然而，它最初缺乏描述拓扑效应的能力，而这些效应在许多物理系统（如低维凝聚态和弦理论）中至关重要。我们的目标是将拓扑结构——特别是离散的拓扑量子数——纳入该框架，以研究BKT相变和T对偶等非微扰和对偶现象。

Method: We generalize neural network field theory by introducing discrete parameters into the parameter space of the network that label topological sectors, such as winding numbers or vortex charges. The ensemble average includes both continuous weights and discrete labels, allowing for configurations with non-trivial topology. We apply this construction to 2D scalar field theories on $S^1$ and toroidal target spaces, simulating the path integral via sampling over network parameters. Topological susceptibility, vortex correlation functions, and duality-invariant observables are computed numerically.

我们通过在网络参数空间中引入标记拓扑扇区（如缠绕数或涡旋电荷）的离散参数，推广了神经网络场论。系综平均同时包含连续权重和离散标签，允许具有非平凡拓扑的构型存在。我们将此构造应用于$S^1$和环面目标空间上的二维标量场论，通过在网络参数上采样来模拟路径积分。拓扑磁化率、涡旋关联函数和对偶不变观测量被数值计算。

Result: We successfully recover the Berezinskii--Kosterlitz--Thouless transition: at low temperatures, spin-wave behavior dominates with algebraic correlations; above a critical temperature, vortices proliferate and destroy long-range order. We also confirm T-duality in the bosonic string: the theory is invariant under exchange of momentum and winding modes on $S^1$, sigma model couplings transform according to Buscher rules on toroidal backgrounds, current algebra enhances at the self-dual radius ($R = \sqrt{\alpha'}$), and we observe transition functions characteristic of T-folds—non-geometric backgrounds arising from T-duality transformations.

我们成功重现了Berezinskii--Kosterlitz--Thouless相变：在低温下，自旋波主导并表现出代数关联；在高于临界温度时，涡旋增殖并破坏长程序。我们还验证了玻色弦中的T对偶性：理论在$S^1$上动量与缠绕模式交换下不变，sigma模型耦合在环面背景下按Buscher规则变换，在自对偶半径（$R = \sqrt{\alpha'}$）处流代数发生增强，并观察到表征T-折叠（T-folds）的转移函数——即由T对偶变换产生的非几何背景。

Conclusion: By incorporating discrete topological parameters into neural network field theory, we extend its applicability to topologically non-trivial sectors and dualities. This enables the first-principles simulation of phenomena such as the BKT transition and stringy T-duality directly from a neural ensemble, opening a pathway toward machine-learning-based exploration of non-perturbative and geometric structures in quantum field theory and string theory.

通过将离散拓扑参数纳入神经网络场论，我们将其适用性扩展到拓扑非平凡扇区和对偶性。这使得从神经网络系综出发首次直接模拟BKT相变和弦论T对偶成为可能，为基于机器学习探索量子场论和弦论中的非微扰与几何结构开辟了道路。

Abstract: Neural network field theory formulates field theory as a statistical ensemble of fields defined by a network architecture and a density on its parameters. We extend the construction to topological settings via the inclusion of discrete parameters that label the topological quantum number. We recover the Berezinskii--Kosterlitz--Thouless transition, including the spin-wave critical line and the proliferation of vortices at high temperatures. We also verify the T-duality of the bosonic string, showing invariance under the exchange of momentum and winding on $S^1$, the transformation of the sigma model couplings according to the Buscher rules on constant toroidal backgrounds, the enhancement of the current algebra at self-dual radius, and non-geometric T-fold transition functions.

</details>

### [35] [Euclid preparation. Non-Gaussianity of 2-pt statistics likelihood: Parameter inference with a non-Gaussian likelihood in Fourier and configuration space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01309)
*Euclid Collaboration,S. Gouyou Beauchamps,J. Bel,P. Baratta,C. Carbone,B. Altieri,S. Andreon,N. Auricchio,C. Baccigalupi,M. Baldi,S. Bardelli,P. Battaglia,F. Bernardeau,A. Biviano,E. Branchini,M. Marggraf,K. Markovic,M. Martinelli,N. Martinet,F. Marulli,R. J. Massey,E. Medinaceli,S. Mei,M. Meneghetti,E. Merlin,G. Meylan,A. Mora,M. Moresco,L. Moscardini,R. Nakajima,C. Neissner,S. -M. Niemi,C. Sakr,A. G. Sánchez,D. Sapone,B. Sartoris,P. Schneider,A. Secroun,G. Seidel,E. Sihvola,P. Simon,C. Sirignano,G. Sirri,P. Tallada-Crespí,A. N. Taylor,I. Tereno,N. Tessore,S. Toft,R. Toledo-Moreo,F. Torradeflot,I. Tutusaus,J. Valiviita,T. Vassallo,G. Verdoes Kleijn,A. Veropalumbo,Y. Wang,J. Weller,G. Zamorani,E. Zucca,M. Ballardini,A. Boucaud,E. Bozzo,C. Burigana,R. Cabanac,M. Calabrese,A. Cappi,T. Castro,J. A. Escartin Vigo,L. Gabarra,J. García-Bellido,J. Macias-Perez,R. Maoli,N. Mauri,R. B. Metcalf,P. Monaco,A. A. Nucita,A. Pezzotta,M. Pöntinen,I. Risso,V. Scottez,M. Sereno,M. Tenti,M. Tucci,M. Viel,M. Wiesmann,Y. Akrami,I. T. Andika,S. Anselmi,M. Archidiacono,F. Atrio-Barandela,L. Bazzanini,D. Bertacca,M. Bethermin,F. Beutler,A. Blanchard,L. Blot,M. Bonici,M. L. Brown,S. Bruton,A. Calabro,B. Camacho Quevedo,F. Caro,C. S. Carvalho,F. Cogato,A. R. Cooray,S. Davini,F. De Paolis,G. Desprez,A. Díaz-Sánchez,S. Di Domizio,J. M. Diego,V. Duret,M. Y. Elkhashab,A. Enia,Y. Lesgourgues,T. I. Liaudat,S. J. Liu,M. Magliocchetti,F. Mannucci,C. J. A. P. Martins,L. Maurin,M. Miluzio,C. Moretti,G. Morgante,C. Murray,S. Nadathur,K. Naidoo,A. Navarro-Alsina,S. Nesseris,L. Pagano,D. Paoletti,F. Passalacqua,K. Paterson,L. Patrizii,C. Pattison,R. Paviot,A. Pisani,D. Potter,G. W. Pratt,S. Quai,M. Radovich,W. Roster,S. Sacquegna,M. Sahlén,D. B. Sanders,A. Schneider,D. Sciotti,E. Sellentin,L. C. Smith,K. Tanidis,C. Tao,F. Tarsitano,G. Testera,R. Teyssier,S. Tosi,A. Troja,A. Venhola,D. Vergani,F. Vernizzi,G. Verza,P. Vielzeuf,S. Vinciguerra,N. A. Walton,A. H. Wright*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The study investigates the impact of non-Gaussianity in cosmological parameter inference using an Edgeworth expansion of the likelihood, incorporating the full skewness tensor from 1-point, 2-point, and 3-point correlators. By transforming to a basis where the precision matrix is diagonalized (effectively whitened), the off-diagonal components of the skewness tensor vanish, and the diagonal elements align with expectations for a Gaussian field. Using over 10,000 \Euclid-like mock catalogs, it is shown that including only diagonal skewness suffices, while the full tensor adds noise without improving accuracy. Cosmological constraints remain stable across likelihood models, with less than 5% variation in figure of merit, regardless of survey geometry, scale cuts, or choice of 2-point statistic (power spectrum or correlation function). No detectable excess skewness is found on intermediate scales due to significant shot noise in the \Euclid spectroscopic sample. Thus, the Gaussian likelihood assumption is validated as robust for \Euclid 2-point analyses in both Fourier and configuration space.

该研究通过Edgeworth展开对宇宙学参数推断中的非高斯性影响进行了分析，包含来自1点、2点和3点关联函数的完整偏度张量。通过变换到精度矩阵被对角化（即白化）的基中，偏度张量的非对角项消失，而对角项与高斯场预期一致。利用超过10,000个\Euclid类模拟样本发现，仅包含对角偏度已足够，完整张量反而引入噪声而不提升精度。宇宙学约束在不同似然模型下保持稳定，优度变化小于5%，且不受巡天几何、尺度截断或两点统计量（功率谱或相关函数）选择的影响。由于\Euclid光谱样本的散粒噪声水平，在中间尺度上未检测到显著超出的偏度。因此，高斯似然假设被证实对于\Euclid在傅里叶空间和组态空间的两点统计分析是稳健的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: In cosmological parameter inference, the assumption of a Gaussian likelihood is widely used but may not hold when higher-order statistics induce significant non-Gaussian features in the data distribution. The skewness — captured by the three-point correlation function and its projections into the likelihood — can in principle bias parameter constraints. With upcoming surveys like \Euclid aiming for percent-level precision, it is critical to assess whether deviations from Gaussianity, particularly through the full skewness tensor (including 1-point, 2-point, and 3-point correlators), must be modelled to avoid biased or over-optimistic uncertainties. This work aims to rigorously test the validity of the Gaussian likelihood assumption by incorporating a complete Edgeworth expansion and evaluating its impact on parameter inference using realistic mocks.

在宇宙学参数推断中，高斯基尼假设被广泛使用，但当高阶统计导致数据分布出现显著非高斯特征时，该假设可能不成立。偏度——由三点关联函数及其在似然中的投影所捕获——原则上可能使参数约束产生偏差。随着\Euclid等下一代巡天追求百分比精度，评估偏离高斯性的程度（特别是通过完整的偏度张量，包括1点、2点和3点关联函数）是否必须建模以避免有偏或过于乐观的不确定性变得至关重要。本工作旨在通过引入完整的Edgeworth展开并利用真实模拟样本评估其对参数推断的影响，严格检验高斯基尼假设的有效性。

Method: The authors employ an Edgeworth expansion of the likelihood function to incorporate non-Gaussianity via the full skewness tensor $ S_{ijk} = \langle x_i x_j x_k \rangle $, constructed from 1-point, 2-point, and 3-point correlators of the data vector $ x $. To simplify computation, they perform a linear transformation to a 'whitened' basis where the precision matrix $ \mathbf{\Psi} = \mathbf{C}^{-1} $ becomes the identity, i.e., $ \tilde{x} = \mathbf{\Psi}^{1/2} x $. In this basis, the structure of the skewness tensor simplifies significantly. They compute the skewness tensor from $ 10\,000 $ \Euclid large-scale structure mocks based on realistic galaxy catalogues mimicking the expected properties of \Euclid's spectroscopic sample. Parameter inference is then performed using Monte Carlo Markov Chains (MCMC) under different likelihood assumptions: Gaussian, diagonal-only skewness, and full skewness tensor. The stability of cosmological constraints and figure of merit (FoM) are compared across these models and under variations in survey volume, geometry, scale cuts, and use of power spectrum vs. correlation function.

作者采用似然函数的Edgeworth展开，通过完整的偏度张量$ S_{ijk} = \langle x_i x_j x_k \rangle $引入非高斯性，该张量由数据向量$ x $的1点、2点和3点关联函数构建。为简化计算，他们执行线性变换至“白化”基，使得精度矩阵$ \mathbf{\Psi} = \mathbf{C}^{-1} $变为单位阵，即$ \tilde{x} = \mathbf{\Psi}^{1/2} x $。在此基中，偏度张量的结构显著简化。他们基于10,000个\Euclid大尺度结构模拟样本（模拟\Euclid光谱样本的星系目录特性）计算偏度张量。随后，在不同似然假设下（高斯、仅对角偏度、完整偏度张量），使用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）进行参数推断，并比较宇宙学约束稳定性及优度指标（FoM）在巡天体积、几何形状、尺度截断以及功率谱与相关函数之间的差异。

Result: In the whitened basis, the off-diagonal elements of the skewness tensor are consistent with zero, and the diagonal elements match theoretical expectations for a Gaussian random field. Including only the diagonal part of the skewness in the likelihood improves numerical stability without degrading performance, whereas including the full skewness tensor introduces noise without enhancing inference accuracy. The cosmological parameter constraints — including their uncertainties and correlations — are nearly identical whether using a Gaussian likelihood or the full Edgeworth-expanded likelihood, with differences in the figure of merit below $ 5\% $. These results are robust against changes in survey volume, geometry, scale cuts, and choice of 2-point statistic (monopole of the power spectrum or correlation function). Analysis of $ 10\,000 $ \Euclid-like mocks shows no statistically significant excess skewness on intermediate scales, primarily due to the high level of shot noise expected in the \Euclid spectroscopic sample.

在白化基中，偏度张量的非对角元素与零一致，对角元素与高斯随机场的理论预期相符。在似然中仅包含偏度对角部分即可提高数值稳定性而不降低性能，而包含完整偏度张量则引入噪声且不提升推断精度。无论是使用高斯基尼还是完整的Edgeworth展开似然，宇宙学参数约束（包括其不确定性与相关性）几乎完全相同，优度差异低于$ 5\% $。这些结果对巡天体积、几何形状、尺度截断以及两点统计量（功率谱单极矩或相关函数）的选择具有鲁棒性。对10,000个\Euclid类模拟的分析表明，在中间尺度上未检测到统计显著的额外偏度，主要归因于\Euclid光谱样本预期的高水平散粒噪声。

Conclusion: The Gaussian likelihood assumption is sufficiently accurate for cosmological parameter inference from \Euclid 2-point statistics, both in Fourier space (power spectrum) and configuration space (correlation function). The expected level of non-Gaussianity, as quantified by the skewness tensor, does not significantly affect parameter constraints due to the dominance of shot noise on intermediate scales. Simplified likelihood models that neglect off-diagonal skewness — or even all skewness — are justified for current and near-future analyses. This validates the standard practice in large-scale structure analyses and supports the robustness of upcoming \Euclid cosmological results.

高斯似然假设对于\Euclid两点统计（无论是在傅里叶空间的功率谱还是组态空间的相关函数）的宇宙学参数推断已足够精确。由偏度张量量化的非高斯性水平，由于中间尺度上散粒噪声占主导，对参数约束无显著影响。忽略非对角偏度甚至全部偏度的简化似然模型在当前及近期未来的分析中是合理的。这验证了大尺度结构分析中的标准做法，并支持即将发布的\Euclid宇宙学结果的稳健性。

Abstract: In this work we account for this skewness in parameter inference by modelling the likelihood through an Edgeworth expansion which involves the complete skewness tensor, composed of 1-point, 2-point, and 3-point correlators. To simplify the calculations of this expansion we perform a change of basis which reduces the precision matrix to the identity. In this basis, the off-diagonal elements of the skewness tensor are consistent with zero, while the amplitude of its diagonal match the level expected for a Gaussian underlying field. We perform parameter inference with this likelihood model and find that including only the diagonal part of the skewness is sufficient, while incorporating the full skewness tensor injects noise without improving accuracy. Despite the estimated excess skewness in the original basis, the cosmological constraints remain effectively unchanged when adopting a Gaussian likelihood or considering the more complete Edgeworth expansion, with variations in the figure of merit of cosmological parameters between the two cases below $5\%$. This result remains unchanged against variations of the survey volume and geometry, scale-cut, and 2-point statistic (power spectrum or correlation function). Using $10\, 000$ cloned \Euclid large mocks based on realistic galaxy catalogues with characteristics close to future \Euclid data, we find no detectable excess skewness on intermediate scales, due to the level of shot noise expected for the \Euclid spectroscopic sample. We conclude that the Gaussian likelihood assumption is robust for \Euclid 2-point statistics analyses in both Fourier and configuration space.

</details>


### [36] [The Cosmic Web in the DESI Early Data Release: A Probabilistic Environment Catalog](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01456)
*Diana C. Zapata-Zuluaga,Sofía Guevara-Montoya,Valeria Torres-Gomez,Juliana Hernandez,Jaime E. Forero-Romero*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We present the first public cosmic-web environment catalog from DESI Early Data Release, using the ASTRA algorithm to classify galaxies into voids, sheets, filaments, and knots without reconstructing a density field. The method is validated against GAMA and other surveys, showing consistent environmental trends in galaxy properties. All data and code are publicly released.

我们基于DESI早期数据发布（EDR）发布了首个公开的宇宙网环境星表，使用ASTRA算法将星系分类为洞穴（void）、片状结构（sheet）、纤维结构（filament）和节点（knot），无需重构连续密度场。该方法经GAMA等巡天验证，星系属性的环境依赖性一致。所有数据与开源代码均已公开。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Cosmic web environments play a crucial role in galaxy formation and evolution, yet robust, observationally driven classifications on large-scale surveys like DESI have been lacking. Existing methods often rely on reconstructed density fields or simulations, limiting their applicability to real data. We aim to provide a reliable, stochastic topological classification directly applicable to discrete survey data.

宇宙网环境在星系形成与演化中起关键作用，但在DESI等大规模巡天中缺乏基于观测的稳健分类方法。现有方法常依赖密度场重构或模拟，限制了其在实际数据中的应用。我们旨在为离散巡天数据提供一种可靠的随机拓扑分类方法。

Method: We apply ASTRA (Algorithm for Stochastic Topological RAnking), a graph-based topological classifier that uses observed galaxy positions and matched random catalogs to assign each object to one of four cosmic web environments—void, sheet, filament, knot—based on local connectivity and spatial statistics. No continuous density field reconstruction is required. The method is applied to four DESI tracers (BGS, LRG, ELG, QSO) across 20 EDR rosettes (~175 deg²), with 100 realizations per tracer-zone pair to compute membership probabilities and classification entropies. Classification thresholds are calibrated using BGS to match volume-filling fractions from GAMA.

我们采用ASTRA（随机拓扑排序算法），一种基于图论的拓扑分类器，利用观测到的星系位置和匹配的随机样本，根据局部连通性和空间统计量将每个天体分类为四种宇宙网环境之一：洞穴（void）、片状结构（sheet）、纤维结构（filament）、节点（knot），无需重构连续密度场。该方法应用于DESI的四类示踪物（BGS、LRG、ELG、QSO）在20个EDR花瓣区域（约175平方度），每对示踪物-区域运行100次以计算成员概率和分类熵。使用BGS作为锚定，校准分类阈值以匹配GAMA报告的体积填充分数。

Result: We obtain robust cosmic web classifications across all DESI extragalactic tracers, with physically consistent morphology (e.g., increasing density from voids to knots). For BGS, the web-type fractions and star formation trends (e.g., lower sSFR in denser environments) match those in GAMA, COSMOS, and SDSS. Normalized mutual information analysis reveals environment-dependent statistical associations between galaxy color, stellar mass, and sSFR, indicating that environment modulates the galaxy property covariance structure.

我们在所有DESI河外示踪物中获得了稳健的宇宙网分类，呈现出物理上一致的形态（例如，从洞穴到节点密度递增）。对于BGS，宇宙网类型比例及恒星形成趋势（如致密环境中sSFR更低）与GAMA、COSMOS和SDSS结果一致。归一化互信息分析揭示了星系颜色、恒星质量与sSFR之间存在环境依赖的统计关联，表明环境调制了星系属性协方差结构。

Conclusion: ASTRA enables robust, simulation-free cosmic web classification directly on observational datasets like DESI. The resulting catalog provides a new baseline for studying galaxy evolution in different large-scale environments. The public release of both data and pipeline supports reproducibility and future applications in cosmology and astrophysics.

ASTRA实现了无需模拟的宇宙网分类，可直接应用于DESI等观测数据集。生成的星表为研究不同大尺度环境下星系演化提供了新基准。数据与流程的公开发布支持科研可重复性及未来在宇宙学与天体物理中的应用。

Abstract: We present the first public cosmic-web environment catalog built on any DESI data release. Using ASTRA (Algorithm for Stochastic Topological RAnking), we classify each object in the DESI Early Data Release into void, sheet, filament, or knot by combining observed positions with matched random catalogs, without reconstructing a continuous density field. We apply this method to four DESI extragalactic tracers (BGS, LRG, ELG, and QSO) across the 20 EDR rosettes ($\sim 175$ deg$^2$ total), running 100 realizations per tracer-zone pair to derive per-object membership probabilities and classification entropies. We calibrate the classification thresholds using BGS as an anchor to match the volume-filling fractions reported for GAMA, and recover a physically consistent web morphology across all tracers. For BGS, the resulting web-type fractions and the environmental dependence of star formation are consistent with GAMA, COSMOS, and SDSS-based references, validating the method against established benchmarks. A normalized mutual information analysis on BGS reveals a clear dependence of the statistical associations between galaxy color, stellar mass, and specific star formation rate across environments. These results provide a new observational baseline for galaxy evolution studies with DESI. All data products and the open-source pipeline are publicly available.

</details>


### [37] [Cosmological Constraints on the Generalized Uncertainty Principle from Redshift-Space Distortions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01713)
*Andronikos Paliathanasis*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We study the cosmological implications of the Generalized Uncertainty Principle (GUP) by modifying the Poisson bracket to include a minimal length, leading to a deformed Raychaudhuri equation and an effective dynamical dark energy model within $\Lambda$CDM. Using growth rate data ($f$ and $f\sigma_8$) and background cosmological observations (CC, BAO, SNIa), we constrain the GUP deformation parameter $\beta$, finding it consistently negative with $\Lambda$CDM within 95\% C.L. Model comparison criteria (AIC and BIC) show weak-to-strong support for the GUP model when SNIa data are included.

我们研究了广义不确定原理（Generalized Uncertainty Principle, GUP）在宇宙学尺度上的影响，通过修改泊松括号引入最小长度，从而得到变形的Raychaudhuri方程，并在$\Lambda$CDM框架内导出一个有效的单参数动力学暗能量模型。利用结构增长数据（$f$ 和 $f\sigma_8$）以及背景观测数据（CC、BAO、SNIa），我们对GUP变形参数$\beta$进行了限制，发现其系统性为负值，而$\Lambda$CDM情形位于95\%置信区间内。当包含超新星数据时，Akaike信息准则（AIC）显示出对GUP模型的弱到强支持，贝叶斯证据也表现出微弱偏好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The Generalized Uncertainty Principle (GUP), motivated by quantum gravity theories, predicts a minimal measurable length, which may leave imprints on cosmological observables. While typically studied in high-energy or black hole physics, its potential effects on late-time cosmic structure formation remain underexplored. We aim to test whether such quantum-gravity-motivated modifications can be probed via cosmological observations, particularly through deviations in the growth of structure and expansion history, offering a window into Planck-scale physics using low-energy data.

广义不确定原理（GUP）受量子引力理论启发，预言存在一个最小可测长度，可能在宇宙学观测量上留下印记。尽管通常在高能或黑洞物理中研究，其对晚期宇宙结构形成的潜在影响仍较少被探索。我们的目标是检验这类受量子引力启发的修正是否可以通过宇宙学观测来探测，特别是通过结构增长和膨胀历史的偏差，从而利用低能观测数据窥探普朗克尺度物理。

Method: We modify the canonical Poisson bracket to incorporate a minimal length scale via the Generalized Uncertainty Principle, resulting in a deformed Raychaudhuri equation. This leads to corrections in the Friedmann and acceleration equations, effectively introducing a one-parameter dynamical dark energy model with a modified equation-of-state parameter dependent on the deformation parameter $\beta$. We derive the corresponding linear growth factor equation and compute the growth rate $f$ and $f\sigma_8(z)$. We perform Bayesian inference using observational datasets: redshift-space distortion measurements of $f\sigma_8$, cosmic chronometers (CC), baryon acoustic oscillations (BAO), and Type Ia supernovae (SNIa). We use Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) methods to constrain $\beta$ and other cosmological parameters, and compare the model to $\Lambda$CDM using information criteria (AIC) and Bayesian evidence.

我们通过广义不确定原理修改正则泊松括号以引入最小长度尺度，从而得到变形的Raychaudhuri方程。这导致Friedmann方程和加速度方程的修正，实质上引入了一个单参数动力学暗能量模型，其状态方程参数依赖于变形参数$\beta$。我们推导出相应的线性增长因子方程，并计算增长率$f$和$f\sigma_8(z)$。我们使用观测数据集进行贝叶斯推断：红移空间畸变测量的$f\sigma_8$、宇宙年代学（CC）、重子声学振荡（BAO）和Ia型超新星（SNIa）。我们采用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）方法对$\beta$及其他宇宙学参数进行限制，并使用信息准则（AIC）和贝叶斯证据与$\Lambda$CDM模型进行比较。

Result: The observational analysis yields a consistently negative best-fit value for the GUP deformation parameter $\beta$, with $\Lambda$CDM ($\beta=0$) lying within the 95\% credible interval. The inclusion of SNIa data strengthens the deviation from zero. The Akaike Information Criterion (AIC) indicates weak-to-strong support for the GUP-modified model over $\Lambda$CDM depending on the SNIa catalogue used, while the Bayesian evidence shows a weak preference. The model predicts a slight deviation from standard structure growth, consistent with current $f\sigma_8$ data.

观测分析得出GUP变形参数$\beta$的最佳拟合值系统性为负，而$\Lambda$CDM情形（$\beta=0$）位于95\%可信区间内。包含SNIa数据后，偏离零的程度增强。Akaike信息准则（AIC）表明，根据所使用的SNIa星表不同，GUP修正模型相对于$\Lambda$CDM具有弱到强的支持，而贝叶斯证据显示微弱偏好。该模型预测结构增长与标准情形有轻微偏离，与当前的$f\sigma_8$数据一致。

Conclusion: The Generalized Uncertainty Principle leaves potentially detectable imprints on cosmological observables, particularly in the growth of large-scale structure. The negative values of $\beta$ favored by data suggest that quantum-gravity-induced minimal length effects could slightly enhance cosmic acceleration, mimicking mild dynamical dark energy. Although $\Lambda$CDM remains consistent with data, the GUP-modified model is statistically comparable and mildly favored by information criteria when SNIa are included, making it a viable phenomenological extension worth further investigation with future surveys.

广义不确定原理可能在宇宙学观测量上留下可探测的印记，特别是在大尺度结构增长方面。数据偏好的负$\beta$值表明，由量子引力诱导的最小长度效应可能会轻微增强宇宙加速，模拟出温和的动力学暗能量行为。尽管$\Lambda$CDM仍与数据一致，但GUP修正模型在统计上相当，且在包含SNIa数据时受到信息准则的轻微支持，使其成为一个值得进一步研究的可行唯象扩展模型。

Abstract: We investigate the imprints of the Generalized Uncertainty Principle on cosmological scales by using redshift-space distortion measurements in combination with background cosmological data to determine constraints on the deformation parameter $β$. We consider the modified Poisson bracket related to the existence of a minimal length, which leads to a modified Raychaudhuri equation for the standard $Λ$CDM model and gives rise to a phenomenological one-parameter dynamical dark energy scenario. Through this modification, we can reveal the effects of the minimal length on the late-time structure of the universe. We employ the $f$ and $fσ_8$ measurements of the growth rate combined with background data, including cosmic chronometers, baryon acoustic oscillations and Type Ia supernova observations. The observational constraints reveal a systematically negative value for the deformation parameter $β$, with the $Λ$CDM limit lying within the 95\% credible interval. When supernova data are included, the Akaike Information Criterion indicates weak-to-strong support in favour of the GUP-modified model depending on the SNIa catalogue, while the Bayesian evidence suggests a weak preference.

### [38] [Estimates of the Dynamic Characteristics of Binary Systems for Traversable Wormholes Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01752)
*I. A. Moiseev,O. S. Sazhina*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper investigates potential observational signatures of traversable wormholes (WHs) in binary systems, where a companion star's motion is perturbed by a massive object on the other side of the WH throat. It analyzes both acceleration and radial velocity effects, comparing detectability against astrophysical noise and alternative configurations such as black holes or triple systems. For future radial velocity precision of 1.5 km/s, perturbations are detectable across all time scales; at 10 km/s, significance is reached after ~17 years with spectral methods reducing required data duration compared to matched filtering.

本文研究了可穿越虫洞（WH）在双星系统中的潜在可观测特征，其中伴星的运动受到虫洞喉部另一侧大质量天体的扰动。分析了加速度和径向速度的变化效应，并与黑洞双星及三体系统等竞争模型进行对比。当未来径向速度观测精度达到1.5 km/s时，所有时间尺度上的扰动均可探测；在更现实的10 km/s精度下，结合谱分析方法在积累约17年数据后可达统计显著性。相比单独使用匹配滤波，谱分析与非参数方法显著缩短所需观测时间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Traversable wormholes remain a theoretical possibility within general relativity but lack observational evidence. The motivation is to identify unique dynamical imprints of WHs in stellar orbits—particularly in binary systems where a companion star is gravitationally influenced by a distant mass connected via a wormhole throat—distinguishing them from conventional systems like black hole binaries or hierarchical triples.

可穿越虫洞在广义相对论中仍属理论可能，但缺乏观测证据。研究动机在于识别虫洞在恒星轨道动力学中的独特印记——特别是在双星系统中，伴星受到通过虫洞喉部连接的远端质量的引力影响，从而将其与黑洞双星或等级式三体系统区分开来。

Method: The authors model two scenarios: (1) a supermassive black hole candidate as a traversable wormhole, analyzing the perturbing acceleration on a nearby star and comparing it to stochastic stellar interactions near the Galactic center; (2) a wide binary system with a WH, modeling the induced radial velocity variations of the companion star. They simulate observational signals and apply spectral analysis, non-parametric methods, and matched-filtering to assess detectability under different velocity precisions (1.5 km/s and 10 km/s) and observation durations.

作者构建了两种情景：(1) 将超大质量黑洞候选体视为可穿越虫洞，分析其对邻近恒星的扰动加速度，并与银心附近恒星随机相互作用的竞争效应进行比较；(2) 含虫洞的宽双星系统，模拟伴星的径向速度变化。通过模拟观测信号，应用谱分析、非参数方法和匹配滤波技术，在不同径向速度精度（1.5 km/s 和 10 km/s）和观测时长下评估可探测性。

Result: For radial velocity precision of 1.5 km/s, wormhole-induced perturbations are detectable across all observation periods. At 10 km/s, statistical significance requires about 17 years of data when using spectral methods, which outperform matched-filtering alone. The radial velocity signature in the WH model differs from both BH binaries and triple systems, offering a potential discriminant. Perturbing accelerations in the supermassive WH scenario are comparable to or exceed those from ambient stars, suggesting observability in high-resolution kinematic surveys.

在1.5 km/s径向速度精度下，虫洞引起的扰动在所有观测时间段内均可探测。当精度为10 km/s时，使用谱分析方法需约17年数据积累才能达到统计显著性，且性能优于单独使用匹配滤波。虫洞模型中的径向速度特征不同于黑洞双星和三体系统，提供了潜在区分手段。在超大质量虫洞情景中，扰动加速度与周围恒星产生的加速度相当甚至更大，表明其可在高分辨率运动学巡天中被观测到。

Conclusion: Traversable wormholes could leave detectable dynamical signatures in the motion of stars in binary-like systems, particularly through anomalous radial velocity variations. With upcoming high-precision astrometric and spectroscopic surveys, such as those from ELT and SKA, these signatures may become observable within decades, especially when advanced data analysis techniques like spectral and non-parametric methods are employed.

可穿越虫洞可能在类双星系统的恒星运动中留下可观测的动力学特征，尤其是异常的径向速度变化。借助即将开展的高精度天体测量与光谱巡天（如ELT和SKA），结合谱分析与非参数方法等先进数据分析技术，这些特征可能在几十年内被观测证实。

Abstract: The work is devoted to the study of the possibilities of observational manifestations of traversable wormholes (WHs). The simplest binary system model consisting of a traversable WH candidate (black hole (BH), supermassive BH) and a companion star, whose motion is perturbed by a massive object (star) located on the other side of the wormhole throat, is considered. In the first case of supermassive BH as WH candidate the perturbing acceleration is analyzed and compared with a competing effect in the form of the stochastic influence of stars adjacent to the companion star. In the second case the features of the change in the radial velocity of the companion star in the model of a wide binary system with a WH are also analyzed in order to distinguish it from the following models: 1) a binary system with a BH, and 2) a triple system. For the observational accuracy in radial velocity expected in the near future, at the level of 1.5 km/s the radial velocity perturbations are detectable for all considered observation time spans. For a more realistic accuracy of 10 km/s, the spectral analysis methods become statistically significant after approximately 17 years of data accumulation. The application of spectral and non-parametric methods significantly decreases the required accumulation time compared to matched-filtering applied in isolation.

</details>


### [39] [No evidence for dynamical dark energy from the Combo correlation of GRBs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01980)
*Marco Muccino,Massimo Della Valle,Luca Izzo,Orlando Luongo*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The study uses updated gamma-ray burst (GRB) data calibrated via the Combo correlation and type Ia supernovae to probe dark energy dynamics and the Hubble constant $H_0$. A model-independent, redshift-binned parametrization of the dark energy equation of state $\omega(z)$ is employed, with careful consideration of spatial curvature. Results favor a cosmological constant ($\omega = -1$) at $z > 0.55$, disfavor curved cosmologies, and yield $H_0 \sim 70$ km/s/Mpc, alleviating the Hubble tension while showing no strong evidence for dynamical dark energy.

本研究使用通过Combo相关性和Ia型超新星校准的最新伽马射线暴（GRB）数据，探测暗能量动力学和哈勃常数$H_0$。采用模型无关的、按红移分箱的暗能量状态方程$\omega(z)$参数化方法，并仔细考虑空间曲率的影响。结果在$z > 0.55$时支持宇宙学常数（$\omega = -1$），排除了弯曲宇宙模型，得到$H_0 \sim 70$ km/s/Mpc，缓解了哈勃张力，且未发现暗能量具有显著动力学行为的证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Recent DESI results suggest possible dynamical dark energy, motivating independent, high-redshift tests of the dark energy equation of state $\omega(z)$. GRBs, extending to $z \sim 9$, offer a unique opportunity to probe $\omega(z)$ beyond the reach of supernovae. However, their use as standardizable candles requires robust calibration free from strong cosmological priors. Additionally, the persistent $H_0$ tension calls for independent $H_0$ measurements. This work aims to test $\omega(z)$ in a model-independent way using GRBs, improve their calibration using low-redshift anchors, and assess the impact of spatial curvature.

最近DESI的结果暗示可能存在动力学暗能量，这促使人们需要对暗能量状态方程$\omega(z)$进行独立的高红移检验。GRB可延伸至$z \sim 9$，为探测超出超新星范围的$\omega(z)$提供了独特机会。然而，将其作为可标准化烛光使用需依赖稳健的校准，避免强宇宙学先验。此外，持续存在的$H_0$张力要求独立测量$H_0$。本工作旨在利用GRB以模型无关方式检验$\omega(z)$，通过低红移锚定改进其校准，并评估空间曲率的影响。

Method: The authors employ the Combo correlation—a luminosity relation for GRBs involving the rest-frame break time, plateau luminosity, and end time of the plateau phase. They calibrate this relation using three type Ia supernova catalogs at $z \leq 0.075$ and B\'ezier interpolation of the Hubble rate $H(z)$, avoiding the poorly convergent cosmographic series at high $z$. A redshift-binned, piecewise-constant parametrization of $\omega(z)$ is adopted for dark energy reconstruction, enabling a model-independent analysis. The impact of spatial curvature $\Omega_k$ is explicitly included as a free parameter in both calibration and DE reconstruction. Bayesian inference and Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) methods are used to constrain parameters.

作者采用Combo相关性——一种涉及静止系断点时间、平台期光度和平台期末时间的GRB光度关系。使用三个在$z \leq 0.075$的Ia型超新星目录以及哈勃率$H(z)$的B\'ezier插值对其进行校准，避免了在高$z$时收敛性差的宇宙学级数展开。对暗能量重构采用红移分箱的逐段常数$\omega(z)$参数化，实现模型无关分析。空间曲率$\Omega_k$被显式地作为自由参数纳入校准和暗能量重构中。使用贝叶斯推断和马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）方法约束参数。

Result: The calibrated Combo correlation yields $H_0 \sim 70$ km/s/Mpc, which lies between local (e.g., SH0ES) and early-universe (e.g., Planck) estimates, thus alleviating the Hubble tension, though with larger uncertainties. In the reconstruction of $\omega(z)$, spatially curved models are statistically disfavored. At low redshifts ($z \lesssim 0.55$), a phantom-like behavior ($\omega < -1$) appears, but this is attributed to sparse data and selection effects near $z=0$. At $z > 0.55$, the data provide statistically robust support for $\omega \approx -1$, consistent with a cosmological constant. No significant evidence for dynamical dark energy is found.

校准后的Combo相关性给出$H_0 \sim 70$ km/s/Mpc，介于局域（如SH0ES）和早期宇宙（如Planck）估计值之间，从而缓解了哈勃张力，尽管不确定性较大。在$\omega(z)$重构中，空间弯曲模型在统计上不被支持。在低红移（$z \lesssim 0.55$）时出现类幽灵行为（$\omega < -1$），但这归因于$z=0$附近数据稀疏和选择效应。在$z > 0.55$时，数据为$\omega \approx -1$提供了统计上稳健的支持，与宇宙学常数一致。未发现暗能量具有显著动力学行为的证据。

Conclusion: Gamma-ray bursts, when calibrated using low-redshift supernovae and model-independently interpolated $H(z)$ data, serve as reliable distance indicators up to very high redshifts. The analysis provides no compelling evidence for deviations from the cosmological constant $\Lambda$, supporting the standard $\Lambda$CDM model at $z > 0.55$. The result $H_0 \sim 70$ km/s/Mpc helps ease the Hubble tension, and the disfavoring of spatial curvature reinforces the assumption of flatness in modern cosmology. GRBs are thus consistent with the current cosmic distance ladder and offer a promising tool for probing dark energy in the high-$z$ universe.

伽马射线暴在使用低红移超新星和模型无关插值得到的$H(z)$数据校准时，可作为高达极高红移的可靠距离指示器。该分析未提供偏离宇宙学常数$\Lambda$的有力证据，支持在$z > 0.55$时的标准$\Lambda$CDM模型。得到的$H_0 \sim 70$ km/s/Mpc有助于缓解哈勃张力，且对空间曲率的排除强化了现代宇宙学中平坦性假设。因此，GRB与当前宇宙距离阶梯一致，是探测高红移宇宙中暗能量的有力工具。

Abstract: Recently, the Dark Energy Spectroscopic Instrument (DESI) collaboration has presented results indicating that dark energy may exhibit dynamical behavior. Calibrated gamma-ray burst (GRB) correlations can be employed to verify or reject a time-evolution of the dark energy (DE) equation of state, $ω(z)$, up to redshifts $z\sim 9$. We use the most updated catalog of GRBs fulfilling the Combo correlation and improve its calibration employing three catalogs of type Ia supernovae at redshifts $z\leq0.075$ and the Bézier interpolation of the Hubble rate, as an alternative to the cosmographic series that fails to be constraining at high redshifts. To test the evolution of $ω(z)$, we adopt a model-independent, redshift-binned DE parametrization. In both the calibration and the DE reconstruction analyses the impact of the spatial curvature on the results is explored. The calibrated Combo correlation yields a Hubble constant $H_0\sim70$ km/s/Mpc which alleviates the existing Hubble tension and is broadly consistent with current measurements, although the uncertainties prevent a high-precision measurement. Regarding the reconstruction of $ω(z)$ of DE, spatially curved scenarios are disfavored and, despite the apparent ''phantom'' behavior at $z\lesssim0.55$ due to the limited statistics caused by the shortage of nearby events, at $z>0.55$ the analysis provides statistically robust evidence in favor of the cosmological constant scenario. The Combo correlation alleviates the Hubble tension and shows no significant evidence in favor of dynamical DE. This suggests that GRBs, as distance indicators, are broadly consistent with the current cosmic distance ladder.

</details>


### [40] [Non-minimally coupled quintessence with sign-switching interaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02204)
*Jia-Qi Wang,Rong-Gen Cai,Zong-Kuan Guo,Yun-He Li,Shao-Jiang Wang,Xin Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We propose a non-minimally coupled quintessence model that explains the late-time weakening of dark energy suggested by recent DESI data. The model features a canonical scalar field coupled to dark matter, inducing an effective crossing of the phantom divide without actual phantom behavior. Current data favor this model over $\Lambda$CDM and $w_0w_a$CDM.

我们提出了一种非最小耦合的quintessence模型，以解释近期DESI数据所提示的暗能量晚期减弱现象。该模型包含一个与暗物质耦合的规范标量场，诱导了有效穿越phantom分界面的行为，而无需真正的phantom场。当前宇宙学数据更支持此模型，优于$\Lambda$CDM和$w_0w_a$CDM模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Recent DESI measurements suggest a possible deviation from $\Lambda$CDM, indicating a weakening of dark energy at late times. This calls for dynamical dark energy models that can naturally explain such behavior without fine-tuning or unphysical features like phantom fields crossing $w = -1$. Our motivation is to construct a physically well-motivated, non-minimally coupled quintessence model that realizes this dynamics through interaction with dark matter.

近期DESI测量表明可能存在偏离$\Lambda$CDM的情况，暗示暗能量在晚期有所减弱。这要求构建能够自然解释此类行为的动力学暗能量模型，而不依赖精细调节或如phantom场穿越$w = -1$之类的非物理特征。我们的动机是构建一个物理上合理、通过与暗物质相互作用实现该动力学的非最小耦合quintessence模型。

Method: We introduce a non-minimal coupling between a canonical quintessence scalar field $\phi$ and dark matter, described by an interaction term in the Lagrangian leading to energy exchange. The coupling function is chosen such that dark energy density starts decreasing only after it dominates the cosmic energy budget. We derive the modified Friedmann equations and solve the background evolution, computing observational predictions for $H(z)$, $E_G$, and growth history $f\sigma_8(z)$. Bayesian analysis is performed using DESI, Planck, SH0ES, and Pantheon+ data to compare with $\Lambda$CDM and $w_0w_a$CDM.

我们在规范quintessence标量场$\phi$与暗物质之间引入非最小耦合，由拉格朗日量中的相互作用项描述，导致能量交换。选择耦合函数使得暗能量密度仅在主导宇宙能量预算后才开始减小。我们推导出修正的Friedmann方程并求解背景演化，计算$H(z)$、$E_G$和增长历史$f\sigma_8(z)$的观测预测。使用DESI、Planck、SH0ES和Pantheon+数据进行贝叶斯分析，与$\Lambda$CDM和$w_0w_a$CDM进行比较。

Result: The model naturally produces a late-time decrease in dark energy density, consistent with DESI hints. The effective equation of state $w_{\rm eff}(z)$ shows an apparent crossing of the phantom divide due to modified dark matter evolution, even though the fundamental $w_\phi > -1$ always. The coupling induces a sign flip in the effective energy transfer rate between dark sectors. Bayesian model comparison yields higher evidence than both $\Lambda$CDM and $w_0w_a$CDM, with $\Delta \ln \mathcal{Z} > 2$ in favor of our model.

该模型自然地产生了暗能量密度在晚期的减小，与DESI的迹象一致。即使基本的$w_\phi > -1$始终成立，由于暗物质演化的修正，有效状态方程$w_{\rm eff}(z)$显示出表观穿越phantom分界面的现象。该耦合诱导了暗区之间有效能量转移率的符号翻转。贝叶斯模型比较显示，我们的模型证据高于$\Lambda$CDM和$w_0w_a$CDM，$\Delta \ln \mathcal{Z} > 2$支持本模型。

Conclusion: A non-minimally coupled quintessence model provides a compelling explanation for the observed late-time weakening of dark energy. The interaction with dark matter generates an effective phantom-like behavior without invoking unphysical scalar fields. This scenario is theoretically well-motivated and preferred by current cosmological observations, offering a viable alternative to $\Lambda$CDM and standard dynamical dark energy models.

非最小耦合的quintessence模型为观测到的暗能量晚期减弱提供了有力解释。与暗物质的相互作用产生了类似phantom的行为，而无需引入非物理的标量场。该情景在理论上具有充分动机，并受到当前宇宙学观测的支持，为$\Lambda$CDM和标准动力学暗能量模型提供了可行的替代方案。

Abstract: We propose a new non-minimally coupled quintessence model to account for the late-time dark energy dynamics indicated by recent DESI measurements. Within this framework, the quintessence density begins to decrease only when it starts to dominate the universe, which naturally accounts for the late-time onset of dark energy weakening. The coupling also induces a sign change in the effective energy transfer between dark matter and dark energy during cosmic evolution. While the scalar field itself remains canonical and never crosses the phantom divide, the modified evolution of the dark matter density gives rise to an effective crossing behavior in the observationally inferred dark energy sector. Compared with both $Λ$CDM and $w_0w_a$CDM models, our model is favored more strongly by current cosmological data. This work may provide a promising avenue for understanding the observational late-time weakening of dark energy and the origin of its dynamics.

</details>


### [41] [Consistency relations of amplitude and phase fluctuations of gravitational waves magnified by strong gravitational lensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02216)
*Yuta Nakazono,Teruaki Suyama*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: The paper studies gravitational wave fluctuations due to wave optics lensing in the combined presence of a strong lens and cosmological weak lenses, deriving the amplification factor up to second order in the weak lensing potential and establishing diagrammatic rules for systematic evaluation. It shows that known consistency relations for weak lensing statistics remain valid even when a strong lens is present, and identifies two key effects: magnification of the signal and a shift of the Fresnel scale to larger scales.

该论文研究了在强透镜和宇宙学弱透镜共同存在下，引力波因波动光学透镜效应产生的振幅和相位涨落。通过推导出弱透镜势二阶精度的放大因子并建立基于图示法则的系统性计算方法，表明原有的弱透镜统计一致性关系即使在强透镜存在时仍严格成立，并发现信号平均值中存在信号放大和菲涅尔尺度向更大尺度移动的现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Gravitational waves (GWs) are increasingly being used as precision probes of cosmology and gravity. However, their propagation is affected by both strong and weak gravitational lensing, which can distort amplitude and phase. While strong lensing is typically treated in geometric optics, wave effects become important at kilohertz frequencies (e.g., from compact binaries). Understanding how weak lensing modulates GW signals in the presence of a strong lens is essential for accurate inference and for extracting cosmological information. The motivation is to develop a consistent theoretical framework that combines both effects and to investigate whether known statistical consistency relations survive in this more complex scenario.

引力波正日益成为宇宙学和引力理论的精确探针。然而，其传播会受到强和弱引力透镜的共同影响，导致振幅和相位畸变。虽然强透镜通常用几何光学处理，但在千赫兹频段（如致密双星）波动效应变得重要。理解在强透镜背景下弱透镜如何调制引力波信号对于精确推断和提取宇宙学信息至关重要。本文动机是建立一个统一的理论框架来结合两种透镜效应，并检验已知的统计一致性关系在此复杂情形下是否依然成立。

Method: The authors employ the path integral formulation of wave propagation in curved spacetime, applying the geometric optics approximation for the strong lens while treating the weak lensing potential perturbatively. They derive the amplification factor $\mathcal{F}$ up to second order in the weak lensing potential $\phi_\mathrm{w}$, using the background Green's function modified by the strong lens. A diagrammatic method is introduced to organize the perturbative expansion, with vertices representing weak lensing interactions and propagators given by the strongly-lensed wave kernel. The statistics of the amplification (mean, variance, etc.) are computed by averaging over weak lensing configurations using the weak lensing power spectrum.

作者采用弯曲时空中的波传播路径积分表述，对强透镜应用几何光学近似，同时将弱透镜势 $\phi_\mathrm{w}$ 作为微扰处理。利用强透镜修正的背景格林函数，推导出放大因子 $\mathcal{F}$ 在弱透镜势二阶精度下的表达式。引入一种图示方法来组织微扰展开，其中顶点表示弱透镜相互作用，传播子由强透镜下的波核给出。通过在弱透镜构型上利用弱透镜功率谱进行平均，计算放大因子的统计量（均值、方差等）。

Result: The amplification factor is derived as $\mathcal{F} \approx 1 + \mathcal{F}^{(1)} + \mathcal{F}^{(2)}$, where $\mathcal{F}^{(1)}$ and $\mathcal{F}^{(2)}$ are linear and quadratic in the weak lensing potential, respectively. The diagrammatic rules allow systematic computation of higher-order terms. The paper shows that the consistency relations—such as the vanishing mean of the imaginary part of $\mathcal{F}$ and specific scaling of the variance with frequency—remain unchanged in form despite the presence of a strong lens. Additionally, it is found that the mean weak lensing signal exhibits both magnification (enhancement of $|\mathcal{F}|^2$) and a shift of the Fresnel scale $r_F = \sqrt{\lambda D}$ to larger scales, where $\lambda$ is the GW wavelength and $D$ is the distance, mirroring trends seen in the variance.

推导出放大因子为 $\mathcal{F} \approx 1 + \mathcal{F}^{(1)} + \mathcal{F}^{(2)}$，其中 $\mathcal{F}^{(1)}$ 和 $\mathcal{F}^{(2)}$ 分别线性和二次依赖于弱透镜势。图示法则可用于系统计算高阶项。论文表明，即使存在强透镜，原有的一致性关系——如 $\mathcal{F}$ 虚部均值为零、方差与频率的特定标度关系——形式上保持不变。此外，发现平均弱透镜信号中既存在放大效应（$|\mathcal{F}|^2$ 增强），也出现菲涅尔尺度 $r_F = \sqrt{\lambda D}$ 向更大尺度移动的现象，这与方差中的趋势一致。

Conclusion: The paper establishes that the statistical properties of weak lensing on gravitational waves, including key consistency relations, are robust against the presence of a strong lens when analyzed within a wave-optics framework. The derived amplification factor and diagrammatic formalism provide a powerful tool for modeling stochastic lensing effects in multi-messenger and multi-wavelength observations. The observed magnification and Fresnel scale shift in the mean signal suggest observable imprints of cumulative weak lensing that could be probed in future high-precision GW data.

本文证明，在波动光学框架下分析时，引力波的弱透镜统计性质（包括关键的一致性关系）在强透镜存在下依然稳健。所推导的放大因子和图示形式体系为建模多信使和多波长观测中的随机透镜效应提供了有力工具。平均信号中观测到的放大效应和菲涅尔尺度移动表明，累积弱透镜可能在未来的高精度引力波数据中留下可观测印记。

Abstract: We discuss the amplitude and phase fluctuations of gravitational waves due to wave optics lensing in the presence of both a strong lens and cosmological weak lenses. By applying the geometric optics approximation to the strong lens and treating the weak lensing potential perturbatively, we obtain the amplification factor up to the second order in the weak lensing potential. Additionally, we establish a methodology to systematically evaluate the weak lensing effects based on diagrammatic rules. Based on the derived amplification factor, we evaluate the statistics of the fluctuations and demonstrate that the consistency relations originally established in the absence of a strong lens still hold in exactly the same form when a strong lens is present. The physical origin of these relations is also discussed. Furthermore, we demonstrate that for the mean of the weak lensing signal, both the magnification of the signal and the shift of the Fresnel scale to larger scales occur, consistent with the behavior observed in the variance.

</details>


### [42] [Revealing the neutrino mass through persistent homology of the cosmic web](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02300)
*Jiaqi Wang,Willem Elbers,Carlos S. Frenk,Shaun Cole,Xiaohu Yang,Ian G. McCarthy,Rien van de Weygaert*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: This paper introduces persistence strips—a new topological summary based on persistent homology—to measure neutrino mass from cosmic web structure. Applied to FLAMINGO simulations, they yield tight neutrino mass constraints ($\sigma_{m_\nu} \approx 0.05\,\mathrm{eV}$) in a high-dimensional cosmological parameter space, outperforming traditional Betti curves by breaking degeneracies via multi-scale environmental sensitivity, especially from voids.

本文引入了持久同调（persistent homology）框架下的新拓扑统计量——持久条带（persistence strips），用于从宇宙网结构中测量中微子质量。在FLAMINGO模拟上应用时，该方法在高维宇宙学参数空间中实现了紧密的中微子质量限制（$\sigma_{m_\nu} \approx 0.05\,\mathrm{eV}$），性能优于传统的未分箱Betti曲线，尤其通过空洞区域的多尺度环境敏感性有效打破参数简并。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Neutrino mass is a key open question in particle physics and cosmology, but its inference from large-scale structure is hindered by parameter degeneracies in standard observables like the power spectrum. Topological summaries, such as Betti curves from persistent homology, offer complementary, non-Gaussian information about the cosmic web. However, full exploitation of persistence diagrams is challenging due to their complexity. We aim to develop a compressed, interpretable representation—persistence strips—that retains sensitivity to neutrino mass while enabling robust statistical inference in a high-dimensional cosmological parameter space.

中微子质量是粒子物理与宇宙学中的关键未解问题，但标准观测量（如功率谱）在大尺度结构中存在参数简并，限制了其推断。拓扑统计量（如来自持久同调的Betti曲线）能提供关于宇宙网的非高斯、互补信息。然而，持久图（persistence diagrams）因复杂难以充分利用。我们旨在发展一种压缩且可解释的表示——持久条带（persistence strips），在保留对中微子质量敏感性的同时，支持高维宇宙学参数空间中的鲁棒统计推断。

Method: We apply persistent homology to matter distributions from the FLAMINGO suite of hydrodynamical $N$-body simulations across a 10-dimensional $w_0 w_a\text{CDM} + \nu$ cosmological parameter space. We introduce persistence strips: a segmentation of Betti curves by persistence (lifetime of topological features), converting 2D persistence diagrams into a set of 1D curves that encode scale- and environment-dependent topology. We build a Gaussian process emulator for these strips to enable fast likelihood evaluation and perform Bayesian inference to forecast neutrino mass constraints, marginalizing over all other parameters, including those degenerate with $m_\nu$ in traditional probes.

我们将持久同调应用于FLAMINGO流体动力学$N$-体模拟套件中的物质分布，覆盖一个10维的$w_0 w_a\text{CDM} + \nu$宇宙学参数空间。我们引入持久条带：按持久性（拓扑特征寿命）对Betti曲线进行分割，将二维持久图转化为一组一维曲线，编码尺度和环境依赖的拓扑信息。构建高斯过程模拟器（emulator）以实现快速似然评估，并通过贝叶斯推断预测中微子质量限制，在包括传统探针中与$m_\nu$简并的所有其他参数上进行边缘化。

Result: Persistence strips achieve a neutrino mass uncertainty of $\sigma_{m_\nu} = 0.05\,\mathrm{eV}$ for the total matter field and $0.13\,\mathrm{eV}$ for the dark matter-only field in a $(350\,\mathrm{Mpc})^3$ volume, significantly improving upon standard Betti curves by a factor of ~2 in constraining power. The strongest signal arises from void topology, where underdense regions show high sensitivity to the neutrino mass fraction. Persistence strips break degeneracies between $m_\nu$, $\Omega_m$, and $\sigma_8$ by leveraging multi-scale, environment-specific responses. Two physically distinct contributions are identified: (i) neutrinos suppress structure formation in low-density regions, altering void topology; (ii) massive neutrinos modify the clustering of dark matter, detectable through filament and wall statistics.

持久条带在$(350\,\mathrm{Mpc})^3$体积中对总物质场实现$\sigma_{m_\nu} = 0.05\,\mathrm{eV}$、对纯暗物质场实现$0.13\,\mathrm{eV}$的中微子质量误差限制，约束能力比标准Betti曲线提升约两倍。最强信号来自空洞拓扑，其中低密度区域对中微子质量分数高度敏感。持久条带利用多尺度、环境特异的响应，打破了$m_\nu$、$\Omega_m$和$\sigma_8$之间的简并。我们识别出两个物理上不同的贡献：(i) 中微子在低密度区抑制结构形成，改变空洞拓扑；(ii) 大质量中微子改变暗物质的成团性，可通过丝状结构与墙状结构的统计检测。

Conclusion: Persistence strips provide a powerful, interpretable topological summary statistic for cosmological inference, particularly effective in probing neutrino mass through void-dominated topology. Their ability to compress complex topological data while preserving sensitivity to physical processes enables degeneracy-breaking in high-dimensional parameter spaces. This work establishes persistent homology—as instantiated by persistence strips—as a competitive tool for next-generation large-scale structure analyses, especially when applied to weak lensing surveys that trace the total matter distribution.

持久条带为宇宙学推断提供了一种强大且可解释的拓扑统计量，尤其在通过以空洞为主的拓扑探测中微子质量方面表现优异。它能在压缩复杂拓扑数据的同时保留对物理过程的敏感性，从而在高维参数空间中打破简并。本研究确立了持久同调（以持久条带为实例）作为下一代大尺度结构分析的竞争性工具，尤其是在追踪总物质分布的弱引力透镜巡天中的应用前景广阔。

Abstract: Cosmological constraints on neutrino mass offer a promising avenue for advancing our understanding of both fundamental particle physics and the evolution of cosmic large-scale structure. To overcome challenges associated with traditional probes of neutrino mass, particularly degeneracies with other parameters, we consider topological summaries of the cosmic web based on the formalism of persistent homology. We introduce persistence strips, a novel representation that segments Betti curves by topological persistence, effectively condensing two-dimensional persistence diagrams into a set of one-dimensional curves. Applied to the FLAMINGO suite of cosmological simulations, these topological descriptors demonstrate pronounced sensitivity to neutrino mass. By constructing an emulator spanning a 10-dimensional $w_0 w_a\text{CDM} +ν$ cosmological parameter space that includes parameters degenerate with neutrino masses in conventional approaches, assuming a volume of only $(350 \, \mathrm{Mpc})^3$, we obtain neutrino mass constraints with an uncertainty of $0.05 \, \mathrm{eV}$ for the total matter field and $0.13 \, \mathrm{eV}$ for the dark matter-only field, with the strongest constraints coming from void topology. Persistence strips exhibit roughly twice the constraining power of unbinned Betti curves and, through their multi-scale, environment-dependent sensitivity, systematically break degeneracies between neutrino mass and other cosmological parameters. We pinpoint the precise physical origin of the signal, identifying two equally important contributions: sensitivity to the neutrino mass fraction, which is highest in underdense regions, and the impact of neutrinos on the distribution of dark matter. Our findings highlight the particular promise of applying topological statistics to weak lensing measurements, which directly probe the total matter distribution.

</details>


### [43] [Smoluchowski Coagulation Equation and the Evolution of Primordial Black Hole Clusters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01684)
*Borui Zhang,Wei-Xiang Feng,Haipeng An*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: We simulate primordial black hole (PBH) clustering and mergers in early dark matter halos using the Smoluchowski coagulation equation, incorporating mass segregation effects and solving it via Monte Carlo methods to explain the rapid formation of high-redshift supermassive black holes observed as 'little red dots' by JWST.

我们利用Smoluchowski凝并方程模拟早期暗物质晕中原初黑洞（PBH）的聚类与合并，包含质量分层效应，并通过蒙特卡洛方法求解，以解释JWST观测到的‘小红点’中高红移超大质量黑洞的快速形成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The discovery of supermassive black holes at high redshifts ($z \gtrsim 10$) in JWST's 'little red dots' challenges standard astrophysical models of black hole formation and growth, motivating an alternative explanation via primordial black hole (PBH) clustering and rapid mergers in dense environments.

JWST在‘小红点’中发现的高红移（$z \gtrsim 10$）超大质量黑洞对标准黑洞形成与增长模型构成挑战，促使我们探索通过原初黑洞（PBH）在致密环境中聚类与快速合并的替代机制。

Method: We solve the Smoluchowski coagulation equation using a Monte Carlo approach with full conditioning via the discrete inverse transformation method. We derive coagulation kernels that account for gravitational interactions of PBHs, including the effects of mass segregation within clusters. The evolution of PBH mass functions and runaway merger timescales are simulated across cosmic redshifts for various initial cluster densities and particle numbers.

我们采用基于离散逆变换法的全条件化蒙特卡洛方法求解Smoluchowski凝并方程。推导了包含引力相互作用及团簇内质量分层效应的凝并核。模拟了不同初始密度和粒子数下，跨越宇宙红移的PBH质量函数演化与失控合并时标。

Result: Our simulations show that PBH clusters with sufficient initial density and number ($\gtrsim 10^3$ PBHs) can undergo runaway mergers on astrophysically short timescales ($\ll 1\,{\rm Gyr}$), forming supermassive black holes by $z \sim 10$. Mass segregation significantly reduces the merger timescale and enhances the efficiency of massive PBH growth.

模拟显示，具有足够初始密度和数量（$\gtrsim 10^3$个PBH）的PBH团簇可在远短于1 Gyr的天体物理时标内发生失控合并，在$z \sim 10$时形成超大质量黑洞。质量分层显著缩短合并时标并提升大质量PBH的增长效率。

Conclusion: Primordial black hole clustering and successive mergers provide a viable pathway for the early emergence of supermassive black holes, consistent with JWST observations of 'little red dots'. This scenario can be further tested through gravitational wave signatures from PBH mergers detectable by LISA and other future observatories.

原初黑洞聚类与连续合并为超大质量黑洞的早期出现提供了可行路径，与JWST对‘小红点’的观测一致。该情景可通过LISA等未来观测站可探测的PBH合并引力波信号进一步验证。

Abstract: In arXiv:2507.07171, we demonstrate that the high-redshift supermassive black holes in the so-called "little red dots" discovered by James Webb Space Telescope (JWST) can be explained by the primordial black hole (PBH) clustering on small scales. In this paper, we present a comprehensive simulation of the successive PBH mergers within a cluster by solving the Smoluchowski coagulation equation. We derive the coagulation kernel considering both cases with and without the effects of mass segregation. Then we employ the Monte Carlo method to solve the equation, implementing the full-conditioning scheme using the discrete inverse transformation method. Our simulations determine the runaway timescales of clusters and the mass population evolution of PBHs across a wide range of cosmic redshifts, depending on the number of PBHs within the cluster and the associated density.
