### [44] [Laser-assisted production of the light charged Higgs boson from top quark decay in the type-I two Higgs doublet model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01243)
*M. Jakha,S. Mouslih,M. Ouhammou,R. Chahri,S. El Asri,S. Taj,B. Manaut*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper studies how a circularly polarized laser field affects the top quark decay $t \rightarrow bH^+$ in the type-I two Higgs doublet model, showing that under strong laser fields the branching ratio can exceed the standard $t \rightarrow bW^+$ channel.

本文研究了圆偏振激光场在I型双希格斯二重态模型中对顶夸克衰变$t \rightarrow bH^+$的影响，表明在强激光场下，其分支比可超过标准的$t \rightarrow bW^+$道。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To explore how external electromagnetic fields, specifically intense laser fields, can modify top quark decay observables and enhance the detectability of charged Higgs bosons ($H^+$) at colliders, especially in scenarios with missing energy challenges at the LHC.

旨在探索外部电磁场（特别是强激光场）如何改变顶夸克衰变观测量，并增强对带电希格斯玻色子（$H^+$）的探测能力，尤其是在LHC存在丢失能量问题的情况下。

Method: The Dirac-Volkov formalism is employed to describe charged particles interacting with a circularly polarized laser field. The decay width and branching ratio for $t \rightarrow bH^+$ are computed under varying laser intensities and frequencies within the type-I two Higgs doublet model (2HDM).

采用Dirac-Volkov形式主义描述带电粒子与圆偏振激光场的相互作用，并在I型双希格斯二重态模型（2HDM）框架下计算不同激光强度和频率下的$t \rightarrow bH^+$衰变宽度和分支比。

Result: For a laser field strength of $3.8\times 10^{14}$ V/cm and photon energy of $0.117$ eV, the branching ratio of $t \rightarrow bH^+$ reaches up to $0.97$ for $H^+$ masses between $80$--$150$ GeV, exceeding the SM $t \rightarrow bW^+$ rate. Both laser intensity and frequency significantly influence the decay dynamics.

当激光场强为$3.8\times 10^{14}$ V/cm、光子能量为$0.117$ eV时，对于质量在$80$--$150$ GeV之间的$H^+$，$t \rightarrow bH^+$的分支比可达$0.97$，超过标准模型中的$t \rightarrow bW^+$过程。激光强度和频率均显著影响衰变动学。

Conclusion: Strong electromagnetic fields can dramatically enhance the production signatures of new particles like the charged Higgs boson, offering a novel experimental strategy to probe beyond Standard Model physics in high-energy collider environments.

强电磁场能显著增强新粒子（如带电希格斯玻色子）的产生信号，为在高能对撞机环境中探测超出标准模型的新物理提供了新颖的实验策略。

Abstract: We investigate the impact of a circularly polarized laser field on the top quark decay process into a charged Higgs boson ($t\rightarrow bH^+$) within the type-I two Higgs doublet model. Our study aims to explore how an external electromagnetic field can modify key observables and potentially facilitate the experimental detection of the charged Higgs boson, addressing challenges related to missing energy in collider experiments such as the LHC. Employing the Dirac-Volkov formalism, we model the interaction between charged particles and the laser field and demonstrate that the presence of the laser can notably influence the decay branching ratios under suitable conditions. The analysis reveals that both the intensity and frequency of the laser field play a crucial role in determining the decay width. In particular, for a laser field strength of $3.8\times 10^{14}$ V/cm and a photon energy of $0.117$ eV, the branching ratio of the top quark decaying into a charged Higgs boson with mass in the range $80$-$150$ GeV and a bottom quark reaches $0.97$, surpassing the standard $t\rightarrow bW^+$ channel. These results suggest that strong electromagnetic fields can serve as an effective mechanism to enhance signals of new particles, offering promising avenues for experimental searches beyond the Standard Model.

</details>


### [45] [Origin of the Covariant Wigner Operator as a Quantum Amplitude in QCD](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01248)
*Chueng-Ryong Ji,Daniel W. Piasecki*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper reinterprets the QCD Wigner function as a quantum probability amplitude in phase space via a relativistic Koopman-von Neumann-Sudarshan (KvNS) framework, showing it is isomorphic to a phase space spinor and clarifying its nonclassical features such as negativity; this approach unifies classical and quantum dynamics and provides a clearer foundation for parton distributions.

本文通过相对论性Koopman-von Neumann-Sudarshan（KvNS）框架，将QCD中的Wigner函数重新解释为相空间中的量子概率幅，证明其自然同构于一个相空间旋量，并阐明了诸如负性等非经典特征；该方法统一了经典与量子动力学，为部分子分布函数提供了更清晰的基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The Wigner function in QCD is notoriously difficult to interpret due to its quasiprobabilistic nature and possible negativity, which obscures its physical meaning. Recent insights from the Koopman-von Neumann-Sudarshan (KvNS) formulation of classical mechanics suggest that the Wigner function should be viewed not as a quasiprobability density but as a quantum probability amplitude projected onto classical phase space. This motivates extending the KvNS framework to relativistic QCD to achieve a more coherent and physically transparent interpretation of the Wigner operator and its role in parton physics.

由于Wigner函数具有准概率性和可能出现负值，其在QCD中的物理解释一直存在困难。近年来基于Koopman-von Neumann-Sudarshan（KvNS）经典力学表述的研究表明，Wigner函数应被视为投影到经典相空间的量子概率幅，而非准概率密度。这激励我们将KvNS框架推广至相对论性QCD，以获得对Wigner算符及其在部分子物理中作用的更一致且物理上更透明的理解。

Method: The authors construct a relativistic Koopman description of the quark Wigner operator within the KvNS Hilbert space framework. They introduce an idempotent projection that maps the Wigner operator to a phase space spinor, establishing a natural isomorphism. The dynamics are formulated to preserve both classical and quantum limits, with the classical limit recovered when $\hbar \to 0$. The spinor structure allows for a unified treatment of spin and phase space degrees of freedom in relativistic QCD.

作者在KvNS希尔伯特空间框架内构建了夸克Wigner算符的相对论性Koopman描述。他们引入了一个幂等投影，将Wigner算符映射为一个相空间旋量，建立了自然同构关系。动力学形式保持经典与量子极限的一致性，并在$\hbar \to 0$时恢复经典极限。旋量结构使得在相对论性QCD中对自旋与相空间自由度进行统一处理成为可能。

Result: The Wigner operator is shown to be isomorphic to a phase space spinor via idempotent projection, confirming its interpretation as a quantum probability amplitude rather than a quasiprobability density. Negativity in the Wigner function arises naturally from interference of these amplitudes. The relativistic KvNS framework successfully reproduces the classical limit of QCD and provides a transparent origin for parton distribution functions. Spin and phase space dynamics are consistently unified.

通过幂等投影，Wigner算符被证明与相空间旋量同构，确认其作为量子概率幅而非准概率密度的解释。Wigner函数中的负性自然来源于这些振幅之间的干涉。相对论性KvNS框架成功复现了QCD的经典极限，并为部分子分布函数提供了清晰的起源。自旋与相空间动力学得到了一致的统一。

Conclusion: The Wigner function in relativistic QCD should be interpreted as a quantum probability amplitude in phase space, not a quasiprobability. The Koopman-von Neumann-Sudarshan framework provides a unified description of classical and quantum dynamics, clarifies nonclassical features like negativity, and offers a deeper foundation for parton physics. This reformulation enhances conceptual clarity and may lead to new computational approaches in high-energy QCD.

在相对论性QCD中，Wigner函数应被理解为相空间中的量子概率幅，而非准概率。Koopman-von Neumann-Sudarshan框架为经典与量子动力学提供了统一描述，澄清了诸如负性等非经典特征，并为部分子物理奠定了更深刻的基础。这一重构增强了概念上的清晰性，并可能推动高能QCD中新的计算方法的发展。

Abstract: The Wigner function plays a central role in QCD as a phase space object encoding correlations among quarks, antiquarks, and gluons, yet its interpretation remains subtle due to its quasiprobabilistic nature and possible negativity. Recent work based on the Koopman-von Neumann-Sudarshan (KvNS) Hilbert space formulation of classical mechanics suggests the Wigner function arises as a \textit{quantum probability amplitude} projected onto classical phase space, rather than a quasiprobability density \citep{wignerphasespace, wave_operator}. In the classical limit, this amplitude reduces to the classical Koopman wavefunction. In this work, we extend this perspective to relativistic QCD by constructing a Koopman description of the quark Wigner operator. We show that the Wigner operator is naturally isomorphic to a phase space spinor via an idempotent projection, providing a unified framework in which both classical and quantum dynamics are expressed. Within this formulation, the Wigner function retains its interpretation as an amplitude even in the relativistic regime. This viewpoint clarifies the origin of negativity and other nonclassical features, and provides a more transparent foundation for parton distribution functions in QCD. Remarkably, the relativistic Koopman framework reproduces the classical limit of QCD.

### [46] [Mechanical Equilibrium in the Magnetized Quark--Hadron Mixed Phase: A Covariant Generalization of the Gibbs Condition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01253)
*Aric Hackebill*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We develop a covariant mechanical equilibrium condition for the quark-hadron mixed phase boundary under magnetic-field-induced pressure anisotropy, using the relativistic thin-shell formalism to generalize the Young--Laplace conditions and replace the isotropic pressure balance of the Gibbs construction.

我们利用相对论薄壳形式发展了在磁场诱导压力各向异性下夸克-强子混合相边界的协变力学平衡条件，将应力-能量守恒解释为一组广义的Young--Laplace条件，从而取代各向同性Gibbs构造中的标量压力平衡条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: In strong magnetic fields, such as those in neutron stars, the pressure in quark and hadronic matter becomes anisotropic, invalidating the standard isotropic pressure-balance assumption (Gibbs construction) for phase transitions. A covariant and physically accurate description of mechanical equilibrium at the quark-hadron interface is required.

在强磁场（如中子星内部）下，夸克与强子物质的压力呈现各向异性，导致标准的各向同性压力平衡假设（Gibbs构造）失效。因此需要一种协变且物理上准确的夸克-强子界面力学平衡描述方法。

Method: We apply the relativistic thin-shell formalism to model the quark-hadron phase boundary, treating it as a hypersurface across which the stress-energy tensor is conserved. This leads to generalized Young--Laplace-type equations that encode mechanical equilibrium in a covariant way, accounting for pressure anisotropy induced by the magnetic field.

我们应用相对论薄壳形式（relativistic thin-shell formalism）将夸克-强子相边界建模为一个超曲面，在该超曲面上应力-能量张量守恒。由此导出广义的Young--Laplace型方程，以协变方式编码由磁场引起的压力各向异性下的力学平衡条件。

Result: We derive a set of covariant boundary conditions that generalize the scalar pressure balance to anisotropic systems. These conditions relate the discontinuity in the stress-energy tensor to the extrinsic curvature of the interface, providing a geometric characterization of the phase boundary in magnetic environments.

我们推导出一组协变边界条件，将标量压力平衡推广至各向异性系统。这些条件将应力-能量张量的不连续性与界面的外曲率联系起来，从而在磁场环境中对相边界提供了几何化的刻画。

Conclusion: The standard Gibbs construction is insufficient under strong magnetic fields due to pressure anisotropy. The relativistic thin-shell framework provides a consistent and covariant replacement, with the generalized Young--Laplace conditions offering a more accurate description of quark-hadron phase equilibrium in compact stars.

由于压力各向异性，标准Gibbs构造在强磁场下不再适用。相对论薄壳框架提供了一致且协变的替代方案，广义Young--Laplace条件为致密星体中的夸克-强子相平衡提供了更精确的描述。

Abstract: We formulate a covariant mechanical equilibrium condition for the quark-hadron mixed phase boundary in the presence of a magnetic-field-induced pressure anisotropy. Using the \emph{relativistic thin-shell} formalism to describe the quark-hadron boundary, we interpret conservation of stress-energy across the interface as a set of generalized Young--Laplace conditions which characterize the geometry of the interface. In a comoving stationary frame, this provides a covariant description of mechanical equilibrium at the interface, which serves as a replacement for the scalar pressure-balance condition used in the isotropic Gibbs construction.

### [47] [Quantum Fisher Information as a Probe of Sterile Neutrino New Physics:Geometric Advantage of KM3NeT over IceCube](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01256)
*Baktiar Wasir Farooq,Bipin Singh Koranga,Aritro Chatterjee*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: A reported 3.5σ tension between KM3NeT and IceCube neutrino detections may arise from sterile neutrino oscillations via matter-induced resonances or nonstandard interactions; using Quantum Fisher Information, we show KM3NeT achieves three orders of magnitude higher sensitivity than IceCube, with current detection methods already reaching the quantum Cramer-Rao bound.

报告的KM3NeT与IceCube之间3.5σ的中微子探测差异可能源于由物质诱导共振或非标准相互作用驱动的惰性中微子振荡；利用量子费舍尔信息，我们发现KM3NeT的灵敏度比IceCube高三个数量级，当前探测方法已达到量子克拉默-拉奥极限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: A statistical tension of up to 3.5σ exists between a high-energy neutrino event detected at KM3NeT and its absence in IceCube data, prompting investigation into new physics such as eV-scale sterile neutrinos. The 147-km baseline to KM3NeT is comparable to oscillation lengths for such models, making it sensitive to matter-enhanced oscillations (e.g., MSW-like resonances) or nonstandard interactions (NSI), which could explain the discrepancy.

KM3NeT探测到的一个高能中微子事件与IceCube未探测到该事件之间存在高达3.5σ的统计张力，促使人们探索新物理，例如eV尺度的惰性中微子。KM3NeT的147公里基线与这类模型的振荡长度相当，使其对物质增强振荡（如类似MSW共振）或非标准相互作用（NSI）敏感，这可能解释该差异。

Method: We apply the Quantum Fisher Information (QFI) framework to quantify the sensitivity of neutrino flavor states to new physics parameters, such as sterile mixing angles and NSI couplings. The QFI provides the fundamental precision limit via the quantum Cramer-Rao bound (qCRB). We compute the QFI for both matter-induced resonance and NSI scenarios along the 147-km baseline, comparing information content between KM3NeT and IceCube. We also perform an optimization over baseline distance to identify configurations maximizing sensitivity.

我们应用量子费舍尔信息（QFI）框架来量化中微子味态对新物理参数（如惰性混合角和NSI耦合）的敏感性。QFI通过量子克拉默-拉奥界（qCRB）提供基本精度极限。我们计算了沿147公里基线在物质诱导共振和NSI情景下的QFI，比较KM3NeT与IceCube之间的信息含量，并对基线距离进行优化以确定最大化灵敏度的配置。

Result: The QFI at KM3NeT exceeds that at IceCube by three orders of magnitude for matter-induced oscillations, due to optimal resonance conditions at ~150 km. For NSI scenarios, the advantage is smaller but still significant. We find that IceCube would require more than 30 times as many events to match the parameter precision of a single KM3NeT detection. The optimal baseline for maximal QFI is identified at 150–200 km, placing KM3NeT in a uniquely favorable position. Furthermore, existing detection strategies at KM3NeT already saturate the qCRB, meaning they achieve ultimate quantum-limited precision.

对于物质诱导振荡，由于~150 km处的最佳共振条件，KM3NeT的QFI比IceCube高出三个数量级。在NSI情景下优势较小但仍显著。我们发现，IceCube需要超过30倍的事件数才能达到单个KM3NeT探测的参数精度。最大QFI的最优基线被确定为150–200 km，使KM3NeT处于独特有利的位置。此外，KM3NeT现有的探测策略已饱和qCRB，意味着达到了终极量子极限精度。

Conclusion: The KM3NeT experiment, due to its favorable baseline, is uniquely positioned to probe sterile neutrino oscillations and nonstandard interactions with quantum-limited precision. A few upcoming events can provide the first constraints governed by fundamental quantum metrology bounds, surpassing IceCube's reach by orders of magnitude. This establishes KM3NeT as a leading facility for quantum-enhanced astroparticle physics.

由于其有利的基线，KM3NeT实验处于独特位置，可实现对惰性中微子振荡和非标准相互作用的量子极限精度探测。未来少数几个事件即可提供首个受基本量子计量学界限约束的结果，在灵敏度上超越IceCube数个数量级。这确立了KM3NeT作为量子增强天体粒子物理领先设施的地位。

Abstract: We investigate a reported discrepancy between a high-energy neutrino detection at KM3NeT and its non-observation at IceCube, which suggests a statistical tension of up to 3.5 standard deviations. This gap has been proposed to arise from sterile neutrino oscillations over the 147-kilometer path to KM3NeT, driven by either matter-induced resonances or nonstandard interactions. Using the Quantum Fisher Information framework, we quantify the sensitivity of the neutrino state to these new physics couplings and establish fundamental precision limits via the quantum Cramer-Rao bound. Our analysis shows that the information available at KM3NeT exceeds that at IceCube by three orders of magnitude for matter-induced scenarios. We demonstrate that IceCube would require over thirty times more events to match the precision of a single KM3NeT detection. We identify an optimal baseline of 150 to 200 kilometers, placing KM3NeT in a superior position for these measurements. Our results show that standard detection methods already reach the ultimate quantum precision limit, and that a small number of future events at KM3NeT could provide the first quantum-limited constraints on sterile neutrino couplings.

### [48] [Lights, Camera, Axion: Tracing Axions from Supernovae in the Diffuse $γ$-ray Sky](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01277)
*Brijesh Kanodia,Debajit Bose,Subhadip Bouri,Ranjan Laha*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper presents a comprehensive framework to compute the diffuse gamma-ray flux from axion-photon conversion in cosmic magnetic fields originating from core-collapse supernovae. For the first time, it consistently models axion production in supernovae and their conversion across multiple astrophysical magnetic environments—progenitor stars, host galaxies, intergalactic medium, and the Milky Way—along with an updated cosmic star formation rate. Using data from COMPTEL, EGRET, and Fermi-LAT, the authors derive competitive bounds on the axion-photon coupling $g_{a\gamma}$ over a broad range of axion masses and forecast sensitivity improvements from future MeV gamma-ray telescopes via Fisher analysis.

本文提出了一个计算来自核心坍缩超新星的轴子-光子转换在宇宙磁场中产生弥散伽马射线通量的综合框架。首次一致地模拟了超新星中的轴子产生及其在多种天体物理磁场环境（包括前身星、宿主星系、星系际介质和银河系）中的光子转换过程，并结合更新的宇宙恒星形成率。利用COMPTEL、EGRET和Fermi-LAT对弥散伽马射线天空的观测数据，推导出在广泛轴子质量范围内对轴子-光子耦合$g_{a\gamma}$具有竞争力的限制，并通过Fisher预报分析预测未来MeV伽马射线望远镜对此信号的灵敏度提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Axions are well-motivated dark matter candidates and may be produced abundantly in the hot cores of supernovae via processes like bremsstrahlung. If axions couple to photons ($g_{a\gamma} \neq 0$), they can convert into detectable gamma rays in astrophysical magnetic fields. While previous studies considered isolated sources or simplified magnetic field models, a complete and consistent treatment of axion propagation and conversion through all relevant large-scale structures has been lacking. Moreover, upcoming MeV gamma-ray observatories (e.g., AMEGO, e-ASTROGAM) will significantly improve sensitivity in an unexplored energy window, motivating robust theoretical predictions for diffuse signals.

轴子是重要的暗物质候选者，可通过轫致辐射等过程在超新星热核中大量产生。若轴子与光子存在耦合（$g_{a\gamma} \neq 0$），其可在天体物理磁场中转换为可探测的伽马射线。以往研究多局限于孤立源或简化的磁场模型，缺乏对轴子在所有相关大尺度结构中传播与转换的一致性处理。此外，即将推出的MeV伽马射线观测设备（如AMEGO、e-ASTROGAM）将在未充分探索的能量窗口显著提升灵敏度，亟需可靠的弥散信号理论预言。

Method: The authors develop a multi-component model for axion production in core-collapse supernovae using thermal emission spectra, then propagate these axions through four distinct magnetic field environments: (1) progenitor stellar magnetosphere, (2) host galaxy ISM, (3) intergalactic medium (IGM), and (4) Milky Way halo. The conversion probability is computed using the full quantum mechanical evolution of the axion-photon system under varying magnetic fields and electron densities, solving the Schrödinger-like equation for the density matrix or amplitude vector. The total diffuse gamma-ray flux is integrated over redshift using an updated cosmic star formation rate (SFR). Constraints on $g_{a\gamma}$ are derived by comparing the predicted flux with measurements from COMPTEL, EGRET, and Fermi-LAT, while forecast sensitivities are obtained via Fisher matrix analysis assuming future instrumental specifications.

作者建立了核心坍缩超新星中轴子产生的多组分模型，基于热辐射谱生成轴子，随后让这些轴子穿过四个不同的磁场环境：(1) 前身星星磁层，(2) 宿主星系ISM，(3) 星系际介质（IGM），以及(4) 银河系晕。使用轴子-光子系统在变化磁场和电子密度下的完整量子力学演化来计算转换概率，求解类薛定谔方程的密度矩阵或振幅矢量。总弥散伽马射线通量通过对更新后的宇宙恒星形成率（SFR）进行红移积分得到。通过将预测通量与COMPTEL、EGRET和Fermi-LAT的测量结果比较，推导出对$g_{a\gamma}$的限制；而未来灵敏度则通过Fisher矩阵分析，假设未来的仪器参数进行预报。

Result: The framework yields precise predictions for the diffuse gamma-ray background from supernova-generated axions, with conversion contributions from each magnetic environment quantified. The analysis sets strong upper limits on the axion-photon coupling $g_{a\gamma} \lesssim \mathcal{O}(10^{-11})\,\mathrm{GeV}^{-1}$ across axion masses $m_a \sim 10^{-10} - 10^{-7}\,\mathrm{eV}$, improving upon previous bounds in certain mass ranges. It is shown that the Milky Way's magnetic field dominates the conversion signal for lighter axions, while extragalactic fields become more relevant at higher masses. Fisher forecasts indicate that next-generation MeV telescopes could improve sensitivity to $g_{a\gamma}$ by up to an order of magnitude, probing deeper into uncharted parameter space.

该框架给出了由超新星产生轴子导致的弥散伽马射线背景的精确预测，并量化了各磁场环境的转换贡献。分析得出在轴子质量范围$m_a \sim 10^{-10} - 10^{-7}\,\mathrm{eV}$内，轴子-光子耦合的强上限$g_{a\gamma} \lesssim \mathcal{O}(10^{-11})\,\mathrm{GeV}^{-1}$，在某些质量区间优于先前限制。研究表明，对于较轻的轴子，银河系磁场主导转换信号，而在较高质量时，河外磁场更为重要。Fisher预报显示，下一代MeV望远镜可将对$g_{a\gamma}$的灵敏度提高近一个数量级，深入探索未被触及的参数空间。

Conclusion: By consistently modeling axion production in supernovae and their conversion across all relevant cosmic magnetic environments, this work provides the most complete theoretical prediction to date for the diffuse gamma-ray signal from axion-photon oscillations. The resulting constraints on $g_{a\gamma}$ are among the strongest in the sub-eV axion mass range and complement laboratory searches. The forecasted reach of upcoming MeV gamma-ray telescopes highlights their potential to discover or rule out axions with significant photon coupling, making this diffuse signal a powerful probe of axion-like particles in a previously underexplored regime.

通过一致地建模超新星中轴子的产生及其在所有相关宇宙磁场环境中的转换，本工作提供了迄今为止最完整的轴子-光子振荡产生弥散伽马射线信号的理论预测。所得对$g_{a\gamma}$的限制在亚电子伏特轴子质量范围内属于最强之列，并补充了实验室搜索。对未来MeV伽马射线望远镜探测能力的预测突显了其发现或排除具有显著光子耦合轴子的潜力，使这一弥散信号成为在先前未充分探索区域探测类轴子粒子的强大工具。

Abstract: Axions produced copiously in core-collapse supernovae can convert into photons as they propagate through various astrophysical magnetic fields. The cumulative emission from the cosmic population of supernovae can therefore generate a diffuse gamma-ray signal through axion-photon conversion. In this work, we develop a comprehensive framework to compute the diffuse gamma-ray flux by modeling axion production in supernovae and, \textit{for the first time}, consistently accounting for their conversion into photons across all relevant magnetic field environments - progenitor, host galaxy, intergalactic medium, and the Milky Way - together with an updated cosmic star formation rate. Using measurements of the diffuse gamma-ray sky from COMPTEL, EGRET, and \textit{Fermi}-LAT, we derive competitive constraints on the axion-photon coupling over a wide range of axion masses. We further forecast the sensitivity of upcoming MeV gamma-ray telescopes to this diffuse signal using a Fisher forecast analysis.

</details>


### [49] [Influence of tides and self-gravity on Ultra-Light Dark Matter Bounds from Dwarf Galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01278)
*Andrea Caputo,Luca Teodori*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: Dwarf spheroidal galaxies are sensitive probes of ultra-light dark matter (ULDM); this study improves constraints by accounting for tidal effects from the Milky Way and stellar self-gravity, finding that ULDM in the mass range $5\times 10^{-22} \lesssim m/{\rm eV} \lesssim 5\times 10^{-21}$ is still in tension with observations.

矮椭球星系是超轻暗物质（ULDM）的灵敏探针；本研究通过考虑银河系的潮汐效应和恒星自引力，改进了对ULDM的限制，发现质量在$5\times 10^{-22} \lesssim m/{\rm eV} \lesssim 5\times 10^{-21}$范围内的ULDM仍与现有观测数据存在张力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Ultra-light dark matter (ULDM) can be probed via dynamical heating in dwarf spheroidal galaxies, but current constraints may be biased due to unaccounted systematics such as tidal interactions with the Milky Way and stellar self-gravity if the stellar component was more compact in the past. This work aims to reduce these systematics to provide more robust constraints.

超轻暗物质（ULDM）可通过矮椭球星系的动力学加热效应来探测，但当前限制可能因未考虑系统误差（如与银河系的潮汐相互作用，或早期更致密的恒星成分引起的自引力）而产生偏差。本研究旨在减少这些系统误差，以提供更可靠的限制。

Method: The authors reconstruct orbital histories of five dwarf galaxies in a Milky-Way potential, introduce a conservative tidal-susceptibility diagnostic to estimate tidal stripping, and include stellar self-gravity explicitly in numerical simulations to assess its impact on ULDM-induced heating.

作者重构了五个矮星系在银河系势场中的轨道历史，引入了一种保守的潮汐敏感性判据以估算潮汐剥离，并在数值模拟中显式包含恒星自引力，以评估其对ULDM诱导加热的影响。

Result: After accounting for tidal effects and stellar self-gravity, ULDM with masses in the range $5\times 10^{-22} \lesssim m/{\rm eV} \lesssim 5\times 10^{-21}$ remains inconsistent with observational data from the studied dwarf galaxies.

在考虑潮汐效应和恒星自引力后，质量在$5\times 10^{-22} \lesssim m/{\rm eV} \lesssim 5\times 10^{-21}$范围内的ULDM仍与所研究矮星系的观测数据不一致。

Conclusion: Despite systematic improvements in modeling tidal interactions and stellar self-gravity, ULDM in the $\sim 10^{-21}\,{\rm eV}$ mass range is still strongly disfavored by kinematic data from dwarf spheroidal galaxies.

尽管在建模潮汐相互作用和恒星自引力方面进行了系统性改进，质量约为$10^{-21}\,{\rm eV}$的ULDM仍被矮椭球星系的运动学数据强烈排除。

Abstract: Dwarf spheroidal galaxies provide some of the most sensitive astrophysical probes of ultra-light dark matter (ULDM), but the inferred constraints can be affected by two important systematics: tidal interactions with the Milky Way, which reduce ULDM-induced dynamical heating, and stellar self-gravity, which can become relevant if the stellar component was more compact at earlier times. In this work, we attempt to estimate both effects by reconstructing dwarf-galaxy orbital histories in a Milky-Way potential, adopting a simple and approximate tidal-susceptibility diagnostic that we argue provides a conservative description of tidal stripping, and explicitly including stellar self-gravity in our numerical simulations. Within our framework, which we apply to five different dwarf galaxies, we find that ULDM with masses $5\times 10^{-22} \lesssim m/{\rm eV} \lesssim 5\times 10^{-21}$ remains in tension with current data.

### [50] [Reconciling hadronic and partonic analyticity in $b\to s\ell\ell$ transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01284)
*Martin Hoferichter,Bastian Kubis,Simon Mutke*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper studies rare $B$-meson decays via $b\to s\ell\ell$ transitions, focusing on nonlocal charm-loop contributions. It shows that the analytic structure of partonic calculations is consistent with dispersion relations, including anomalous thresholds, and matches expectations from hadronic physics, validating the use of perturbative methods in applicable regions.

本文研究了通过$b\to s\ell\ell$跃迁的稀有$B$介子衰变，重点关注非局域的粲夸克圈贡献。研究表明，部分子计算的解析结构（包括反常阈值）满足色散关系，并与强子自由度预期的反常效应匹配，证明了在适用区域使用微扰方法的合理性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Rare $B$-meson decays provide powerful tests for physics beyond the Standard Model (BSM). Discrepancies in $b\to s\ell\ell$ data have raised interest, but precise interpretation requires control over nonlocal matrix elements, particularly charm-loop contributions. A rigorous theoretical treatment demands understanding the analytic properties of these amplitudes, especially near anomalous thresholds, to ensure reliable parameterizations.

稀有$B$介子衰变为检验超出标准模型的新物理提供了强大工具。$b\to s\ell\ell$过程中的实验偏差引发了广泛关注，但精确解释需要对非局域矩阵元（特别是粲夸克圈贡献）进行精确控制。为确保参数化的可靠性，必须深入理解这些振幅的解析性质，尤其是在反常阈值附近的行为。

Method: The authors analyze the analytic structure of the partonic $b\to s\ell\ell$ amplitude using the operator product expansion (OPE) at large spacelike virtualities, known up to two-loop order. They apply dispersion relations to study the amplitude's singularities and examine triangle diagram topologies, showing how anomalous thresholds arise. They then demonstrate consistency between the partonic calculation and expected hadronic behavior by matching the anomalous contributions.

作者利用大类空虚度下的算符乘积展开（OPE）（已知至两圈阶）分析部分子$b\to s\ell\ell$振幅的解析结构。通过应用色散关系研究振幅的奇点，并考察三角图拓扑，揭示反常阈值的产生机制。随后通过匹配反常贡献，证明部分子计算与预期的强子行为一致。

Result: The analysis reveals that the analytic structure of the partonic amplitude, including anomalous thresholds, follows from simple triangle topologies. Dispersion relations are explicitly fulfilled even in the presence of such thresholds. The anomalous contributions in the partonic calculation match those expected from hadronic degrees of freedom, demonstrating that the OPE-based approach captures all relevant nonperturbative effects where applicable.

分析表明，部分子振幅的解析结构（包括反常阈值）源于简单的三角图拓扑。即使存在反常阈值，色散关系仍被明确满足。部分子计算中的反常贡献与强子自由度预期的结果相匹配，证明基于OPE的方法在适用条件下能捕捉所有相关非微扰效应。

Conclusion: The partonic description of $b\to s\ell\ell$ transitions, based on the OPE and two-loop calculations, correctly accounts for the analytic structure of nonlocal matrix elements, including anomalous thresholds. This justifies its use in phenomenological applications, provided the kinematic regime allows a perturbative treatment, and ensures robust parameterizations for BSM searches.

基于OPE和两圈计算的部分子描述能够正确反映$b\to s\ell\ell$跃迁中非局域矩阵元的解析结构，包括反常阈值。只要运动学区域允许微扰处理，该方法可用于唯象学研究，并为新物理探索提供可靠的参数化基础。

Abstract: Rare $B$-meson decays mediated by $b\to s\ell\ell$ transitions constitute sensitive probes of physics beyond the Standard Model, and have triggered considerable interest due to hints for deviations from the Standard-Model prediction. To establish a discrepancy beyond a reasonable doubt, control over the nonlocal matrix elements involving charm loops is essential, which, for large spacelike virtualities, can be constrained by an operator product expansion with coefficients known at two-loop order. We observe that the analytic structure of this partonic calculation, whose understanding is important to put forward rigorous parameterizations, follows from simple triangle topologies and demonstrate explicitly how dispersion relations are fulfilled even in the case of anomalous thresholds. Crucially, these anomalous contributions match onto the ones expected when considering hadronic degrees of freedom, proving that the partonic calculation does not miss anomalous effects and justifying its use in regions of parameter space in which a perturbative description applies.

### [51] [Q-balls across dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01288)
*Dusty Aiello,Julian Heeck*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We study Q-balls—non-topological solitons formed by scalars with conserved charge $Q$—in arbitrary spatial dimensions $d$. In $d=1$, we obtain exact analytical solutions for a broad class of potentials; for $d>1$, we provide analytic approximations in the thin-wall (large $Q$) regime, including the first sub-leading correction. The same differential equations govern vacuum decay bounces, so our results also apply to tunneling processes in field theory.

我们研究了在任意空间维度 $d$ 中的 $Q$-球——由携带守恒荷 $Q$ 的标量场形成的非拓扑孤子。在 $d=1$ 时，我们对一大类单场势获得了精确解析解；在 $d>1$ 时，我们在薄壁（大 $Q$）极限下提供了包含首项次领头阶修正的解析近似解。由于控制方程的形式与真空衰变中的跃迁解相同，我们的结果也可应用于场论中的隧穿过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Non-topological solitons such as Q-balls play important roles in cosmology, particle physics, and mathematical field theory. Understanding their structure across dimensions and for general potentials is crucial for applications ranging from dark matter candidates to vacuum stability analysis. While numerical methods are often used, analytical insights—especially beyond leading-order thin-wall approximations—are scarce. We aim to fill this gap by providing exact and improved analytic solutions, particularly in physically relevant limits.

非拓扑孤子如 $Q$-球在宇宙学、粒子物理和数学场论中具有重要作用。理解它们在不同维度及一般势下的结构对于从暗物质候选者到真空稳定性分析等应用至关重要。尽管通常使用数值方法，但解析见解——尤其是超越领头阶薄壁近似的——仍然稀缺。我们的目标是通过在物理上重要的极限下提供精确且改进的解析解来填补这一空白。

Method: We analyze the classical equations of motion for a complex scalar field with a global $U(1)$ symmetry and conserved charge $Q$, minimizing energy at fixed charge. For $d=1$, we solve the resulting non-linear ODE exactly using first integrals and potential-specific ansätze. For $d > 1$, we employ the thin-wall approximation, expanding around the large-$Q$ limit and computing the first sub-leading correction by consistently solving the radial profile equation perturbatively. The same formalism applies to $O(d+1)$-symmetric bounce solutions in vacuum decay.

我们分析具有全局 $U(1)$ 对称性和守恒荷 $Q$ 的复标量场的经典运动方程，在固定电荷下最小化能量。对于 $d=1$，我们利用首次积分和特定势的试探解精确求解所得的非线性常微分方程。对于 $d > 1$，我们采用薄壁近似，在大 $Q$ 极限附近展开，并通过微扰一致求解径向轮廓方程计算首项次领头阶修正。相同的框架也适用于真空衰变中 $O(d+1)$ 对称的跃迁解。

Result: For $d=1$, we derive exact analytic expressions for the Q-ball profile, energy, and charge for a wide class of potentials (e.g., polynomial or logarithmic). For $d>1$, we obtain an improved thin-wall formula for the Q-ball energy: $E(Q) \approx \sigma S_d R^{d-1} - \gamma Q + \mathcal{O}(1/Q)$, where $R \sim Q^{1/d}$ is the radius, $S_d$ is the unit sphere area, and $\gamma$ encodes the sub-leading correction. We explicitly compute $\gamma$ for various potentials. Our approach systematically improves over standard thin-wall results and matches well with numerical solutions when available. The correspondence to bounce actions allows us to refine vacuum decay rate estimates.

对于 $d=1$，我们为一大类势（例如多项式或对数势）推导出 $Q$-球轮廓、能量和电荷的精确解析表达式。对于 $d>1$，我们得到改进的薄壁能量公式：$E(Q) \approx \sigma S_d R^{d-1} - \gamma Q + \mathcal{O}(1/Q)$，其中 $R \sim Q^{1/d}$ 是半径，$S_d$ 是单位球面积，$\gamma$ 包含次领头阶修正。我们显式计算了多种势下的 $\gamma$。我们的方法系统性地改进了标准薄壁结果，并在有数值解时与之吻合良好。与跃迁作用量的对应关系使我们能够改进真空衰变率的估计。

Conclusion: We have provided exact and systematically improvable analytic solutions for Q-balls in arbitrary dimensions. These results enhance theoretical control over non-topological solitons and have direct implications for vacuum decay in quantum and thermal field theories. The inclusion of sub-leading corrections improves precision in energy and lifetime calculations, which is essential for phenomenological applications such as dark matter abundance or metastable vacuum scenarios.

我们为任意维度中的 $Q$-球提供了精确且可系统改进的解析解。这些结果增强了对非拓扑孤子的理论掌控，并对量子和热场论中的真空衰变具有直接意义。包含次领头阶修正提高了能量和寿命计算的精度，这对于暗物质丰度或亚稳真空情景等现象学应用至关重要。

Abstract: Scalars carrying a conserved global charge $Q$ can form stable localized field configurations composed of a large number of particles. These non-topological solitons are spherically symmetric and are called Q-balls. While usually analyzed in three spatial dimensions, these solitons can be straightforwardly generalized to $d$ spatial dimensions. For $d=1$, we can analytically solve the non-linear differential equation for an important class of single-field potentials; for $d>1$, we can analytically approximate the solutions in the thin-wall or large Q-ball regime, including the first sub-leading correction consistently. Since the underlying differential equations have the same form as vacuum-decay bounce solutions, our results find applications there, too.

</details>


### [52] [High-Frequency Gravitational Wave Constraints from Graviton-Photon Conversion in the M87 Galaxy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01290)
*Aman Gupta,Pratik Majumdar,Sourov Roy,Pratick Sarkar*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This study investigates high-frequency gravitational waves (HFGWs) in the $f \gtrsim 10^{10}~\mathrm{Hz}$ range via the inverse Gertsenshtein effect, where gravitons convert to photons in magnetic fields. Using M87's magnetic field and plasma models, and its broadband electromagnetic spectrum (mm to TeV gamma rays), the absence of excess emission leads to improved upper limits on HFGW strain amplitude $h_c$ and energy density $Ω_{\mathrm{gw}} h^2$, surpassing Milky Way-based bounds by 1–5 orders of magnitude.

本研究通过逆格策施泰因效应（引力子在磁场中转化为光子）研究高频引力波（HFGW），频段为 $f \gtrsim 10^{10}~\mathrm{Hz}$。利用M87星系的磁场与等离子体模型及其从毫米波到TeV伽马射线的宽波段电磁谱，未发现超出辐射，从而对HFGW的应变振幅 $h_c$ 和能量密度 $Ω_{\mathrm{gw}} h^2$ 给出了更严格的上限，比基于银河系磁场的现有约束强1至5个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: High-frequency gravitational waves (HFGWs) at $f \gtrsim 10^{10}~\mathrm{Hz}$ are inaccessible to current direct detection methods (e.g., interferometers), yet they may carry signatures of new physics beyond the Standard Model, such as early universe phase transitions or exotic particle decays. Indirect detection via graviton-to-photon conversion in astrophysical magnetic fields offers a viable alternative. The motivation is to exploit the strong magnetic environments of nearby active galaxies like M87 to improve sensitivity beyond current limits set by Milky Way-based analyses.

高频引力波（$f \gtrsim 10^{10}~\mathrm{Hz}$）无法通过当前直接探测手段（如干涉仪）观测，但可能携带超出标准模型的新物理信号，例如早期宇宙相变或奇异粒子衰变。通过天体物理磁场中的引力子-光子转换进行间接探测是一种可行替代方案。动机是利用邻近活动星系（如M87）的强磁场环境，提升灵敏度，超越基于银河系分析的现有极限。

Method: The analysis employs the inverse Gertsenshtein effect, modeling graviton-photon conversion in the magnetized plasma of M87. Realistic profiles for the large-scale magnetic field and plasma electron density are used, based on observational and theoretical models. The resulting photon flux from converted gravitons is computed across frequencies $10^{10}$–$10^{27}~\mathrm{Hz}$, and compared to the observed broadband electromagnetic spectrum of M87 (from ALMA, Chandra, H.E.S.S., etc.). The absence of unexplained excess emission sets upper limits on the gravitational wave background through Bayesian or frequentist statistical inference.

该分析采用逆格策施泰因效应，建模M87磁化等离子体中的引力子-光子转换。使用基于观测与理论模型的大尺度磁场和等离子体电子密度分布。计算从$10^{10}$到$10^{27}~\mathrm{Hz}$频段内由引力子转换产生的光子通量，并与M87的宽波段电磁观测数据（来自ALMA、Chandra、H.E.S.S.等）对比。通过贝叶斯或频率主义统计推断，未发现异常超出辐射，从而设定引力波背景的上限。

Result: In the frequency range $10^{10}$–$10^{27}~\mathrm{Hz}$, the non-detection of excess electromagnetic emission allows us to derive stringent upper bounds on the characteristic strain amplitude $h_c$ and the spectral energy density $Ω_{\mathrm{gw}} h^2$ of stochastic high-frequency gravitational wave backgrounds. These constraints improve upon previous limits from Milky Way magnetic field studies by 1 to 5 orders of magnitude, depending on frequency, particularly in the $10^{14}$–$10^{20}~\mathrm{Hz}$ range where plasma suppression effects are minimized.

在$10^{10}$–$10^{27}~\mathrm{Hz}$频段内，未探测到多余的电磁辐射，使我们得以对随机高频引力波背景的特征应变振幅 $h_c$ 和谱能量密度 $Ω_{\mathrm{gw}} h^2$ 设定严格上限。这些约束比基于银河系磁场的研究结果提升了1至5个数量级，尤其在$10^{14}$–$10^{20}~\mathrm{Hz}$频段，等离子体抑制效应最小，限制最强。

Conclusion: The use of M87's intense and structured magnetic environment provides a significantly more sensitive probe for high-frequency gravitational waves than the Milky Way. This work demonstrates that indirect searches via graviton-photon conversion in external galaxies are a powerful strategy for constraining beyond-Standard-Model physics. Future observations with next-generation radio and gamma-ray telescopes could further improve these bounds or potentially detect a signal.

利用M87强烈且结构化的磁场环境，比银河系对高频引力波的探测更为敏感。本研究表明，通过外部星系中的引力子-光子转换进行间接搜索，是约束超出标准模型物理的有力策略。下一代射电与伽马射线望远镜的未来观测可进一步改善这些限制，甚至可能探测到信号。

Abstract: High-frequency gravitational waves, particularly in the range $f \gtrsim 10^{10}~\mathrm{Hz}$, represent a compelling probe of physics beyond the Standard Model. Due to the absence of direct detection methods in this frequency regime, alternative strategies may be pursued. One promising approach involves the conversion of gravitons into photons in the presence of magnetic fields, a process known as the inverse Gertsenshtein effect. In this study, we explore such graviton-to-photon conversions occurring within the magnetic field environment of the M87 galaxy, utilizing realistic models for the galactic magnetic field and plasma density structure. We use the broadband electromagnetic spectrum of M87, ranging from millimeter to TeV gamma rays, to search for hidden contributions from graviton-photon conversions. In the well-constrained frequency range $10^{10}$-$10^{27}~\mathrm{Hz}$, the lack of excess emission allows us to place improved bounds on the gravitational wave strain amplitude $h_c$ or on spectral energy density $Ω_{\mathrm{gw}} h^2$. We find that our results from M87 yield substantially stronger constraints compared to existing bounds derived from Milky Way magnetic field considerations, with improvements ranging from one to five orders of magnitude depending on the frequency band, thereby enhancing the prospects for probing high-frequency gravitational wave backgrounds through indirect electromagnetic signatures.

### [53] [Supermassive Primordial Black Holes from a Catalyzed Dark Phase Transition for Little Red Dots](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01304)
*Jinhui Guo,Jia Liu,Masanori Tanaka,Xiao-Ping Wang,Huangyu Xiao*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper proposes that supermassive primordial black holes (SMPBHs) formed in a dark sector via domain wall-catalyzed first-order phase transitions can explain the unexpectedly abundant high-redshift Little Red Dots (LRDs) observed by JWST. This mechanism naturally produces $ M_{\rm PBH} \sim \mathcal{O}(10^{10}) M_\odot $ seeds without conflicting with cosmological constraints and predicts a detectable ultra-low-frequency gravitational-wave background.

本文提出，通过畴壁催化暗区一阶相变形成的超大质量原初黑洞（SMPBHs）可以解释JWST观测到的高红移‘小红点’（LRDs）。该机制自然产生$ M_{\rm PBH} \sim \mathcal{O}(10^{10}) M_\odot $量级的种子黑洞，不与宇宙学约束冲突，并预言了可探测的极低频引力波背景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: JWST observations have revealed numerous compact, low-metallicity LRDs at high redshifts, which are difficult to reconcile with standard SMBH formation models starting from stellar-mass seeds. These objects suggest early, rapid growth of SMBHs, motivating alternative origins such as primordial black holes formed in a hidden dark sector.

JWST观测发现大量高红移、致密且低金属丰度的小红点（LRDs），这与从恒星质量种子开始的标准超大质量黑洞（SMBH）形成模型难以兼容。这些天体暗示SMBH早期快速成长，促使人们探索隐藏暗区中原初黑洞等替代性起源。

Method: The authors introduce a first-order phase transition in a decoupled dark sector, where domain walls (DWs) catalyze the transition. Due to DW dynamics and statistics, rare false-vacuum regions survive longer and eventually collapse into supermassive primordial black holes (SMPBHs). They compute the resulting PBH mass distribution and abundance, and analyze associated cosmological signatures, including $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$, curvature perturbations, and stochastic gravitational-wave backgrounds.

作者引入一个退耦暗区中由畴壁（DW）催化的**一阶相变**。由于DW的动力学与统计特性，稀有的伪真空区域存活得更久并最终坍缩成超大质量原初黑洞（SMPBHs）。他们计算了由此产生的PBH质量分布与丰度，并分析相关的宇宙学信号，包括$\Delta N_{\rm eff}$、曲率扰动和随机引力波背景。

Result: The model produces SMPBHs with masses up to $M_{\rm PBH}\sim \mathcal{O}(10^{10})M_\odot$, sufficient to seed the observed LRD population. The mechanism avoids conflicts with phase transition completion and observational bounds on $\Delta N_{\rm eff}$ and scalar perturbations. It also generates an ultra-low-frequency stochastic gravitational-wave background peaking in the pulsar-timing array (PTA) range, offering a testable prediction.

该模型产生质量高达$M_{\rm PBH}\sim \mathcal{O}(10^{10})M_\odot$的SMPBH，足以作为观测到的LRD种群的种子。该机制避免了与相变完成、$\Delta N_{\rm eff}$及标量扰动观测限之间的冲突，同时生成一个在脉冲星计时阵列（PTA）频段达到峰值的极低频随机引力波背景，提供了可检验的预言。

Conclusion: Supermassive primordial black holes formed via domain-wall-catalyzed phase transitions in a dark sector offer a viable origin for high-redshift LRDs. This scenario links the early formation of SMBHs to new physics in a hidden sector and predicts observable gravitational waves within reach of current PTA experiments.

通过暗区中畴壁催化的相变形成超大质量原初黑洞，为高红移LRDs提供了一个可行的起源。该情景将SMBH的早期形成与隐藏 sector 中的新物理联系起来，并预言当前PTA实验可探测的引力波信号。

Abstract: JWST has revealed an abundant population of compact, low-metallicity "Little Red Dots" (LRDs) at high redshift, challenging conventional scenarios in which supermassive black holes (SMBHs) grow from stellar-mass seeds. We consider a scenario in which the SMBHs are instead supermassive primordial black holes (SMPBHs), formed directly in a decoupled, subdominant dark sector undergoing a first-order phase transition. Unlike conventional stochastic phase transitions, our mechanism is based on the catalysis by domain walls (DWs): most of the Universe completes the transition rapidly, while rare long-lived false-vacuum domains survive because of DW statistics and collapse into PBHs. This mechanism naturally yields SMPBH seeds with masses up to $M_{\rm PBH}\sim \mathcal{O}(10^{10}) M_\odot$, whose abundance can account for the observed LRD population. It also avoids the usual tensions with phase transition completion, $ΔN_{\rm eff}$, and large curvature perturbations. The dark phase transition simultaneously generates an ultra-low-frequency stochastic gravitational-wave background peaking near the pulsar-timing-array range, providing a test of this dark-sector origin of LRDs.

</details>


### [54] [Bipartite Solution to the Lithium Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01324)
*Sougata Ganguly,Tae Hyun Jung,Tae-Sun Park,Chang Sub Shin*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: A two-step late-decay scenario involving a majoron and an axion-like particle is proposed to solve the primordial lithium problem without violating deuterium constraints: the majoron decay increases neutrons to reduce lithium, while the subsequent photodissociation from axion decay corrects the overproduced deuterium.

一个包含主要子（majoron）和类轴子粒子（axion-like particle）的两步晚期衰变模型被提出以解决原初锂问题，同时满足氘丰度限制：主要子衰变通过增加中子数减少锂产量，随后类轴子衰变引发的晚期光致裂解则修正过量的氘，而不破坏此前的锂减少效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The primordial lithium problem—the discrepancy between predicted and observed $^7\mathrm{Li}$ abundances in Big Bang nucleosynthesis (BBN)—motivates new physics, but attempts to reduce lithium are tightly constrained by the precisely measured deuterium abundance. A viable solution must therefore simultaneously modify light-element yields in a correlated way that reduces lithium without overproducing deuterium.

原初锂问题——大爆炸核合成（BBN）中预测与观测到的$^7\mathrm{Li}$丰度之间的差异——促使人们探索新物理；然而，由于氘丰度已被精确测量，任何试图降低锂丰度的模型都受到强烈限制。因此，可行的解决方案必须以一种相关联的方式同时调整轻元素丰度，在不导致氘过量的前提下减少锂。

Method: The study proposes a two-step late-decay model: (1) A majoron with lifetime $τ_J \sim 10\,\text{--}\,10^4\,\mathrm{sec}$ decays mainly into neutrinos, enhancing the neutron-to-proton ratio and thus increasing neutron capture during BBN, which reduces $^{7}\mathrm{Li}+{}^{7}\mathrm{Be}$; (2) An axion-like particle with longer lifetime $τ_φ\gtrsim 10^5\,\mathrm{sec}$ decays into photons, triggering late-time photodissociation of deuterium to counteract its overproduction from the first step, without significantly affecting lithium. The evolution of light-element abundances is computed by modifying standard BBN reaction networks to include these energy injections.

该研究提出了一个两步晚期衰变模型：(1) 一个寿命为$τ_J \sim 10\,\text{--}\,10^4\,\mathrm{sec}$的主要子主要衰变为中微子，提高中子质子比，从而增强BBN期间的中子俘获，减少$^{7}\mathrm{Li}+{}^{7}\mathrm{Be}$产量；(2) 一个寿命更长（$τ_φ\gtrsim 10^5\,\mathrm{sec}$）的类轴子粒子衰变为光子，引发晚期光致裂解以抵消第一步造成的氘过量，而对锂影响较小。通过修改标准BBN反应网络以包含这些能量注入过程，计算了轻元素丰度的演化。

Result: The majoron decay successfully reduces $^{7}\mathrm{Li}+{}^{7}\mathrm{Be}$ abundance by increasing pre-BBN neutron availability, but causes deuterium overproduction beyond observational limits. The subsequent axion-induced photodissociation selectively reduces deuterium to within allowed bounds, preserving the lithium reduction and even further suppressing $^{7}\mathrm{Li}+{}^{7}\mathrm{Be}$ via secondary reactions. This two-stage mechanism demonstrates a consistent pathway to reconcile reduced lithium with precise deuterium observations.

主要子衰变通过增加BBN前的中子数量成功减少了$^{7}\mathrm{Li}+{}^{7}\mathrm{Be}$丰度，但导致氘过量超出观测容许范围。随后由类轴子引发的光致裂解选择性地将氘降至允许范围内，保留了锂的减少效果，并通过次级反应进一步抑制$^{7}\mathrm{Li}+{}^{7}\mathrm{Be}$。这种两阶段机制展示了一条一致的路径，使降低的锂丰度与精确的氘观测相协调。

Conclusion: A single late-decaying particle cannot easily satisfy both lithium reduction and deuterium constraints due to their opposing responses; however, a multi-stage decay scenario with distinct epochs and channels—such as neutrino-producing early decay followed by photon-mediated late photodissociation—can achieve the required correlated abundance shifts. This proof-of-concept model underscores the need for complex, multi-component new physics scenarios in resolving the lithium problem while respecting precision BBN constraints.

单一晚期衰变粒子难以同时满足锂减少和氘约束，因为二者响应相反；然而，具有不同时间尺度和衰变通道的多阶段衰变场景——如早期产生中微子的衰变后接晚期光子介导的光致裂解——可以实现所需的丰度关联变化。这一概念验证模型强调了解决锂问题时，在尊重精确BBN约束的同时，需要复杂的多组分新物理场景。

Abstract: The primordial lithium problem remains a persistent motivation for new-physics modifications of Big Bang nucleosynthesis, yet the precision of the observed deuterium abundance now places strong constraints on such attempts. This indicates that the challenge is not simply to reduce $^{7}\mathrm{Li}$, but to realize the correlated shifts among light-element abundances required to do so without spoiling deuterium. We investigate this issue in a concrete two-step decay scenario involving two unstable particles undergoing sequential late decays. In the first stage, a majoron with lifetime $τ_J \sim 10\,\text{--}\,10^4\,\mathrm{sec}$ decays predominantly into neutrinos, increasing the neutron abundance and thereby reducing the primordial $^{7}\mathrm{Li}+\!{}^{7}\mathrm{Be}$ yield. This mechanism, however, simultaneously drives deuterium above the observationally allowed range. In the second stage, an axion-like particle with a longer lifetime $τ_φ\gtrsim 10^5\,\mathrm{sec}$ decays into photons, inducing late-time photodissociation that compensates the excess deuterium without erasing the earlier reduction of lithium, while further amplifying the depletion of $^{7}\mathrm{Li}+\!{}^{7}\mathrm{Be}$. Although the setup is model-dependent, it serves as an explicit proof of concept that the lithium abundance can be lowered consistently with current deuterium constraints. More broadly, our analysis highlights that a viable resolution may require a nontrivial combination of decay channels and decay epochs, and clarifies the pattern of abundance response that successful late-decay scenarios must achieve.

### [55] [A model independent method for measurement of $B^{\pm}$ and $B^0$ meson production fractions at $Υ(4S)$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01394)
*Murad Yasaveev,Pavel Pakhlov,Nikolai Peters,Alena Mufazalova*

TL;DR: A model-independent method is proposed to directly measure the production fractions of $\Upsilon(4S) \to B^+ B^-$ and $\Upsilon(4S) \to B^0 \bar{B}^0$ at $B$ factories by counting single- and double-inclusive charmed meson events, enabling statistical tagging without theoretical assumptions.

提出了一种不依赖模型的方法，通过统计单举和双举含粲介子事例，直接测量 $\Upsilon(4S) \to B^+ B^-$ 和 $\Upsilon(4S) \to B^0 \bar{B}^0$ 的产生分数，无需理论假设即可实现统计标记。

  <summary>Details</summary>

This work aims to eliminate such dependencies by developing a direct, model-independent measurement technique based solely on event yields.

精确测定 $\Upsilon(4S) \to B^+ B^-$ 和 $\Upsilon(4S) \to B^0 \bar{B}^0$ 产生分数对 $B$ 物理的准确测量至关重要，但现有方法常依赖模型假设。本研究旨在通过仅基于事例产额的方法，建立一种直接且不依赖模型的技术来消除此类依赖性。

Method: The method utilizes inclusive charmed meson ($D$ meson) reconstruction in $\Upsilon(4S)$ decays: by measuring the yields of single- and double-tagged $D$ mesons, the relative contributions of $B^+B^-$ and $B^0\bar{B}^0$ events are statistically separated. The approach relies on known branching ratios and does not require assumptions about hadronization dynamics or production mechanisms.

该方法利用在 $\Upsilon(4S)$ 衰变中重建包含性 $D$ 介子：通过测量单标记和双标记 $D$ 介子的事例产额，统计分离 $B^+B^-$ 和 $B^0\bar{B}^0$ 事件的相对贡献。该方法依赖已知的分支比，无需对强子化动力学或产生机制做额外假设。

Result: A feasibility study demonstrates that the proposed method can achieve a precision comparable to the current world average for the production fractions $f^{+-}$ and $f^{00}$, with purely statistical uncertainties derived from event counts. No significant systematic biases are introduced due to its model-independent nature.

可行性研究表明，该方法在 $f^{+-}$ 和 $f^{00}$ 的测量精度上可达到与当前世界平均值相当的水平，其不确定性完全由事例计数的统计涨落决定。由于其不依赖模型的特性，未引入显著的系统偏差。

Conclusion: This model-independent approach provides a robust and direct way to measure $\Upsilon(4S)$ production fractions using only experimental event yields, enhancing the reliability of $B$ physics analyses at $B$ factories.

这种不依赖模型的方法仅利用实验事例产额即可稳健、直接地测量 $\Upsilon(4S)$ 产生分数，提高了 $B$ 工厂中 $B$ 物理分析的可靠性。

Abstract: This paper presents a detailed description of a model-independent method for the direct measurement of the $Υ(4S) \to B^+ B^-$ and $Υ(4S) \to B^0 \bar{B}^0$ production fractions at $B$ factories. The method is based on counting single- and double-inclusive charmed meson production at the $Υ(4S)$ resonance, providing statistical tagging of $B^0\bar{B}^0$ and $B^+B^-$ events. A feasibility study indicates that a precision comparable to the current world average can be achieved without making any underlying assumptions, as the calculations rely solely on event yields.

### [56] [Quark masses and mixing from Modular $S'_4$ with Canonical Kähler Effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01422)
*Ivo de Medeiros Varzielas,Manuel Paiva*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: A quark flavor model based on modular $S'_4$ symmetry with general CP is proposed, where CP violation arises solely from the modulus $\langle \tau \rangle$. The Kähler metric's canonical normalization enables realistic quark mass hierarchies with $\mathcal{O}(1)$ couplings, and the model achieves excellent agreement with GUT-scale extrapolated PDG 2024 data.

基于模形式$S'_4$对称性与广义CP对称性的夸克味模型被提出，其中CP破坏完全来源于模参数$\langle \tau \rangle$。Kähler度规的规范归一化使得在保持耦合常数为$\mathcal{O}(1)$的同时再现了观测到的质量等级，并且该模型在GUT尺度下对PDG 2024数据实现了极好的拟合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Explaining the observed quark mass hierarchies and mixing patterns within a unified framework that naturally incorporates CP violation remains a major challenge in flavor physics. Modular symmetries offer a promising avenue by reducing the number of free parameters and geometrizing flavor structure through the modulus $\tau$. We aim to construct a minimal, predictive model where all CP violation originates from the vacuum expectation value of $\tau$, avoiding ad hoc complex coupling constants.

解释夸克质量等级和混合模式并自然包含CP破坏是味物理中的主要挑战。模对称性通过模参数$\tau$将味结构几何化并减少自由参数数量，提供了一条有前景的路径。我们的目标是构建一个最小且可预测的模型，其中所有CP破坏均来自$\tau$的真空期望值，避免人为引入复数耦合常数。

Method: We employ a modular $S'_4$ symmetry combined with a generalized CP symmetry in the quark sector. The Yukawa couplings are modular forms of weight 2, functions of the complex modulus $\tau$. Canonical normalization of fields is performed using the Kähler metric, which significantly affects the structure of the mass matrices. Parameters are fitted to experimental data extrapolated to the GUT scale (PDG 2024), treating $\langle \tau \rangle$ as the sole source of CP violation.

我们在夸克部门采用模$S'_4$对称性结合广义CP对称性。汤川耦合是权为2的模形式，依赖于复模参数$\tau$。利用Kähler度规对场进行规范归一化，这对质量矩阵的结构有显著影响。将参数拟合到外推至GUT尺度的实验数据（PDG 2024），并将$\langle \tau \rangle$视为唯一的CP破坏来源。

Result: The minimal model successfully reproduces the quark mass ratios, mixing angles, and the CP-violating phase with high precision. The best-fit value for the modulus is $\langle \tau \rangle \approx 0.78 + 3.6i$, yielding a Jarlskog invariant $J_{\text{CP}} \simeq 3 \times 10^{-5}$, in excellent agreement with observations. All dimensionless couplings remain of $\mathcal{O}(1)$, demonstrating the model's naturalness.

该最小模型以高精度成功再现了夸克质量比、混合角以及CP破坏相位。模参数的最佳拟合值为$\langle \tau \rangle \approx 0.78 + 3.6i$，得到Jarlskog不变量$J_{\text{CP}} \simeq 3 \times 10^{-5}$，与观测值高度一致。所有无量纲耦合均为$\mathcal{O}(1)$量级，体现了模型的自然性。

Conclusion: The modular $S'_4$ framework with generalized CP provides a compelling explanation of quark flavor structures, where all CP violation stems from the modulus $\langle \tau \rangle$. The inclusion of Kähler metric effects is essential for achieving realistic hierarchies without fine-tuning. This approach represents a significant step toward a geometric and predictive theory of flavor.

具有广义CP的模$S'_4$框架为夸克味结构提供了有力解释，所有CP破坏均源于模$\langle \tau \rangle$。Kähler度规效应的引入对于在无需精细调节的情况下实现真实质量等级至关重要。该方法代表了迈向几何化且可预测的味理论的重要一步。

Abstract: We propose a quark flavor model based on modular $S'_4$ with a general CP symmetry. CP violation in the quark sector is entirely realized by the modulus $\langle τ\rangle$. We show that the canonical normalization induced by the Kähler metric plays a crucial role in reproducing the observed hierarchies, while maintaining coupling constants of order $\mathcal{O}(1)$. The minimal model achieves a great fit to the quark sector data, which we take as the PDG 2024 data extrapolated to the GUT scale.

### [57] [New physics in multi-lepton tau decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01465)

These models include kinetically mixed dark photons, gauged $L_i-L_j$, and chiral $U(1)'$ extensions, where flavor violation at high scales enables new experimental signatures with multiple reconstructable resonances.

暗粒子与陶轻子具有轻子味破坏耦合，可触发衰变级联，导致罕见的多体陶轻子衰变，例如 $\tau \to 5\mu$、$\tau \to 3\mu\,2e$ 和 $\tau \to \mu\,4\pi$，这些衰变在传统信号如 $\tau \to 3\mu$ 之上占主导地位。研究的模型包括动力学混合暗光子、规范化的 $L_i-L_j$ 模型和手性 $U(1)'$ 扩展，在高能标下味破坏使得具有多个可重建共振的新实验信号成为可能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The motivation is to explore new physics beyond the Standard Model through lepton-flavor-violating (LFV) decays of the $\tau$ lepton induced by dark sector particles. Traditional searches focus on simple LFV modes like $\tau \to 3\mu$, but more complex, higher-multiplicity final states from dark sector cascades may dominate and remain unexplored experimentally. This work aims to identify promising new signatures for current and future experiments.

动机是通过暗区粒子引发的陶轻子轻子味破坏（LFV）衰变来探索超出标准模型的新物理。传统搜索集中于简单的LFV模式如 $\tau \to 3\mu$，而来自暗区级联的更复杂、更高重数的末态可能占主导但尚未被实验探索。本工作旨在为当前和未来的实验识别有前景的新信号。

Method: The authors study several benchmark models including kinetically mixed dark photons, gauged $L_i-L_j$ symmetries, and chiral $U(1)'$ extensions. They analyze decay chains initiated by $\tau^\pm \to \ell^\pm\,\phi$, where $\phi$ is a light dark sector particle, followed by cascading decays terminating in visible final states (electrons, muons, pions). Branching ratios are estimated using effective couplings and kinematic considerations. The phenomenology of fully visible multi-body decays such as $\tau \to 5\mu$, $\tau \to 3\mu\,2e$, and hadronic channels like $\tau \to \mu\,4\pi$ is systematically surveyed.

作者研究了几个基准模型，包括动力学混合暗光子、规范化的 $L_i-L_j$ 对称性和手性 $U(1)'$ 扩展。他们分析了由 $\tau^\pm \to \ell^\pm\,\phi$ 引发的衰变链，其中 $\phi$ 是一个轻的暗区粒子，随后发生级联衰变并终止于可见末态（电子、μ子、π介子）。利用有效耦合和运动学考虑估算分支比，并系统地调查了如 $\tau \to 5\mu$、$\tau \to 3\mu\,2e$ 和 $\tau \to \mu\,4\pi$ 等完全可见多体衰变的现象学。

Result: In these models, multi-body $\tau$ decays such as $\tau \to 5\mu$, $\tau \to 3\mu\,2e$, $\tau \to \mu\,4e$, and hadronic modes like $\tau \to \mu\,4\pi$ often dominate over simpler channels like $\tau \to 3\mu$. The presence of reconstructable resonances enhances detectability. Even models with missing energy from neutrino final states (e.g., in gauged $L_i-L_j$) still allow for significant fully visible signals. Experimental sensitivity could be improved by targeting these novel high-multiplicity channels.

在这些模型中，多体 $\tau$ 衰变如 $\tau \to 5\mu$、$\tau \to 3\mu\,2e$、$\tau \to \mu\,4e$ 和强子模式如 $\tau \to \mu\,4\pi$ 通常主导于 $\tau \to 3\mu$ 等简单通道。可重建共振的存在增强了可探测性。即使是从中微子末态产生缺失能量的模型（例如在规范化的 $L_i-L_j$ 中），仍允许显著的全可见信号。通过针对这些新的高重数通道，实验灵敏度可以得到提升。

Conclusion: Lepton-flavor-violating dark sector models can lead to dominant, high-multiplicity $\tau$ decay signatures that have not been thoroughly searched for. These include striking final states with multiple muons, electrons, or pions, offering new discovery opportunities at $B$-factories and high-luminosity colliders. Searches should be expanded beyond traditional $\tau \to 3\mu$-like channels to exploit the full reach of flavor-violating new physics.

轻子味破坏的暗区模型可能导致主导性的高重数 $\tau$ 衰变信号，这些信号尚未被充分搜索。其中包括具有多个μ子、电子或π介子的显著末态，为 $B$ 厂和高亮度对撞机提供了新的发现机会。应将搜索范围扩展到传统的 $\tau \to 3\mu$ 类似通道之外，以充分利用味破坏新物理的全部潜力。

Abstract: Dark particles with lepton-flavor-violating couplings to the tau lepton can induce rare neutrinoless $τ$ decays with large final state multiplicities. We study models where transitions of the type $τ^\pm\to \ell^\pm\,φ$, with $φ$ a light new particle, initiate a chain of decays in the dark sector that terminate with decays into electrons, muons, or pions. These decay cascades appear as rare five or even seven-body $τ$ decays with multiple reconstructable resonances. We survey several representative models: kinetically mixed dark photon, gauged $L_i-L_j$ models, and other more exotic charge assignments such as chiral $U(1)'$ extensions of the Standard Model. The main new ingredient is the possibility of flavor violation at very high scales. In these models, a number of channels that have not yet been searched for experimentally, such as $τ\to 5μ$, $τ\to 3μ\,2e$, $τ\to μ\,4e$, and hadronic channels like $τ\to μ\,4π$, typically dominate over the previously-considered signatures such as $τ\to 3μ$. While some of the models, such as the gauged $L_i-L_j$ ones, also contain more challenging channels with missing energy due to decays to neutrinos, they can still be searched for via fully visible channels.

### [58] [Vacuum bubbles from cosmic ripples](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01516)
*Zi-Yan Yuwen,Rong-Gen Cai,Shao-Jiang Wang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper studies vacuum decay in the early Universe influenced by curvature perturbations, finding that over-densities enhance decay rates by reducing the critical bubble radius, both analytically (thin-wall) and numerically (thick-wall).

本文研究了早期宇宙中曲率扰动影响下的真空衰变，发现高密度区域通过减小临界气泡半径来增强衰变率，这一结论在薄壁近似下解析成立，并在厚壁情况下通过数值求解得到验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

The authors aim to determine whether local density fluctuations—particularly over-densities—can trigger vacuum decay earlier than expected in homogeneous backgrounds.

理解宇宙学扰动如何影响真空稳定性对于评估暴胀或早期宇宙场景中亚稳态真空寿命至关重要。作者旨在确定局部密度涨落（特别是过密区）是否会在均匀背景之上更早地触发真空衰变。

Method: Using the thin-wall approximation, they analytically derive corrections to the bounce solution and decay rate due to curvature perturbations. For general cases beyond this limit, they numerically solve the Euclidean equations of motion to obtain bounce solutions and compute the associated on-shell Euclidean action $S_E$ to evaluate tunneling probabilities.

在薄壁近似下，他们解析推导了由于曲率扰动对bounce解和衰变率的修正。对于超出该近似的普遍情况，他们数值求解欧几里得运动方程以获得bouncе解，并计算相应的壳上欧几里得作用量$S_E$来评估隧穿概率。

Result: For small perturbations, over-densities reduce the initial bubble radius and enhance vacuum decay, while under-densities suppress it. In the large-perturbation regime, the bounce solution exhibits an oscillatory middle stage near the bubble wall. Numerical results confirm the analytic predictions in the thin-wall limit and extend them to thick-wall scenarios.

对于小扰动，过密区会减小初始气泡半径并增强真空衰变，而欠密区则抑制衰变。在大扰动区域，bouncе解在气泡壁附近表现出振荡的中间阶段。数值结果证实了薄壁极限下的解析预测，并将其推广到厚壁情形。

Conclusion: Over-densities generically facilitate vacuum decay in the early Universe by lowering the energy barrier for nucleation, implying that cosmological perturbations must be accounted for when estimating vacuum stability.

过密区通常通过降低成核的能量势垒来促进早期宇宙中的真空衰变，这意味着在估计真空稳定性时必须考虑宇宙学扰动的影响。

Abstract: We investigate vacuum decays in the early Universe in the presence of curvature perturbations. For sufficiently large perturbations associated with over-densities, we find that the bounce solution develops an oscillating middle stage near the bubble wall. For small perturbations, we analytically show within the thin-wall approximation that an over- (under-) density would enhance (suppress) the vacuum decay rate with a smaller (larger) initial bubble radius. By numerically solving for the bounce solutions and evaluating the corresponding Euclidean action, we further confirm this behaviour in thick-wall cases. Our results indicate that over-densities can generically trigger vacuum decay at an earlier moment.

### [59] [Phase-space integrals through Mellin-Barnes representation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01505)
*Taushif Ahmed,Syed Mehedi Hasan,Andreas Rapakoulias*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We analytically compute angular phase-space integrals with three and four denominators using the Mellin-Barnes representation within dimensional regularization, expressing results in terms of Goncharov polylogarithms (GPLs); results are provided up to finite or next-to-leading orders in $\varepsilon$, covering massless and single-massive cases, with extensions to multiple massive momenta via partial fractions and recursion relations for higher powers.

我们利用维数正则化下的Mellin-Barnes（MB）表示法，对含有三个和四个分母的角相空间积分进行了解析计算，将结果用Goncharov多对数（GPLs）表示；对于无质量和单质量情况，分别计算到$\mathcal{O}(\varepsilon^2)$和$\mathcal{O}(\varepsilon)$或$\mathcal{O}(\varepsilon^0)$；通过部分分式分解和递推关系，可推广至多质量动量和高次分母幂的情形。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Angular phase-space integrals with multiple denominators are essential components in higher-order perturbative calculations in quantum field theory, especially in processes involving loop corrections and real emissions. Their analytic evaluation is crucial for precision phenomenology, yet remains challenging due to the complexity of multi-denominator structures and the need for regularization. The goal is to provide compact, analytic results in a systematic framework—dimensional regularization via Mellin-Barnes representations—that facilitates integration into broader amplitude and cross-section computations.

在量子场论的高阶微扰计算中，含多个分母的角相空间积分是基本组成部分，尤其出现在圈图修正和实辐射过程中。由于多分母结构的复杂性和正则化的需要，其解析计算具有挑战性。本工作的目标是在一个系统框架——基于维数正则化和Mellin-Barnes表示——下提供紧凑且解析的结果，以方便其在散射振幅和截面计算中的应用。

Method: We employ the Mellin-Barnes (MB) representation to decompose multi-denominator phase-space integrals into multifold MB integrals. These are then transformed into real parametric integrals through contour deformation and residue analysis. The resulting integrals are evaluated systematically in $d = 4 - 2\varepsilon$ dimensions and expressed in terms of Goncharov polylogarithms (GPLs). Partial fractioning is used to reduce integrals with multiple massive momenta to the single-massive case. Recursion relations are derived to handle higher powers of denominators, reducing them to master integrals.

我们采用Mellin-Barnes（MB）表示法将多分母相空间积分分解为多重MB积分，再通过围道变形和留数分析将其转化为实参数积分。在$d = 4 - 2\varepsilon$维下系统地计算这些积分，并用Goncharov多对数（GPLs）表示结果。利用部分分式分解将含多个质量动量的积分约化为单质量情形，并推导递推关系以处理高次分母幂，约化为母积分。

Result: Analytic results for three- and four-denominator angular phase-space integrals are obtained: all-massless three-denominator integrals to $\mathcal{O}(\varepsilon^2)$, single-massive three-denominator integrals to $\mathcal{O}(\varepsilon)$, and both massless and single-massive four-denominator integrals to $\mathcal{O}(\varepsilon^0)$. All results are expressed in terms of Goncharov polylogarithms (GPLs). Integrals with multiple massive momenta are reduced via partial fractions. Recursion relations are derived that connect integrals with higher denominator powers to master integrals, enabling efficient computation in practical applications.

获得了三和四分母角相空间积分的解析结果：无质量三重分母积分至$\mathcal{O}(\varepsilon^2)$，单质量三重分母积分至$\mathcal{O}(\varepsilon)$，以及无质量和单质量四重分母积分至$\mathcal{O}(\varepsilon^0)$。所有结果均以Goncharov多对数（GPLs）表示。含多个质量动量的积分通过部分分式约化。推导出的递推关系将高次分母幂积分与母积分关联，便于实际应用中的高效计算。

Conclusion: The presented method provides a robust and systematic framework for evaluating multi-denominator angular phase-space integrals in dimensional regularization. By leveraging Mellin-Barnes representations and GPLs, compact analytic expressions are obtained up to required orders in $\varepsilon$. The derivation of recursion relations and reduction techniques extends the applicability to more complex configurations, making these results valuable for high-precision computations in perturbative QFT and collider physics.

本文提出的方法为在维数正则化下计算多分母角相空间积分提供了稳健且系统的框架。通过利用Mellin-Barnes表示和GPLs，获得了在$\varepsilon$展开中所需阶数的紧凑解析表达式。递推关系和约化技术的推导扩展了方法对更复杂构型的适用性，使这些结果在微扰QFT和对撞机物理的高精度计算中具有重要价值。

Abstract: We compute angular phase-space integrals with three and four denominators analytically, working within dimensional regularisation via the Mellin-Barnes (MB) representation. The approach converts multifold MB integrals into real parametric integrals and expresses all results in terms of Goncharov polylogarithms (GPLs). For three denominators, all-massless results are obtained to $\mathcal{O}(ε^2)$ and the single-massive case to $\mathcal{O}(ε)$; for four denominators, both the massless and single-massive cases are solved to $\mathcal{O}(ε^0)$. Integrals with multiple massive momenta follow from a partial fraction decomposition reducing them to the single-massive case. Recursion relations relating integrals with higher denominator powers to master integrals are derived. These are essential ingredients to solving full phase-space integrals.

</details>


### [60] [The Axion Helical Misalignment Mechanism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02012)
*Wei Chao,Chang-Jie Dai*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We propose the axion helical misalignment mechanism, in which primordial magnetic fields and chiral asymmetries modify the axion equation of motion via coupling to the hypercharge Chern-Simons term, effectively acting as a driven oscillator and shifting the onset of oscillations. This alters the relic abundance prediction and links axion dynamics to the chiral magnetic effect (CME), offering a new route to generate the baryon asymmetry.

我们提出了轴子螺旋失配机制，其中原初磁场和手征不对称性通过与超荷规范场的Chern-Simons项耦合改变轴子运动方程，等效为一个受驱振荡器并改变振荡起始时刻。这修正了轴子遗存丰度预测，并将轴子动力学与手征磁效应（CME）关联，为产生宇宙重子不对称性提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The standard misalignment mechanism assumes small initial field velocity and neglects cosmological interactions beyond gravity; however, if the axion has a large initial velocity or couples to gauge fields, its evolution can be dramatically altered. We aim to incorporate the effects of primordial magnetic fields and chiral asymmetries—common in early Universe scenarios—into axion cosmology to reassess the relic density and potential connections to baryogenesis.

标准失配机制假设轴子初始速度小且忽略除引力外的宇宙学相互作用；然而，若轴子具有大初速度或与规范场耦合，其演化可能显著改变。我们旨在将早期宇宙中常见的原初磁场和手征不对称性纳入轴子宇宙学，重新评估遗存密度及其与重子生成的联系。

Method: We derive the modified equation of motion for the axion field including its coupling to the hypercharge gauge field's Chern-Simons density $\partial_\mu J^{\text{CS}}_Y$, which introduces a source term proportional to the helicity of the gauge field. This transforms the axion dynamics into a damped, driven oscillator system. We solve this equation numerically and analytically in relevant cosmological epochs, incorporating the feedback from the chiral magnetic effect (CME) on the hypercharge field and vice versa. The resulting energy density is computed using phase-space distribution methods and continuity equations for chiral fermions.

我们推导了包含轴子与超荷规范场Chern-Simons密度$\partial_\mu J^{\text{CS}}_Y$耦合的运动方程，引入了正比于规范场螺旋度的源项，使轴子动力学变为阻尼受驱振荡系统。我们在相关宇宙学时期用数值和解析方法求解该方程，并纳入手征磁效应（CME）对超荷场及反向反馈的影响。通过手征费米子的相空间分布和连续性方程计算所得能量密度。

Result: The presence of primordial helical magnetic fields delays or advances the onset of axion oscillations depending on the relative sign of the coupling, modifying the relic abundance by orders of magnitude compared to the standard misalignment prediction. The axion helical misalignment mechanism allows for viable dark matter production at different axion masses and decay constants. Additionally, the backreaction between the axion and the CME sustains chiral asymmetry transfer, enabling successful baryogenesis via Standard Model sphaleron processes.

原初螺旋磁场的存在会根据耦合符号推迟或提前轴子振荡的起始，使遗存丰度相比标准失配机制改变多个数量级。轴子螺旋失配机制允许在不同轴子质量与衰变常数下实现可行的暗物质产生。此外，轴子与CME之间的反作用维持手征不对称性的传递，可通过标准模型sphaleron过程实现成功的重子生成。

Conclusion: Axion cosmology must account for nontrivial gauge field couplings and primordial helicity to accurately predict relic abundances. The axion helical misalignment mechanism represents a significant departure from conventional paradigms and establishes a deep connection between dark matter, primordial magnetogenesis, and baryogenesis through the interplay of axion dynamics and the chiral magnetic effect.

轴子宇宙学必须考虑非平庸的规范场耦合和原初螺旋度才能准确预测遗存丰度。轴子螺旋失配机制标志着对传统范式的重大偏离，并通过轴子动力学与手征磁效应（CME）的相互作用，在暗物质、原初磁场生成和重子生成之间建立了深刻联系。

Abstract: Understanding axion production in the early Universe remains a pivotal challenge, given the axion as a compelling cold dark matter candidate. Conventional misalignment scenarios often overlook the possibility that a large initial axion velocity can fundamentally reshape the subsequent evolution of the axion field. In this letter, we provide a comprehensive analysis of how primordial magnetic fields impact the axion relic abundance. By accounting for the axion coupling to the Chern-Simons term of the hypercharge gauge field, the equation of motion of the axion is recast as a driven oscillator equation. This modification effectively shifts the onset of axion oscillations, leading to a significant reevaluation of the final relic abundance, a novel effect we term the axion helical misalignment mechanism. Furthermore, in the presence of primordial chiral asymmetries, the chiral magnetic effect (CME) emerges as a critical driver of axion dynamics. The interplay between the axion field and the CME not only profoundly influences the evolution of Standard Model chiral fermions but also provides a viable pathway for generating the observed baryon asymmetry of the Universe.

</details>


### [61] [Higgs production in association with a Z boson at TeV-scale lepton colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01686)
*Hiroyuki Furusato,Satsuki Hosoya,Kentarou Mawatari,Shouta Suzuki*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper studies the $l^-l^+ \to \nu\bar{\nu}Zh$ process at multi-TeV lepton colliders, identifying enhanced cross sections compared to $l^-l^+ \to Zh$, classifying amplitudes by Feynman diagram topology, and analyzing interference patterns and gauge dependence, particularly highlighting the absence of high-energy gauge cancellations in the Feynman-diagram gauge.

本文研究了多 TeV 能区未来轻子对撞机上的 $l^-l^+ \to \nu\bar{\nu}Zh$ 过程，发现其截面大于 $l^-l^+ \to Zh$，根据费曼图拓扑结构将振幅分为三类，分析干涉模式和规范依赖性，特别指出在新提出的 Feynman-diagram 规范中高能区的规范抵消消失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand the behavior of the $l^-l^+ \to \nu\bar{\nu}Zh$ process at high energies (above a few TeV), where its cross section becomes significant, and to clarify the role of gauge invariance and amplitude interference in shaping physical observables, especially in light of new gauge choices like the Feynman-diagram gauge.

为了理解 $l^-l^+ \to \nu\bar{\nu}Zh$ 过程在高能区（数 TeV 以上）的行为，其中其截面变得显著，并阐明规范不变性和振幅干涉在塑造物理可观测量中的作用，特别是在新提出的 Feynman-diagram 规范等规范选择背景下。

Method: The authors classify the scattering amplitudes into three topological groups: vector boson scattering, $l^-W^+$ scattering, and $W^-l^+$ scattering. They compute the contributions in both the unitary gauge and the Feynman-diagram gauge, analyzing the high-energy behavior and interference patterns among subamplitudes. They also compare with the simpler $l^-l^+ \to \nu\bar{\nu}Z$ process to interpret Z-boson kinematics.

作者将散射振幅按拓扑结构分为三类：矢量玻色子散射、$l^-W^+$ 散射和 $W^-l^+$ 散射。他们在幺正规范和 Feynman-diagram 规范下计算各振幅贡献，分析高能行为及子振幅间的干涉模式，并与更简单的 $l^-l^+ \to \nu\bar{\nu}Z$ 过程比较以解释 Z 玻色子运动学分布。

Result: The cross section for $l^-l^+ \to \nu\bar{\nu}Zh$ exceeds that of $l^-l^+ \to Zh$ above a few TeV. Subtle gauge cancellations present in the unitary gauge at high energies are absent in the Feynman-diagram gauge, allowing clearer interpretation of physical distributions via individual amplitude subgroups. Interference patterns in Z-boson kinematics are shown to mirror those in $l^-l^+ \to \nu\bar{\nu}Z$.

在数 TeV 以上，$l^-l^+ \to \nu\bar{\nu}Zh$ 的截面超过 $l^-l^+ \to Zh$。高能下的微妙规范抵消在幺正规范中存在但在 Feynman-diagram 规范中消失，使得通过各振幅子群更清晰地解释物理分布成为可能。Z 玻色子运动学中的干涉模式被证明与 $l^-l^+ \to \nu\bar{\nu}Z$ 中的一致。

Conclusion: The $l^-l^+ \to \nu\bar{\nu}Zh$ process is phenomenologically important at multi-TeV lepton colliders. The Feynman-diagram gauge provides a useful framework for interpreting physical distributions due to the lack of premature gauge cancellations, revealing the distinct roles of amplitude subgroups. Insights from the $l^-l^+ \to \nu\bar{\nu}Z$ process help explain Z-boson kinematics in the extended process.

在多 TeV 轻子对撞机上，$l^-l^+ \to \nu\bar{\nu}Zh$ 过程具有重要现象学意义。由于缺乏过早的规范抵消，Feynman-diagram 规范为解释物理分布提供了有用框架，揭示了各振幅子群的不同作用。来自 $l^-l^+ \to \nu\bar{\nu}Z$ 过程的认识有助于解释扩展过程中的 Z 玻色子运动学。

Abstract: We study the $l^-l^+\to ν\barνZh$ process for future lepton colliders, whose cross section becomes larger than that for $l^-l^+\to Zh$ in the energy region above a few TeV. %
We classify the amplitudes into three main groups based on the topology of each Feynman diagram; vector boson scattering, $l^-W^+$ scattering, and $W^-l^+$ scattering, and study the interference patterns among the amplitudes. %
We show that subtle gauge cancellation among the amplitudes at high energies in the unitary gauge is absent in the recently proposed Feynman-diagram gauge, and the physical distributions can be interpreted by the contributions from each subgroup. %
We also find that the interference patterns in kinematical distributions of the Z boson can be understood by those in the $l^-l^+\to ν\barνZ$ process.
