### [62] [Localized Steps toward ACT-Favored Inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02148)
*Kai-Ge Zhang,Chengjie Fu,Jian-Feng He,Zong-Kuan Guo*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: A smooth step in the inflaton potential can shift the predicted scalar spectral index $n_s$ and tensor-to-scalar ratio $r$ by altering the field value at horizon exit of the CMB pivot scale, helping reconcile plateau-like inflation models with recent ACT measurements.

在原初暴胀势能中引入一个平滑的局部台阶，可通过改变CMB pivot尺度穿越视界的场值，调节预测的标量谱指数$n_s$和张量标量比$r$，从而帮助使平台型暴胀模型与最新的ACT观测结果一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Recent measurements from the Atacama Cosmology Telescope (ACT) suggest a higher scalar spectral index $n_s$ than the Planck satellite's determination, creating tension with many canonical single-field slow-roll inflation models, especially plateau-type attractors like Starobinsky or Higgs inflation. This motivates exploring modifications to the inflaton potential that can increase $n_s$ without violating other observational constraints.

阿塔卡马宇宙学望远镜（ACT）的最新测量显示标量谱指数$n_s$高于普朗克卫星的结果，这对许多标准的单场慢滚暴胀模型（尤其是Starobinsky或希格斯暴胀等平台型模型）构成挑战。因此，有必要探索能在不违反其他观测限制的前提下提升$n_s$的原初暴胀势能修正机制。

Method: We consider a smooth, localized step in the inflaton potential of the form $\Delta V(\phi) \propto \tanh\left[(\phi - \phi_0)/\delta\right]$, which introduces a transient feature during inflation. Using linear perturbation theory and slow-roll approximations, we compute corrections to the slow-roll parameters $\epsilon$, $\eta$, and their runnings, which modify the predictions for $n_s$ and $r$. The shift in the field value $\phi_*$ at which the CMB pivot scale $k_* = 0.05~\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1}$ exits the horizon is calculated numerically and analytically, showing how the step displaces the effective initial condition for observable modes.

我们考虑一种形式为$\Delta V(\phi) \propto \tanh\left[(\phi - \phi_0)/\delta\right]$的平滑局部台阶势。利用线性微扰理论和慢滚近似，计算该结构对慢滚参数$\epsilon$、$\eta$及其跑动的修正，进而改变$n_s$和$r$的预测值。通过数值和解析方法计算CMB pivot尺度$k_* = 0.05~\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1}$穿越视界时的场值$\phi_*$的偏移，揭示台阶如何改变可观测模式的有效初始条件。

Result: The step feature induces a positive shift in the scalar spectral index $\Delta n_s \sim 0.01$, bringing plateau-like models (e.g., T-models in EFTofLSS or $\alpha$-attractors) into better agreement with ACT data. The tensor-to-scalar ratio $r$ is mildly suppressed due to reduced inflationary energy scale near the step. Monomial potentials (e.g., $V \propto \phi^2$) also show improvement but remain marginally consistent. In contrast, natural inflation models exhibit insufficient shifts in $n_s$, failing to resolve the tension with ACT.

该台阶特征可引起标量谱指数正向偏移$\Delta n_s \sim 0.01$，使平台型模型（如EFTofLSS中的T模型或$\alpha$-attractor）更符合ACT数据。由于台阶附近暴胀能标降低，张量标量比$r$略有抑制。单项式势（如$V \propto \phi^2$）也有改善但仍仅勉强符合；而自然暴胀模型中$n_s$的偏移不足，无法缓解与ACT的张力。

Conclusion: A smooth step in the inflaton potential provides a viable mechanism to reconcile single-field plateau inflation models with the higher $n_s$ values reported by ACT. The effect arises from a shift in the horizon-crossing field value $\phi_*$, modifying the effective initial conditions for observable perturbations. This highlights the importance of sub-Planckian features in the potential for precision inflationary model building.

原初暴胀势中的平滑台阶为调和单场平台型暴胀模型与ACT观测到的较高$n_s$值提供了可行机制。该效应源于视界穿越场值$\phi_*$的偏移，改变了可观测扰动的有效初始条件。这凸显了势能中亚普朗克尺度特征在精确暴胀模型构建中的重要性。

Abstract: Recent ACT measurements favor a scalar spectral index n_s larger than the Planck value, posing a challenge to many single-field slow-roll inflation models. We show that a smooth, localized step in the inflaton potential can shift the predicted values of n_s and r by displacing the field value at which the CMB pivot scale exits the horizon. This mechanism can move monomial and, in particular, plateau-like attractor models toward the ACT-favored region, whereas the induced shift remains insufficient in natural inflation.

### [63] [Exclusive semileptonic and nonleptonic $J/ψ$ decays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01782)
*V. O. Galkin,I. S. Sukhanov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: The paper studies exclusive semileptonic and nonleptonic $J/\psi$ decays using a relativistic quark model based on the quasipotential approach and QCD. Form factors are computed with full relativistic corrections as overlap integrals of meson wave functions, enabling predictions of decay branching fractions in the full kinematic range. Semileptonic decays to electrons and muons are evaluated, while nonleptonic decays are analyzed under the factorization approximation in the $N_c \to \infty$ limit. Predicted branching ratios lie in the range $10^{-9} \sim 10^{-12}$, consistent with prior theory and experiment.

本文在基于准势方法和量子色动力学的相对论夸克模型框架下，研究了$J/\psi$介子的道独家轻子衰变和非轻子衰变。计算中完整包含了相对论效应，将描述弱流强子矩阵元的形状因子表示为介子波函数的重叠积分，并在全部运动学区域内确定。在此基础上，计算了包含电子和缪子的半轻子衰变分支比；非轻子衰变则在颜色数$N_c\to\infty$极限下的因子化近似中处理。所得分支比约为$10^{-9}\sim10^{-12}$，并与以往理论预测及现有实验上限进行了比较。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To accurately predict the branching fractions of exclusive semileptonic and nonleptonic $J/\psi$ decays by incorporating relativistic effects within a consistent theoretical framework rooted in quantum chromodynamics (QCD), and to compare these predictions with experimental limits and prior theoretical models.

准确预测道独家轻子和非轻子$J/\psi$衰变的分支比，通过在基于量子色动力学（QCD）的自洽理论框架内纳入相对论效应，并将这些预测与实验限制和先前的理论模型进行比较。

Method: The relativistic quark model based on the quasipotential approach is employed to compute the form factors for $J/\psi$ decays. These form factors are derived as overlap integrals of the initial and final meson wave functions, with complete relativistic corrections included. The semileptonic decay rates are calculated directly from these form factors, while nonleptonic decays are treated in the factorization approximation in the large-$N_c$ limit ($N_c \to \infty$).

采用基于准势方法的相对论夸克模型来计算$J/\psi$衰变的形状因子。这些形状因子被表示为初态和末态介子波函数之间的重叠积分，并完整包含相对论修正。半轻子衰变速率由这些形状因子直接计算，而非轻子衰变则在大$N_c$极限（$N_c \to \infty$）的因子化近似下处理。

Result: Form factors for $J/\psi$ decays are obtained across the entire kinematically allowed range. Branching fractions for semileptonic decays involving electrons and muons are predicted, and nonleptonic decay rates are estimated under factorization. The resulting branching ratios are in the range $10^{-9} \sim 10^{-12}$, consistent with previous theoretical estimates and within current experimental upper bounds.

在全运动学范围内获得了$J/\psi$衰变的形状因子。预测了涉及电子和缪子的半轻子衰变分支比，并在因子化假设下估算了非轻子衰变速率。所得分支比在$10^{-9}\sim10^{-12}$量级，与以往理论预测一致，且处于当前实验上限范围内。

Conclusion: The relativistic quark model with full relativistic treatment provides reliable predictions for rare $J/\psi$ decays. The inclusion of relativistic effects via the quasipotential approach significantly improves accuracy. The predicted branching fractions, though extremely small, are potentially testable in high-luminosity experiments such as those at BESIII or future charm factories.

采用完整相对论处理的相对论夸克模型为稀有$J/\psi$衰变提供了可靠的预测。通过准势方法引入相对论效应显著提高了计算精度。尽管预测的分支比极小，但在BESIII或未来的粲物理工厂等高亮度实验中仍具有可检验性。

Abstract: Exclusive semileptonic and nonleptonic $J/ψ$ decays are investigated in the framework of the relativistic quark model based on the quasipotential approach and quantum chromodynamics. The form factors parameterizing the hadronic matrix element of the weak current are calculated with the complete account of the relativistic effects. These form factors are expressed as the overlap integrals of the meson wave functions and are determined in the whole accessible kinematic range. On this basis the semileptonic decay branching fractions are evaluated for decays involving both electrons and muons. The nonleptonic decays are considered in the factorization approximation in the limit for the number of colors $N_c\to \infty$. The obtain branching fractions are found to be of the order $10^{-9}\sim 10^{-12}$. They are compared with the previous theoretical predictions and available experimental upper bounds.

### [64] [The scaling Pomeron](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01822)
*R. Peschanski,B. G. Giraud*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: A Regge-theoretical analysis of pp elastic scattering at LHC energies reveals a positive-signature Pomeron amplitude with scaling behavior, successfully describing the dip-bump structure in the differential cross-section; an analytic continuation of t-channel partial waves reveals pole singularities at fractional values on the real $l_t$ axis.

LHC能量下质子-质子弹性散射的Regge理论分析揭示了一种具有标度行为的正宇称Pomeron振幅，成功描述了微分截面中的dip-bump结构；对t道部分波进行解析延拓后，在实$ l_t $轴的分数值处发现了一系列极点奇点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: To understand the scaling behavior in the differential cross-sections of pp elastic scattering at high energies (LHC) within the framework of Regge theory, particularly focusing on the role of the Pomeron and the structure of the dip-bump region.

旨在利用Regge理论框架解释高能（LHC）质子-质子弹性散射微分截面中的标度行为，特别是Pomeron的作用以及dip-bump区域的结构。

Method: Application of Regge theory to derive a positive-signature (Pomeron) amplitude exhibiting scaling; analytic continuation of t-channel partial waves with angular momentum index $l_t$ is performed to explore the complex plane structure, identifying singularities and scaling properties.

应用Regge理论推导出具有标度特性的正宇称（Pomeron）振幅；通过对角动量指数为$ l_t $的t道部分波进行解析延拓，研究其在复平面上的结构，识别奇点和标度特性。

Result: A scaling Pomeron amplitude is derived that describes the dip-bump region in $d\sigma/dt$ at LHC energies consistent with experimental data; the analytic continuation reveals a singularity structure consisting of a series of poles located at fractional values along the real $l_t$ axis, with no other singularities present.

推导出的标度Pomeron振幅能够描述LHC能量下$d\sigma/dt$中的dip-bump区域，并与实验数据一致；解析延拓结果显示奇点结构由位于实$ l_t $轴上分数值处的一系列极点组成，无其他奇点存在。

Conclusion: The observed scaling in pp elastic scattering at high energies can be explained within Regge theory via a special class of Pomeron amplitude with analytic properties characterized by fractional poles in the $l_t$ plane, offering new insight into the non-perturbative dynamics of QCD.

高能质子-质子弹性散射中观测到的标度行为可通过Regge理论中一类具有$ l_t $平面分数极点解析特性的Pomeron振幅来解释，为QCD非微扰动力学提供了新的见解。

Abstract: We examine the Regge theoretical properties for the scaling observed in pp elastic scattering differential cross-sections at the LHC. A positive signature amplitude (i.e. the Pomeron) with scaling properties has been derived. It is found to describe the dip-bump region of momentum transfer at LHC energies in agreement with data. We derive the analytic continuation in the whole plane of the t-channel partial waves of index $l_t$ specific to the Regge formalism. The analytic form of the amplitude exhibits a specific scaling property without singularities, except for a series of poles in the $l_t$ real axis at fractional values.

</details>


### [65] [Tetraquark-Jet Systems at the High-Luminosity LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01865)
*Francesco Giovanni Celiberto*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This review explores the high-energy production of fully heavy tetraquark-jet systems at the LHC using fragmentation functions within a nonrelativistic QCD framework, providing NLL/NLO$^+$ predictions via the (sym)Jethad framework to probe multiquark dynamics in QCD.

本文综述了在LHC上利用非相对论性QCD框架中的碎裂函数研究全重四夸克-喷注系统的高能产生，通过(sym)Jethad框架提供NLL/NLO$^+$精度的预测，以探究QCD中的多夸克动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Fully heavy tetraquarks ($T_{4Q}$) serve as unique probes of exotic hadronic structure and nonperturbative QCD dynamics; understanding their production in high-energy collisions allows access to multiquark correlations beyond conventional quark models.

全重四夸克($T_{4Q}$)是奇特强子结构和非微扰QCD动力学的独特探针；理解其在高能碰撞中的产生有助于探索超越传统夸克模型的多夸克关联。

Method: The study employs the TQ4Q1.1 fragmentation functions based on nonrelativistic QCD (NRQCD), including both gluon- and heavy-quark-initiated channels, with threshold-consistent DGLAP evolution via the HF-NRevo scheme; uncertainties are analyzed through color-composite long-distance matrix elements (LDMEs) and perturbative scale variations (H-/F-MHOUs); predictions are computed within the (sym)Jethad framework at NLL/NLO$^+$ accuracy.

本研究采用基于非相对论性QCD(NRQCD)的TQ4Q1.1碎裂函数，包含胶子和重夸克引发的通道，并通过HF-NRevo方案实现阈值一致的DGLAP演化；通过颜色复合的长距离矩阵元(LDMEs)和微扰尺度变化(H-/F-MHOUs)分析不确定性；在(sym)Jethad框架下以NLL/NLO$^+$精度进行预测计算。

Result: Phenomenological predictions for semi-inclusive $T_{4Q}$-jet production are provided at LHC energies, with consistent treatment of mass thresholds and scale dependence, enabling discrimination between different LDME scenarios and offering sensitivity to gluon vs. heavy-quark fragmentation contributions.

提供了LHC能量下半单举$T_{4Q}$-喷注产生的现象学预测，一致处理了质量阈值和尺度依赖性，能够区分不同LDME情景并对胶子与重夸克碎裂贡献具有敏感性。

Conclusion: The fragmentation-based approach combined with modern QCD tools establishes fully heavy tetraquarks as viable probes of exotic hadron structure and high-energy QCD dynamics, particularly in the context of future high-luminosity collider experiments.

基于碎裂的方法结合现代QCD工具，确立了全重四夸克作为奇特强子结构和高能QCD动力学的有效探针，特别是在未来高亮度对撞机实验中的应用前景。

Abstract: We investigate the high-energy production of tetraquark-jet systems at the LHC and its forthcoming High-Luminosity upgrade. In this review, we examine the leading-power fragmentation of fully heavy tetraquarks ($T_{4Q}$) in hadronic collisions, highlighting their relevance as novel probes of multiquark dynamics in QCD. Our analysis relies on the hadron-structure-oriented TQ4Q1.1 fragmentation functions, built within a nonrelativistic QCD framework that incorporates both gluon- and heavy-quark-initiated channels. Threshold-consistent DGLAP evolution is performed through the HF-NRevo scheme, enabling a unified treatment of mass thresholds and scale variations. We also provide a systematic discussion of uncertainties arising from color-composite long-distance matrix elements (LDMEs) and from perturbative hard- and fragmentation-scale inputs (H- and F-MHOUs). Phenomenological predictions are obtained using the (sym)Jethad framework at NLL/NLO$^+$ accuracy for semi-inclusive tetraquark-jet production at the LHC and beyond. This review connects the emerging spectroscopy of fully heavy exotics with modern fragmentation-based approaches to hadron structure and high-energy QCD.

### [66] [Heavy-Flavor Fragmentation: The QCD Portal to Exotic Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.01867)
*Francesco Giovanni Celiberto*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We study the production mechanism of fully heavy tetraquarks (QQ\bar{Q}\bar{Q}) via collinear fragmentation functions in a nonrelativistic QCD framework, considering scalar ($0^{++}$), axial vector ($1^{+-}$), and tensor ($2^{++}$) states. Using leading-power single-parton fragmentation and DGLAP evolution with threshold resummation (HF-NRevo), we provide the first uncertainty quantification from long-distance matrix elements, strengthening links between exotic hadron structure and precision QCD.

我们通过非相对论QCD框架下的共线碎裂函数研究全重四夸克（QQ\bar{Q}\bar{Q}）的产生机制，考虑标量（$0^{++}$）、轴矢量（$1^{+-}$）和张量（$2^{++}$）态。采用单部分子碎裂主导项及带有阈值重求和的DGLAP演化（HF-NRevo），我们首次量化了来自长程矩阵元的不确定性，加强了奇特强子结构与精确QCD之间的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Exotic hadrons such as fully heavy tetraquarks challenge conventional quark model paradigms and offer probes of nonperturbative QCD dynamics. A rigorous QCD-based description of their production is essential to interpret current and future LHC data, particularly for distinguishing compact tetraquark states from molecular or kinematic effects. The lack of precise theoretical predictions including uncertainty estimates has hindered definitive identification.

全重四夸克等奇特强子挑战了传统夸克模型范式，提供了探测量子色动力学（QCD）非微扰效应的途径。对其产生过程进行严格的QCD理论描述对于解释当前和未来的LHC数据至关重要，特别是用于区分紧致四夸k夸克态与分子态或运动学效应。缺乏包含不确定性估计的精确理论预测阻碍了明确识别。

Method: We employ leading-power single-parton fragmentation functions within a nonrelativistic QCD (NRQCD) framework, specialized for tetraquark Fock state configurations. The initial-scale fragmentation probabilities are derived from updated gluon- and heavy-quark ($Q = c, b$) channels, incorporating color-composite long-distance matrix elements (LDMEs). These inputs are evolved using threshold-resummed DGLAP equations implemented in the HF-NRevo code, ensuring consistency across kinematic thresholds. Uncertainties in LDMEs are systematically propagated through the evolution and fragmentation process.

我们在非相对论QCD（NRQCD）框架内采用主导幂次的单部分子碎裂函数，并针对四夸克Fock态构型进行了专门化处理。初始尺度的碎裂概率源自更新后的胶子和重夸克（$Q = c, b$）通道，并包含颜色复合的长程矩阵元（LDMEs）。这些输入通过HF-NRevo代码中实现的阈值重求和DGLAP方程进行演化，确保跨运动学阈值的一致性。LDME中的不确定性在演化和碎裂过程中被系统传播。

Result: We obtain the first complete set of TQ4Q1.1 collinear fragmentation functions for scalar ($0^{++}$), axial vector ($1^{+-}$), and tensor ($2^{++}$) fully heavy tetraquarks, with full uncertainty bands derived from LDME variations. The evolution exhibits strong scale dependence near thresholds, with distinct patterns across quantum numbers. Gluon-initiated channels dominate at low scales, while heavy-quark channels become relevant at higher energies. The predicted fragmentation probabilities span several orders of magnitude depending on flavor and spin configuration.

我们获得了首套完整的TQ4Q1.1共线碎裂函数，适用于标量（$0^{++}$）、轴矢量（$1^{+-}$）和张量（$2^{++}$）全重四夸克，并基于LDME变化得出了完整的不确定带。演化在阈值附近表现出强烈的能标依赖性，且不同量子数间呈现明显差异。胶子主导的通道在低能标占优，而重夸克通道在高能区变得重要。预测的碎裂概率根据味和自旋构型跨越多个数量级。

Conclusion: This work establishes a robust QCD foundation for the production of fully heavy tetraquarks via fragmentation, enabling precision tests of exotic hadron formation. The systematic inclusion of LDME uncertainties allows for meaningful comparisons with experimental data and distinguishes compact tetraquark interpretations from alternative models. The framework bridges nonperturbative hadronic structure with high-precision perturbative evolution, advancing the field of exotic matter in the QCD regime.

本工作为通过碎裂机制产生全重四夸克建立了坚实的QCD基础，使对奇特强子形成的精确检验成为可能。系统地包含LDME不确定性使得与实验数据进行有意义的比较成为可能，并有助于区分紧致四夸克解释与其他替代模型。该框架连接了非微扰强子结构与高精度微扰演化，推动了QCD区域内奇特物质领域的进展。

Abstract: We investigate the core dynamics behind exotic matter formation via the TQ4Q1.1 set of collinear fragmentation functions for fully charmed or bottomed tetraquarks in three quantum configurations: scalar ($0^{++}$), axial vector ($1^{+-}$), and tensor ($2^{++}$). We adopt leading-power single-parton fragmentation within a nonrelativistic QCD framework tailored to tetraquark Fock states. Initial-scale inputs are constructed from updated gluon- and heavy-quark channels, and evolved through threshold-consistent DGLAP within HF-NRevo. We present the first systematic propagation of uncertainties from color-composite long-distance matrix elements governing tetraquark hadronization. This study advances the connection between hadronic structure, precision QCD, and exotic matter.

TL;DR: We present the full OMG3Q1.0 family of collinear fragmentation functions for triply heavy $\Omega_{3Q}$ baryons, extending to both charm ($\Omega_{3c}$) and bottom ($\Omega_{3b}$) sectors, based on improved proxy-model calculations matched to flavor-aware DGLAP evolution (HF-NRevo), enabling NLL/NLO$^+$ predictions for semi-inclusive $\Omega_{3Q}$ + jet production at future colliders via the (sym)JETHAD framework.

我们使用改进的代理模型计算重夸克和胶子向$\Omega_{3Q}$碎裂的过程，构建面向强子结构的碎裂函数，并将其匹配到味觉感知的DGLAP演化框架(HF-NRevo)中。生成的OMG3Q1.0函数被实现在(sym)JETHAD多模块接口中，用于计算半单举$\Omega_{3Q}$加喷注产生的NLL重求和和NLO$^+$截面。

Result: We deliver the complete OMG3Q1.0 set of collinear fragmentation functions for both $\Omega_{3c}$ and $\Omega_{3b}$ baryons. 我们提供了完整的OMG3Q1.0共线碎裂函数集，适用于$\Omega_{3c}$和$\Omega_{3b}$重子。给出了在HL-LHC和FCC能量下$\Omega_{3Q}$+喷注产生的NLL/NLO$^+$精度预测，揭示了对初态胶子碎裂和重夸克质量效应的增强敏感性。该框架能够在多重重夸克区域定量检验强子化模型。

Abstract: We investigate the leading-power fragmentation of triply heavy $Ω$ baryons in high-energy hadronic collisions. ### [68] [Many Wrongs Make a Right: Leveraging Biased Simulations Towards Unbiased Parameter Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02219)
*Ezequiel Alvarez,Sean Benevedes,Manuel Szewc,Jesse Thaler*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: We propose a Template-Adapted Mixture Model (TAMM) for signal fraction estimation in mixed signal-background samples, using multiple biased simulations to enable data-driven distribution estimation and reduce domain shift effects. The method yields well-calibrated uncertainties in both toy Gaussian and semi-realistic di-Higgs examples.

我们提出了一种模板适配混合模型（TAMM），用于在信号与背景混合样本中估计信号比例，利用多个有偏模拟实现数据驱动的分布估计，减少模拟与真实之间的域偏移效应。该方法在高斯玩具模型和半真实的双希格斯测量示例中均给出良好校准的不确定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: In particle physics, simulation-based inference is crucial, but standard methods suffer from simulation-data mismodeling biases, especially due to domain shifts between simulated and real data. These biases can severely impact parameter estimation, particularly in signal fraction inference where signal and background distributions are complex and poorly modeled. Controlling such biases within traditional pipelines remains challenging.

在粒子物理中，基于模拟的推断至关重要，但标准方法常受模拟与数据之间建模偏差的影响，尤其是模拟与真实数据间的域偏移问题。这些偏差会严重影响参数估计，特别是在信号比例推断中，当信号与背景分布复杂且建模不当时尤为突出。在传统流程中控制此类偏差仍具挑战性。

Method: We introduce the Template-Adapted Mixture Model (TAMM), which uses multiple biased simulations from different domains (e.g., simulation configurations) to construct flexible, data-driven estimates of signal and background distributions in the target (data) domain. By modeling the mixture components via weighted combinations of simulation templates—optimized using statistical methods such as maximum likelihood—we correct for domain shift. We explore various feature representations, model selection strategies (e.g., cross-validation), and regularization techniques to ensure robustness. The framework operates without requiring perfectly accurate simulations, only that they span diverse plausible variations.

我们提出了模板适配混合模型（TAMM），利用来自不同域（如不同模拟配置）的多个有偏模拟，构建目标域（真实数据）中信号与背景分布的灵活、数据驱动估计。通过使用统计方法（如最大似然）优化模拟模板的加权组合来建模混合分量，从而校正域偏移。我们探索了多种特征表示、模型选择策略（如交叉验证）和正则化技术以确保鲁棒性。该框架无需完全精确的模拟，只需模拟能覆盖多样化的合理变化即可。

Result: Applied to a Gaussian toy model and a semi-realistic di-Higgs ($hh \rightarrow bb\gamma\gamma$) analysis, TAMM successfully reduces bias in signal fraction estimation compared to conventional methods. The resulting uncertainties are well-calibrated, with coverage properties close to nominal levels (e.g., 95% confidence intervals contain the true value ~95% of the time). Different feature representations (e.g., high-level vs. low-level features) and model selections affect performance, but proper validation ensures optimal choices. The method demonstrates robustness even when individual simulations are highly biased.

在高斯玩具模型和半真实的双希格斯（$hh \rightarrow bb\gamma\gamma$）分析中的应用表明，与传统方法相比，TAMM显著降低了信号比例估计的偏差。所得不确定性具有良好校准性，覆盖概率接近标称水平（例如95%置信区间约95%时间包含真值）。不同的特征表示（如高层与低层特征）和模型选择会影响性能，但适当的验证可确保最优选择。即使单个模拟存在严重偏差，该方法仍表现出鲁棒性。

Conclusion: The Template-Adapted Mixture Model provides a robust, data-driven approach to signal fraction estimation under simulation-data mismodeling. By leveraging multiple biased simulations, it mitigates domain shift without relying on perfect simulation accuracy, enabling more reliable inference in particle physics and other data-rich sciences.

模板适配混合模型为在模拟-数据建模偏差条件下进行信号比例估计提供了一种稳健且数据驱动的方法。通过利用多个有偏模拟，它在不依赖完美模拟精度的情况下缓解了域偏移问题，可在粒子物理及其他数据密集型科学中实现更可靠的推断。

Abstract: In particle physics, as in many areas of science, parameter inference relies on simulations to bridge the gap between theory and experiment. Recent developments in simulation-based inference have boosted the sensitivity of analyses; however, biases induced by simulation-data mismodeling can be difficult to control within standard inference pipelines. In this work, we propose a Template-Adapted Mixture Model to confront this problem in the context of signal fraction estimation: inferring the population proportion of signal in a mixed sample of signal and background, both of which follow arbitrarily complex distributions. We harness many biased simulations to perform data-driven estimates of each process distribution in the signal region, substantially reducing the bias on the signal fraction due to the domain shift between simulation and reality. We explore different methodological choices, including model selection, feature representation, and statistical method, and apply them to a Gaussian toy example and to a semi-realistic di-Higgs measurement. We find that the presented methods successfully leverage the biased simulations to provide estimates with well-calibrated uncertainties.

</details>


### [69] [Search for dark photons at future e$^+$e$^-$ colliders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.02245)
*Mikael Berggren*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: This paper studies the sensitivity of future $e^+e^-$ colliders, particularly the ILC Higgs factory with the ILD detector, to dark photons ($A_D$) in the mass range beyond Belle II's reach, using the $A_D \rightarrow \mu^+\mu^-$ decay channel. By fully simulating signal and background events, it derives exclusion limits on the kinetic mixing parameter $\epsilon$ as a function of $A_D$ mass, taking into account detector resolution and efficiency. The analysis highlights the advantages of $e^+e^-$ machines for narrow resonance searches due to low backgrounds and excellent momentum resolution.

本文研究了未来正负电子对撞机（特别是ILC Higgs工厂配备ILD探测器）在Belle II不可及的质量范围内，利用暗光子（$A_D$）衰变到缪子对（$A_D \rightarrow \mu^+\mu^-$）的通道对其探测灵敏度。通过对信号和标准模型背景事件进行完整模拟，推导出动能混合参数$\epsilon$作为$A_D$质量函数的排除极限，并考虑了探测器分辨率和效率的影响。分析强调了由于本底低且动量分辨率优异，正负电子对撞机在窄共振态搜索中的优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Dark matter may reside in a hidden 'dark sector' with its own forces, such as a U(1) gauge symmetry giving rise to a dark photon ($A_D$). Kinetic mixing between the dark photon and the ordinary photon provides a renormalizable portal connecting the dark sector to the Standard Model (SM), parameterized by $\epsilon$. This mixing allows $A_D$ production and decay into SM particles. For $\epsilon$ values not yet excluded, $A_D$ would appear as a narrow, prompt resonance—undetectable by current experiments like Belle II at higher masses. Thus, future high-energy $e^+e^-$ colliders offer an ideal environment to probe this unexplored parameter space due to their clean environments, precise detectors, and well-understood backgrounds.

暗物质可能存在于一个隐藏的“暗区”中，该区域拥有自身的相互作用，例如由U(1)规范对称性产生的暗光子（$A_D$）。暗光子与普通光子之间的动能混合提供了一个可重正化的通往标准模型（SM）的门户，其强度由参数$\epsilon$描述。这种混合使得$A_D$能够被产生并衰变为SM粒子。对于尚未被排除的$\epsilon$值，$A_D$将表现为一个窄而即时的共振态——当前实验如Belle II在较高质量区域无法探测到。因此，未来的高能正负电子对撞机因其干净的环境、高精度探测器和已知背景，成为探索这一未开发参数空间的理想场所。

Method: The study uses full GEANT-based simulation of the ILD detector at the ILC Higgs factory operating at $\sqrt{s} = 250$ GeV. Signal events for $e^+e^- \rightarrow \gamma A_D$, followed by $A_D \rightarrow \mu^+\mu^-$, are generated across a range of $A_D$ masses and $\epsilon$ values. Backgrounds from SM processes, especially $e^+e^- \rightarrow \mu^+\mu^-(\gamma)$, are fully simulated. Event selection criteria are optimized to isolate narrow dimuon resonances. Limits on $\epsilon$ are derived using a profile likelihood ratio method under the asymptotic approximation, incorporating systematic uncertainties. Extrapolations to other $e^+e^-$ collider energies and generic detector performances are discussed based on scaling laws for cross sections, branching ratios, and detector capabilities.

该研究使用基于GEANT的完整模拟，针对运行在$\sqrt{s} = 250$ GeV的ILC Higgs工厂上的ILD探测器开展。生成了从$e^+e^- \rightarrow \gamma A_D$随后$A_D \rightarrow \mu^+\mu^-$的信号事件，覆盖一系列$A_D$质量和$\epsilon$值。对来自标准模型过程（尤其是$e^+e^- \rightarrow \mu^+\mu^-(\gamma)$）的背景进行了完全模拟。通过优化事例选择标准以分离窄的双缪子共振态。采用轮廓似然比方法（在渐近近似下），结合系统误差，推导出对$\epsilon$的限制。基于截面、分支比和探测器性能的标度律，讨论了向其他$e^+e^-$对撞机能量和通用探测器性能的外推。


Result: Projected exclusion limits on the kinetic mixing parameter $\epsilon$ are presented as a function of the dark photon mass $m_{A_D}$ in the range $\mathcal{O}(10)$ MeV to $\sim 100$ GeV, significantly extending beyond current Belle II constraints. For example, at $m_{A_D} \sim 10$ GeV, sensitivities down to $\epsilon \sim 3 \times 10^{-4}$ are projected with 2 ab$^{-1}$ of data. The analysis demonstrates that the excellent momentum resolution ($\Delta p/p \sim 10^{-4}$) and high track-finding efficiency of ILD enable detection of very narrow resonances unresolved by the detector. Systematic uncertainties, particularly from luminosity and background modeling, are shown to be subdominant to statistical errors in most of the parameter space.

作为暗光子质量$m_{A_D}$的函数，给出了动能混合参数$\epsilon$的预期排除极限，范围从$\mathcal{O}(10)$ MeV到约100 GeV，显著超越当前Belle II的限制。例如，在$m_{A_D} \sim 10$ GeV时，利用2 ab$^{-1}$的数据可达到$\epsilon \sim 3 \times 10^{-4}$的灵敏度。分析表明，ILD探测器优异的动量分辨率（$\Delta p/p \sim 10^{-4}$）和高跟踪效率使其能够探测到探测器无法分辨的极窄共振态。系统误差（特别是来自亮度和背景建模的误差）在大部分参数空间中低于统计误差。


Conclusion: Future $e^+e^-$ colliders, such as the ILC operating at the Higgs factory stage, offer unparalleled sensitivity to dark photons in the MeV–GeV mass range via the $A_D \rightarrow \mu^+\mu^-$ channel. The combination of low backgrounds, high luminosity, and precision tracking enables discovery or exclusion of dark photons with kinetic mixing parameters several orders of magnitude below current bounds. This makes such facilities powerful tools for exploring weakly coupled dark sectors. The methodology and scaling arguments presented can guide projections for other $e^+e^-$ machines, including FCC-ee and CEPC.

未来的正负电子对撞机（如处于Higgs工厂阶段的ILC）通过$A_D \rightarrow \mu^+\mu^-$通道，在MeV至GeV质量范围内的暗光子探测方面具有无与伦比的灵敏度。低本底、高亮度和精密追踪能力的结合，使得发现或排除动能混合参数比当前界限低数个数量级的暗光子成为可能。这使此类设施成为探索弱耦合暗区的强大工具。本文提出的方法和标度论证可用于指导其他正负电子对撞机（包括FCC-ee和CEPC）的预期性能评估。

Abstract: In a class of theories, dark matter is explained by postulating the existence of a `dark sector', which interacts gravitationally with ordinary matter. If this dark sector contains a U(1) symmetry, and a corresponding `dark' photon ($A_{D}$) , it is natural to expect that this particle kineticly mix with the ordinary photon, and hence become a `portal' through which the dark sector can be studied. The strength of the mixing is given by a mixing parameter $(ε)$. This same parameter governs both the production and the decay of the $A_{D}$ back to SM particles, and for values of $ε$ not already excluded, the signal would be a quite small, and quite narrow resonance: If $ε$ is large enough to yield a detectable signal, its decay width will be smaller than the detector resolution, but so large that the decay back to SM particles is prompt. For masses of the dark photon above the reach of Belle II, future high energy e$^+$e$^-$ colliders are ideal for searches for such a signal, due to the low and well-known backgrounds, and the excellent momentum resolution and equally excellent track-finding efficiency of the detectors at such colliders. This contribution will discuss a study investigating the dependency of the limit on the mixing parameter and the mass of the $A_{D}$ using the $A_{D}\rightarrowμ^{+}μ^{-}$ decay mode in the presence of standard model background, using fully simulated signal and background events in the ILD detector at the ILC Higgs factory. In addition, a more general discussion about the capabilities expected for generic detectors at e$^+$e$^-$ colliders operating at other energies will be given.

</details>
